March 14, 2026

DecoVLN: Decoupling Observation, Reasoning, and Correction for Vision-and-Language Navigation

Abstract (English): Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) requires agents to follow long-horizon instructions and navigate complex 3D environments. However, existing approaches face two major challenges: constructing an effective long-term memory bank and overcoming the compounding errors problem. To address these issues, we propose DecoVLN, an effective framework designed for robust streaming perception and closed-loop control in long-horizon navigation. First, we formulate long-term memory construction as an optimization problem and introduce adaptive refinement mechanism that selects frames from a historical candidate pool by iteratively optimizing a unified scoring function. This function jointly balances three key criteria: semantic relevance to the instruction, visual diversity from the selected memory, and temporal coverage of the historical trajectory. Second, to alleviate compounding errors, we introduce a state-action pair-level corrective finetuning strategy. By leveraging geodesic distance between states to precisely quantify deviation from the expert trajectory, the agent collects high-quality state-action pairs in the trusted region while filtering out the polluted data with low relevance. This improves both the efficiency and stability of error correction. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of DecoVLN, and we have deployed it in real-world environments.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言导航（VLN）要求智能体遵循长程指令并在复杂的 3D 环境中导航。然而，现有方法面临两个主要挑战：构建有效的长期记忆库和克服复合误差问题。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了 DecoVLN，一种为长程导航中稳健的流式感知和闭环控制而设计的有效框架。首先，我们将长期记忆构建形式化为一个优化问题，并引入自适应精炼机制，通过迭代优化统一的评分函数，从历史候选池中选择帧。该函数联合平衡三个关键标准：与指令的语义相关性、与已选记忆的视觉多样性以及历史轨迹的时间覆盖率。其次，为了缓解复合误差，我们引入了一种状态-动作对级别的校正微调策略。通过利用状态之间的测地距离来精确量化与专家轨迹的偏差，智能体在可信区域收集高质量的状态-动作对，同时过滤掉低相关性的污染数据。这提高了误差校正的效率和稳定性。大量的实验证明了 DecoVLN 的有效性，并且我们已将其部署在真实环境中。

TLDR: DecoVLN addresses long-horizon Vision-and-Language Navigation by decoupling observation, reasoning, and correction through adaptive memory refinement and corrective finetuning, achieving improved performance and stability.

简要说明: DecoVLN通过解耦观察、推理和修正，利用自适应记忆优化和纠正性微调，解决了长程视觉-语言导航问题，实现了性能和稳定性的提升。

Authors: Zihao Xin, Wentong Li, Yixuan Jiang, Bin Wang, Runming Cong, Jie Qin, Shengjun Huang

ESPIRE: A Diagnostic Benchmark for Embodied Spatial Reasoning of Vision-Language Models

Abstract (English): A recent trend in vision-language models (VLMs) has been to enhance their spatial cognition for embodied domains. Despite progress, existing evaluations have been limited both in paradigm and in coverage, hindering rapid, iterative model development. To address these limitations, we propose ESPIRE, a diagnostic benchmark for embodied spatial reasoning. ESPIRE offers a simulated world that physically grounds VLMs and evaluates them on spatial-reasoning-centric robotic tasks, thus narrowing the gap between evaluation and real-world deployment. To adapt VLMs to robotic tasks, we decompose each task into localization and execution, and frame both as generative problems, in stark contrast to predominant discriminative evaluations (e.g., via visual-question answering) that rely on distractors and discard execution. This decomposition further enables a fine-grained analysis beyond passive spatial reasoning toward reasoning to act. We systematically design ESPIRE both at the instruction level and at the environment level, ensuring broad coverage of spatial reasoning scenarios. We use ESPIRE to diagnose a range of frontier VLMs and provide in-depth analysis of their spatial reasoning behaviors.

摘要（中文）: 视觉语言模型 (VLMs) 的一个最新趋势是增强其在具身领域中的空间认知能力。尽管取得了进展，但现有的评估在范式和覆盖范围上都存在局限性，阻碍了快速、迭代的模型开发。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了 ESPIRE，一个用于具身空间推理的诊断性基准。ESPIRE 提供了一个模拟世界，可以将 VLM 进行物理接地，并根据以空间推理为中心的机器人任务对其进行评估，从而缩小了评估与实际部署之间的差距。为了使 VLM 适应机器人任务，我们将每个任务分解为定位和执行，并将两者都构建为生成问题，这与主要依赖于干扰项并舍弃执行的判别式评估（例如，通过视觉问答）形成鲜明对比。这种分解进一步实现了超越被动空间推理到推理以采取行动的细粒度分析。我们从指令级别和环境级别系统地设计 ESPIRE，以确保对空间推理场景的广泛覆盖。我们使用 ESPIRE 诊断了一系列前沿 VLM，并深入分析了它们的空间推理行为。

TLDR: The paper introduces ESPIRE, a new diagnostic benchmark for evaluating the embodied spatial reasoning abilities of vision-language models in robotic tasks, addressing limitations of existing evaluations by focusing on generative tasks and offering a fine-grained analysis of reasoning to act.

简要说明: 本文提出了ESPIRE，一个新的诊断基准，用于评估视觉-语言模型在机器人任务中的具身空间推理能力。它通过关注生成任务和提供对推理到行动的细粒度分析，解决了现有评估的局限性。

Authors: Yanpeng Zhao, Wentao Ding, Hongtao Li, Baoxiong Jia, Zilong Zheng

RoboStream: Weaving Spatio-Temporal Reasoning with Memory in Vision-Language Models for Robotics

Abstract (English): Enabling reliable long-horizon robotic manipulation is a crucial step toward open-world embodied intelligence. However, VLM-based planners treat each step as an isolated observation-to-action mapping, forcing them to reinfer scene geometry from raw pixels at every decision point while remaining unaware of how prior actions have reshaped the environment. Despite strong short-horizon performance, these systems lack the spatio-temporal reasoning required for persistent geometric anchoring and memory of action-triggered state transitions. Without persistent state tracking, perceptual errors accumulate across the execution horizon, temporarily occluded objects are catastrophically forgotten, and these compounding failures lead to precondition violations that cascade through subsequent steps. In contrast, humans maintain a persistent mental model that continuously tracks spatial relations and action consequences across interactions rather than reconstructing them at each instant. Inspired by this human capacity for causal spatio-temporal reasoning with persistent memory, we propose RoboStream, a training-free framework that achieves geometric anchoring through Spatio-Temporal Fusion Tokens (STF-Tokens), which bind visual evidence to 3D geometric attributes for persistent object grounding, and maintains causal continuity via a Causal Spatio-Temporal Graph (CSTG) that records action-triggered state transitions across steps. This design enables the planner to trace causal chains and preserve object permanence under occlusion without additional training or fine-tuning. RoboStream achieves 90.5% on long-horizon RLBench and 44.4% on challenging real-world block-building tasks, where both SoFar and VoxPoser score 11.1%, demonstrating that spatio-temporal reasoning and causal memory are critical missing components for reliable long-horizon manipulation.

摘要（中文）: 实现可靠的长程机器人操作是迈向开放世界具身智能的关键一步。然而，基于VLM的规划器将每一步都视为一个孤立的“观察-行动”映射，迫使它们在每个决策点都从原始像素重新推断场景几何结构，同时对先前行动如何重塑环境一无所知。尽管在短程任务中表现出色，但这些系统缺乏持久的几何锚定和对由行动触发的状态转移记忆所需的时空推理能力。由于缺乏持久的状态追踪，感知错误在执行过程中累积，暂时遮挡的物体会被灾难性地遗忘，这些复合故障会导致前提条件违背，并在后续步骤中级联。相比之下，人类维护着一个持久的心理模型，该模型持续追踪跨交互的空间关系和行动后果，而不是在每个时刻都进行重建。受人类具有因果时空推理和持久记忆能力启发，我们提出了RoboStream，这是一个免训练框架，它通过时空融合令牌（STF-Tokens）实现几何锚定，该令牌将视觉证据绑定到3D几何属性，用于持久的物体接地；并通过因果时空图（CSTG）维持因果连续性，该图记录跨步骤的行动触发的状态转移。这种设计使得规划器能够追踪因果链，并在遮挡下保持物体恒常性，而无需额外的训练或微调。RoboStream在长程RLBench上实现了90.5%的成功率，在具有挑战性的真实世界积木搭建任务中实现了44.4%的成功率，而SoFar和VoxPoser的得分均为11.1%，这表明时空推理和因果记忆是可靠长程操作中关键的缺失组件。

TLDR: RoboStream is a training-free framework that enhances VLM-based robotic manipulation by incorporating spatio-temporal reasoning and causal memory via Spatio-Temporal Fusion Tokens (STF-Tokens) and a Causal Spatio-Temporal Graph (CSTG), demonstrating improved performance on long-horizon tasks.

简要说明: RoboStream是一个无需训练的框架，通过时空融合令牌(STF-Tokens)和因果时空图(CSTG)将时空推理和因果记忆融入基于VLM的机器人操作中，从而提高长程任务的性能。

Authors: Yuzhi Huang, Jie Wu, Weijue Bu, Ziyi Xiong, Gaoyang Jiang, Ye Li, Kangye Ji, Shuzhao Xie, Yue Huang, Chenglei Wu, Jingyan Jiang, Zhi Wang

Beyond Dense Futures: World Models as Structured Planners for Robotic Manipulation

Abstract (English): Recent world-model-based Vision-Language-Action (VLA) architectures have improved robotic manipulation through predictive visual foresight. However, dense future prediction introduces visual redundancy and accumulates errors, causing long-horizon plan drift. Meanwhile, recent sparse methods typically represent visual foresight using high-level semantic subtasks or implicit latent states. These representations often lack explicit kinematic grounding, weakening the alignment between planning and low-level execution. To address this, we propose StructVLA, which reformulates a generative world model into an explicit structured planner for reliable control. Instead of dense rollouts or semantic goals, StructVLA predicts sparse, physically meaningful structured frames. Derived from intrinsic kinematic cues (e.g., gripper transitions and kinematic turning points), these frames capture spatiotemporal milestones closely aligned with task progress. We implement this approach through a two-stage training paradigm with a unified discrete token vocabulary: the world model is first trained to predict structured frames and subsequently optimized to map the structured foresight into low-level actions. This approach provides clear physical guidance and bridges visual planning and motion control. In our experiments, StructVLA achieves strong average success rates of 75.0% on SimplerEnv-WidowX and 94.8% on LIBERO. Real-world deployments further demonstrate reliable task completion and robust generalization across both basic pick-and-place and complex long-horizon tasks.

摘要（中文）: 基于世界模型的视觉-语言-动作(VLA)架构通过预测性视觉前瞻技术改进了机器人操作。然而，密集的未来预测引入了视觉冗余并累积误差，导致长程规划漂移。同时，最近的稀疏方法通常使用高级语义子任务或隐式潜在状态来表示视觉前瞻。这些表示通常缺乏显式的运动学基础，削弱了规划与底层执行之间的对齐。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了StructVLA，它将生成世界模型重新 формулирует 为一个显式的结构化规划器，用于可靠的控制。StructVLA 预测稀疏、物理意义明确的结构化帧，而不是密集的展开或语义目标。这些帧源于内在运动学线索（例如，夹爪转换和运动学转折点），捕捉到与任务进度紧密对齐的时空里程碑。我们通过一个具有统一离散令牌词汇的两阶段训练范式来实现这种方法：首先训练世界模型来预测结构化帧，然后优化它将结构化前瞻映射到低层动作。这种方法提供了清晰的物理指导，并将视觉规划和运动控制连接起来。在我们的实验中，StructVLA 在 SimplerEnv-WidowX 上实现了 75.0% 的强劲平均成功率，并在 LIBERO 上实现了 94.8% 的成功率。真实世界的部署进一步证明了在基本拾取放置和复杂长程任务中可靠的任务完成和强大的泛化能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces StructVLA, a structured planner for robotic manipulation that predicts sparse, physically meaningful structured frames derived from kinematic cues, improving reliability and generalization in both simulation and real-world tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了StructVLA，一种用于机器人操作的结构化规划器，它预测从运动学线索导出的稀疏的、具有物理意义的结构化帧，从而提高了仿真和真实世界任务的可靠性和泛化能力。

Authors: Minghao Jin, Mozheng Liao, Mingfei Han, Zhihui Li, Xiaojun Chang

One-Step Flow Policy: Self-Distillation for Fast Visuomotor Policies

Abstract (English): Generative flow and diffusion models provide the continuous, multimodal action distributions needed for high-precision robotic policies. However, their reliance on iterative sampling introduces severe inference latency, degrading control frequency and harming performance in time-sensitive manipulation. To address this problem, we propose the One-Step Flow Policy (OFP), a from-scratch self-distillation framework for high-fidelity, single-step action generation without a pre-trained teacher. OFP unifies a self-consistency loss to enforce coherent transport across time intervals, and a self-guided regularization to sharpen predictions toward high-density expert modes. In addition, a warm-start mechanism leverages temporal action correlations to minimize the generative transport distance. Evaluations across 56 diverse simulated manipulation tasks demonstrate that a one-step OFP achieves state-of-the-art results, outperforming 100-step diffusion and flow policies while accelerating action generation by over $100\times$. We further integrate OFP into the $π_{0.5}$ model on RoboTwin 2.0, where one-step OFP surpasses the original 10-step policy. These results establish OFP as a practical, scalable solution for highly accurate and low-latency robot control.

摘要（中文）: 生成式流模型和扩散模型为高精度机器人策略提供了连续、多模态的动作分布。然而，它们对迭代采样的依赖引入了严重的推理延迟，降低了控制频率并损害时间敏感操作中的性能。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种单步流策略（OFP），这是一个从零开始的自蒸馏框架，用于高保真、单步动作生成，无需预训练教师模型。OFP统一了一个自洽性损失，以强制跨时间间隔的连贯传输，以及一个自引导正则化，以锐化预测，使其朝向高密度专家模式。此外，一种热启动机制利用时间动作相关性来最小化生成传输距离。在56个不同的模拟操作任务中的评估表明，单步OFP取得了最先进的结果，优于100步扩散和流策略，同时将动作生成速度提高了100倍以上。我们进一步将OFP集成到RoboTwin 2.0上的$π_{0.5}$模型中，其中单步OFP超越了原有的10步策略。这些结果确立了OFP作为一种实用的、可扩展的解决方案，用于高度准确和低延迟的机器人控制。

TLDR: The paper introduces One-Step Flow Policy (OFP), a self-distillation framework that generates high-fidelity actions in a single step, significantly reducing latency compared to iterative flow and diffusion models, resulting in state-of-the-art robotic manipulation performance with over 100x speedup.

简要说明: 该论文提出了单步流策略 (OFP)，一种自蒸馏框架，可单步生成高保真动作，与迭代流和扩散模型相比，显著降低了延迟，从而实现最先进的机器人操作性能，并实现了超过 100 倍的加速。

Authors: Shaolong Li, Lichao Sun, Yongchao Chen

VGGT-World: Transforming VGGT into an Autoregressive Geometry World Model

Abstract (English): World models that forecast scene evolution by generating future video frames devote the bulk of their capacity to photometric details, yet the resulting predictions often remain geometrically inconsistent. We present VGGT-World, a geometry world model that side-steps video generation entirely and instead forecasts the temporal evolution of frozen geometry-foundation-model (GFM) features. Concretely, we repurpose the latent tokens of a frozen VGGT as the world state and train a lightweight temporal flow transformer to autoregressively predict their future trajectory. Two technical challenges arise in this high-dimensional (d=1024) feature space: (i) standard velocity-prediction flow matching collapses, and (ii) autoregressive rollout suffers from compounding exposure bias. We address the first with a clean-target (z-prediction) parameterization that yields a substantially higher signal-to-noise ratio, and the second with a two-stage latent flow-forcing curriculum that progressively conditions the model on its own partially denoised rollouts. Experiments on KITTI, Cityscapes, and TartanAir demonstrate that VGGT-World significantly outperforms the strongest baselines in depth forecasting while running 3.6-5 times faster with only 0.43B trainable parameters, establishing frozen GFM features as an effective and efficient predictive state for 3D world modeling.

摘要（中文）: 世界模型通过生成未来视频帧来预测场景演变，将其大部分容量用于光度细节，但由此产生的预测通常在几何上仍然不一致。我们提出了 VGGT-World，一种几何世界模型，它完全绕过视频生成，而是预测冻结几何基础模型 (GFM) 特征的时间演变。具体来说，我们将冻结 VGGT 的潜在令牌重新用作世界状态，并训练一个轻量级的时间流变换器来自回归地预测它们的未来轨迹。在这个高维 (d=1024) 特征空间中出现了两个技术挑战：(i) 标准的速度预测流匹配会崩溃，以及 (ii) 自回归展开会受到复合暴露偏差的影响。我们通过使用产生明显更高信噪比的干净目标（z-预测）参数化来解决第一个问题，并通过一个两阶段潜在流强制课程来解决第二个问题，该课程逐步地根据模型自身的局部去噪展开来调节模型。在 KITTI、Cityscapes 和 TartanAir 上的实验表明，VGGT-World 在深度预测方面显著优于最强的基线，同时仅使用 0.43B 可训练参数运行速度提高 3.6-5 倍，从而确立了冻结 GFM 特征作为 3D 世界建模的有效且高效的预测状态。

TLDR: This paper introduces VGGT-World, a geometry world model that predicts the temporal evolution of frozen geometry foundation model features autoregressively, achieving state-of-the-art depth forecasting performance with significantly improved speed and efficiency compared to video-based world models.

简要说明: 本文介绍了VGGT-World，一个几何世界模型，通过自回归方式预测冻结的几何基础模型特征的时间演变，与基于视频的世界模型相比，该模型在深度预测方面实现了最先进的性能，并显著提高了速度和效率。

Authors: Xiangyu Sun, Shijie Wang, Fengyi Zhang, Lin Liu, Caiyan Jia, Ziying Song, Zi Huang, Yadan Luo

RoboStereo: Dual-Tower 4D Embodied World Models for Unified Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): Scalable Embodied AI faces fundamental constraints due to prohibitive costs and safety risks of real-world interaction. While Embodied World Models (EWMs) offer promise through imagined rollouts, existing approaches suffer from geometric hallucinations and lack unified optimization frameworks for practical policy improvement. We introduce RoboStereo, a symmetric dual-tower 4D world model that employs bidirectional cross-modal enhancement to ensure spatiotemporal geometric consistency and alleviate physics hallucinations. Building upon this high-fidelity 4D simulator, we present the first unified framework for world-model-based policy optimization: (1) Test-Time Policy Augmentation (TTPA) for pre-execution verification, (2) Imitative-Evolutionary Policy Learning (IEPL) leveraging visual perceptual rewards to learn from expert demonstrations, and (3) Open-Exploration Policy Learning (OEPL) enabling autonomous skill discovery and self-correction. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate RoboStereo achieves state-of-the-art generation quality, with our unified framework delivering >97% average relative improvement on fine-grained manipulation tasks.

摘要（中文）: 可扩展的具身智能面临着根本性的限制，因为真实世界交互的成本过高且存在安全风险。虽然具身世界模型（EWMs）通过想象展开提供希望，但现有方法存在几何幻觉，并且缺乏统一的优化框架来实现实用的策略改进。我们引入 RoboStereo，一种对称双塔式 4D 世界模型，它采用双向跨模态增强来确保时空几何一致性并减轻物理幻觉。在此高保真 4D 模拟器的基础上，我们提出了第一个基于世界模型的策略优化统一框架：（1）测试时策略增强（TTPA）用于预执行验证，（2）模仿-进化策略学习（IEPL），利用视觉感知奖励从专家演示中学习，以及（3）开放探索策略学习（OEPL），实现自主技能发现和自我纠正。全面的实验表明，RoboStereo 实现了最先进的生成质量，而我们的统一框架在精细操作任务上实现了 >97% 的平均相对改进。

TLDR: The paper introduces RoboStereo, a dual-tower 4D world model with a unified policy optimization framework (TTPA, IEPL, OEPL) for embodied AI, demonstrating significant improvements in manipulation tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了RoboStereo，一个双塔式4D世界模型，具有统一的策略优化框架（TTPA、IEPL、OEPL），用于具身人工智能，并在操作任务中展示了显著的改进。

Authors: Ruicheng Zhang, Guangyu Chen, Zunnan Xu, Zihao Liu, Zhizhou Zhong, Mingyang Zhang, Jun Zhou, Xiu Li

PhysMoDPO: Physically-Plausible Humanoid Motion with Preference Optimization

Abstract (English): Recent progress in text-conditioned human motion generation has been largely driven by diffusion models trained on large-scale human motion data. Building on this progress, recent methods attempt to transfer such models for character animation and real robot control by applying a Whole-Body Controller (WBC) that converts diffusion-generated motions into executable trajectories. While WBC trajectories become compliant with physics, they may expose substantial deviations from original motion. To address this issue, we here propose PhysMoDPO, a Direct Preference Optimization framework. Unlike prior work that relies on hand-crafted physics-aware heuristics such as foot-sliding penalties, we integrate WBC into our training pipeline and optimize diffusion model such that the output of WBC becomes compliant both with physics and original text instructions. To train PhysMoDPO we deploy physics-based and task-specific rewards and use them to assign preference to synthesized trajectories. Our extensive experiments on text-to-motion and spatial control tasks demonstrate consistent improvements of PhysMoDPO in both physical realism and task-related metrics on simulated robots. Moreover, we demonstrate that PhysMoDPO results in significant improvements when applied to zero-shot motion transfer in simulation and for real-world deployment on a G1 humanoid robot.

摘要（中文）: 基于文本的人体运动生成领域的最新进展主要得益于在大型人体运动数据上训练的扩散模型。在此基础上，最近的方法尝试通过应用全身控制器 (WBC) 来转换这些模型，用于角色动画和真实机器人控制，WBC 将扩散模型生成的运动转换为可执行的轨迹。虽然 WBC 轨迹能够满足物理约束，但它们可能与原始运动产生显著偏差。为了解决这个问题，我们在这里提出了 PhysMoDPO，一种直接偏好优化框架。与先前依赖于手工设计的、具有物理意识的启发式方法（如足部滑动惩罚）的工作不同，我们将 WBC 集成到我们的训练管道中，并优化扩散模型，使得 WBC 的输出既符合物理约束，又符合原始文本指令。为了训练 PhysMoDPO，我们部署了基于物理和特定任务的奖励，并使用它们为合成轨迹分配偏好。我们在文本到运动和空间控制任务上的大量实验表明，PhysMoDPO 在模拟机器人的物理真实性和任务相关指标上都表现出持续的改进。此外，我们证明了 PhysMoDPO 在应用于模拟中的零样本运动迁移和 G1 人形机器人的真实部署时，能够带来显著的改进。

TLDR: The paper introduces PhysMoDPO, a Direct Preference Optimization framework that trains diffusion models to generate physically-plausible human motion by integrating a Whole-Body Controller (WBC) into the training loop and optimizing for physics compliance and text alignment. It shows improvements in simulation and real-world robot deployment.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了PhysMoDPO，一个直接偏好优化框架，通过将全身控制器(WBC)集成到训练循环中，并针对物理兼容性和文本对齐进行优化，来训练扩散模型以生成物理上合理的人体运动。它展示了在模拟和真实机器人部署中的改进。

Authors: Yangsong Zhang, Anujith Muraleedharan, Rikhat Akizhanov, Abdul Ahad Butt, Gül Varol, Pascal Fua, Fabio Pizzati, Ivan Laptev

Evaluating VLMs' Spatial Reasoning Over Robot Motion: A Step Towards Robot Planning with Motion Preferences

Abstract (English): Understanding user instructions and object spatial relations in surrounding environments is crucial for intelligent robot systems to assist humans in various tasks. The natural language and spatial reasoning capabilities of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have the potential to enhance the generalization of robot planners on new tasks, objects, and motion specifications. While foundation models have been applied to task planning, it is still unclear the degree to which they have the capability of spatial reasoning required to enforce user preferences or constraints on motion, such as desired distances from objects, topological properties, or motion style preferences. In this paper, we evaluate the capability of four state-of-the-art VLMs at spatial reasoning over robot motion, using four different querying methods. Our results show that, with the highest-performing querying method, Qwen2.5-VL achieves 71.4% accuracy zero-shot and 75% on a smaller model after fine-tuning, and GPT-4o leads to lower performance. We evaluate two types of motion preferences (object-proximity and path-style), and we also analyze the trade-off between accuracy and computation cost in number of tokens. This work shows some promise in the potential of VLM integration with robot motion planning pipelines.

摘要（中文）: 理解用户指令以及周围环境中物体的空间关系对于智能机器人系统在各种任务中辅助人类至关重要。视觉-语言模型(VLMs)的自然语言和空间推理能力有可能增强机器人规划器在新任务、物体和运动规范上的泛化能力。尽管基础模型已被应用于任务规划，但它们在多大程度上具备 enforced 用户对运动的偏好或约束 (例如，与物体的期望距离、拓扑属性或运动风格偏好) 所需的空间推理能力仍不清楚。在本文中，我们使用四种不同的查询方法，评估了四种最先进的 VLMs 在机器人运动上的空间推理能力。我们的结果表明，在使用表现最佳的查询方法时，Qwen2.5-VL 实现了 71.4% 的零样本准确率，并在微调后在较小模型上实现了 75% 的准确率，而 GPT-4o 的性能较低。我们评估了两种类型的运动偏好（物体邻近度和路径风格），并且还分析了准确率和计算成本（以 token 数量衡量）之间的权衡。这项工作展示了 VLM 与机器人运动规划流程集成的潜在前景。

TLDR: This paper evaluates the spatial reasoning capabilities of VLMs for robot motion planning, focusing on user preferences and motion constraints, and finds Qwen2.5-VL promising.

Authors: Wenxi Wu, Jingjing Zhang, Martim Brandão

Language-Grounded Decoupled Action Representation for Robotic Manipulation

Abstract (English): The heterogeneity between high-level vision-language understanding and low-level action control remains a fundamental challenge in robotic manipulation. Although recent methods have advanced task-specific action alignment, they often struggle to generate robust and accurate actions for novel or semantically related tasks. To address this, we propose the Language-Grounded Decoupled Action Representation (LaDA) framework, which leverages natural language as a semantic bridge to connect perception and control. LaDA introduces a fine-grained intermediate layer of three interpretable action primitives--translation, rotation, and gripper control--providing explicit semantic structure for low-level actions. It further employs a semantic-guided soft-label contrastive learning objective to align similar action primitives across tasks, enhancing generalization and motion consistency. An adaptive weighting strategy, inspired by curriculum learning, dynamically balances contrastive and imitation objectives for stable and effective training. Extensive experiments on simulated benchmarks (LIBERO and MimicGen) and real-world demonstrations validate that LaDA achieves strong performance and generalizes effectively to unseen or related tasks.

摘要（中文）: 高层视觉-语言理解与底层动作控制之间的异质性仍然是机器人操作中的一个根本挑战。尽管最近的方法在特定任务的动作对齐方面取得了进展，但它们通常难以为新颖或语义相关的任务生成稳健且准确的动作。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了语言引导的解耦动作表示（LaDA）框架，该框架利用自然语言作为语义桥梁来连接感知和控制。LaDA引入了一个细粒度的中间层，包含三个可解释的动作原语——平移、旋转和夹爪控制——为底层动作提供显式的语义结构。它进一步采用语义引导的软标签对比学习目标来对齐跨任务的相似动作原语，从而增强泛化能力和运动一致性。一种受课程学习启发的自适应加权策略，动态平衡对比学习和模仿学习目标，以实现稳定有效的训练。在模拟基准测试（LIBERO和MimicGen）和真实世界演示上的大量实验验证了LaDA实现了强大的性能，并能有效地泛化到未见或相关任务。

TLDR: The paper introduces LaDA, a language-grounded framework for robotic manipulation that uses interpretable action primitives and contrastive learning to improve generalization to novel tasks.

Authors: Wuding Weng, Tongshu Wu, Liucheng Chen, Siyu Xie, Zheng Wang, Xing Xu, Jingkuan Song, Heng Tao Shen

ReMem-VLA: Empowering Vision-Language-Action Model with Memory via Dual-Level Recurrent Queries

Abstract (English): Vision-language-action (VLA) models for closed-loop robot control are typically cast under the Markov assumption, making them prone to errors on tasks requiring historical context. To incorporate memory, existing VLAs either retrieve from a memory bank, which can be misled by distractors, or extend the frame window, whose fixed horizon still limits long-term retention. In this paper, we introduce ReMem-VLA, a Recurrent Memory VLA model equipped with two sets of learnable queries: frame-level recurrent memory queries for propagating information across consecutive frames to support short-term memory, and chunk-level recurrent memory queries for carrying context across temporal chunks for long-term memory. These queries are trained end-to-end to aggregate and maintain relevant context over time, implicitly guiding the model's decisions without additional training or inference cost. Furthermore, to enhance visual memory, we introduce Past Observation Prediction as an auxiliary training objective. Through extensive memory-centric simulation and real-world robot experiments, we demonstrate that ReMem-VLA exhibits strong memory capabilities across multiple dimensions, including spatial, sequential, episodic, temporal, and visual memory. ReMem-VLA significantly outperforms memory-free VLA baselines $π$0.5 and OpenVLA-OFT and surpasses MemoryVLA on memory-dependent tasks by a large margin.

摘要（中文）: 闭环机器人控制的视觉-语言-行动(VLA)模型通常基于马尔可夫假设，这使得它们在需要历史信息的任务中容易出错。 为了整合记忆，现有的VLA模型要么从记忆库中检索，这可能被干扰因素误导，要么扩展帧窗口，但其固定的时间范围仍然限制了长期记忆。 在本文中，我们提出了ReMem-VLA，一种循环记忆VLA模型，配备了两组可学习的查询：帧级循环记忆查询，用于在连续帧之间传播信息，以支持短期记忆；以及块级循环记忆查询，用于在时间块之间传递上下文，以实现长期记忆。 这些查询经过端到端训练，可以聚合和维护随时间推移的相关上下文，从而在不增加额外训练或推理成本的情况下，隐式地指导模型的决策。 此外，为了增强视觉记忆，我们引入了“过去观察预测”作为辅助训练目标。 通过大量的以记忆为中心的模拟和真实世界的机器人实验，我们证明了ReMem-VLA在多个维度上表现出强大的记忆能力，包括空间、序列、情景、时间和视觉记忆。 ReMem-VLA 显著优于无记忆的VLA基线$π$0.5和OpenVLA-OFT，并且在依赖记忆的任务上大大超过了MemoryVLA。

TLDR: The paper introduces ReMem-VLA, a novel Vision-Language-Action model that incorporates dual-level recurrent memory queries for improved short-term and long-term memory, leading to better performance in memory-dependent robotic tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 ReMem-VLA，一种新型的视觉-语言-动作模型，它结合了双层递归记忆查询，以改善短期和长期记忆，从而在依赖记忆的机器人任务中取得更好的性能。

Authors: Hang Li, Fengyi Shen, Dong Chen, Liudi Yang, Xudong Wang, Jinkui Shi, Zhenshan Bing, Ziyuan Liu, Alois Knoll

MotionAnymesh: Physics-Grounded Articulation for Simulation-Ready Digital Twins

Abstract (English): Converting static 3D meshes into interactable articulated assets is crucial for embodied AI and robotic simulation. However, existing zero-shot pipelines struggle with complex assets due to a critical lack of physical grounding. Specifically, ungrounded Vision-Language Models (VLMs) frequently suffer from kinematic hallucinations, while unconstrained joint estimation inevitably leads to catastrophic mesh inter-penetration during physical simulation. To bridge this gap, we propose MotionAnymesh, an automated zero-shot framework that seamlessly transforms unstructured static meshes into simulation-ready digital twins. Our method features a kinematic-aware part segmentation module that grounds VLM reasoning with explicit SP4D physical priors, effectively eradicating kinematic hallucinations. Furthermore, we introduce a geometry-physics joint estimation pipeline that combines robust type-aware initialization with physics-constrained trajectory optimization to rigorously guarantee collision-free articulation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that MotionAnymesh significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in both geometric precision and dynamic physical executability, providing highly reliable assets for downstream applications.

摘要（中文）: 将静态3D网格转换为可交互的铰接资产对于具身人工智能和机器人仿真至关重要。然而，由于缺乏关键的物理基础，现有的零样本流程在处理复杂资产时会遇到困难。具体而言，无物理基础的视觉-语言模型（VLMs）经常遭受运动学幻觉的影响，而无约束的关节估计不可避免地导致物理仿真过程中灾难性的网格相互穿透。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出MotionAnymesh，一种自动化的零样本框架，可以无缝地将非结构化静态网格转换为可用于仿真的数字孪生。我们的方法采用了一种运动学感知的部件分割模块，通过显式的SP4D物理先验来支持VLM推理，有效地消除运动学幻觉。此外，我们引入了一种几何-物理联合估计流程，该流程结合了稳健的类型感知初始化与物理约束的轨迹优化，以严格保证无碰撞的铰接运动。大量的实验表明，在几何精度和动态物理可执行性方面，MotionAnymesh显著优于最先进的基准方法，为下游应用提供高度可靠的资产。

TLDR: MotionAnymesh is a zero-shot framework that converts static 3D meshes into physics-grounded, simulation-ready articulated assets by addressing kinematic hallucinations and mesh inter-penetration issues in existing methods.

简要说明: MotionAnymesh是一个零样本框架，通过解决现有方法中存在的运动学幻觉和网格穿透问题，将静态3D网格转换为具有物理基础、可用于模拟的铰接资产。

Authors: WenBo Xu, Liu Liu, Li Zhang, Dan Guo, RuoNan Liu

GoalSwarm: Multi-UAV Semantic Coordination for Open-Vocabulary Object Navigation

Abstract (English): Cooperative visual semantic navigation is a foundational capability for aerial robot teams operating in unknown environments. However, achieving robust open-vocabulary object-goal navigation remains challenging due to the computational constraints of deploying heavy perception models onboard and the complexity of decentralized multi-agent coordination. We present GoalSwarm, a fully decentralized multi-UAV framework for zero-shot semantic object-goal navigation. Each UAV collaboratively constructs a shared, lightweight 2D top-down semantic occupancy map by projecting depth observations from aerial vantage points, eliminating the computational burden of full 3D representations while preserving essential geometric and semantic structure. The core contributions of GoalSwarm are threefold: (1) integration of zero-shot foundation model -- SAM3 for open vocabulary detection and pixel-level segmentation, enabling open-vocabulary target identification without task-specific training; (2) a Bayesian Value Map that fuses multi-viewpoint detection confidences into a per-pixel goal-relevance distribution, enabling informed frontier scoring via Upper Confidence Bound (UCB) exploration; and (3) a decentralized coordination strategy combining semantic frontier extraction, cost-utility bidding with geodesic path costs, and spatial separation penalties to minimize redundant exploration across the swarm.

摘要（中文）: 合作视觉语义导航是无人机团队在未知环境中作业的一项基础能力。然而，由于在机载部署重型感知模型的算力限制以及去中心化多智能体协调的复杂性，实现鲁棒的开放词汇目标物导航仍然具有挑战性。我们提出GoalSwarm，一个用于零样本语义目标物导航的完全去中心化多无人机框架。每个无人机通过投影来自空中有利位置的深度观测，协作构建一个共享的、轻量级的2D俯视语义占据栅格地图，消除了完整3D表示的计算负担，同时保留了必要的几何和语义结构。GoalSwarm的核心贡献有三方面：（1）集成零样本基础模型——SAM3，用于开放词汇检测和像素级分割，无需特定任务训练即可实现开放词汇目标识别；（2）一个贝叶斯价值地图，将多视点检测置信度融合到每个像素的目标相关性分布中，通过置信上限（UCB）探索实现知情的边界评分；以及（3）一种去中心化协调策略，结合语义边界提取、带测地线路径成本的成本-效用竞标，以及空间分离惩罚，以最大限度地减少蜂群中的冗余探索。

TLDR: This paper presents GoalSwarm, a decentralized multi-UAV framework for open-vocabulary object-goal navigation, leveraging zero-shot foundation models and a Bayesian Value Map for efficient semantic exploration.

简要说明: 这篇论文提出了GoalSwarm，一个用于开放词汇目标导航的去中心化多无人机框架，它利用了零样本基础模型和贝叶斯价值地图来实现高效的语义探索。

Authors: MoniJesu Wonders James, Amir Atef Habel, Aleksey Fedoseev, Dzmitry Tsetserokou

Beyond Imitation: Reinforcement Learning Fine-Tuning for Adaptive Diffusion Navigation Policies

Abstract (English): Diffusion-based robot navigation policies trained on large-scale imitation learning datasets, can generate multi-modal trajectories directly from the robot's visual observations, bypassing the traditional localization-mapping-planning pipeline and achieving strong zero-shot generalization. However, their performance remains constrained by the coverage of offline datasets, and when deployed in unseen settings, distribution shift often leads to accumulated trajectory errors and safety-critical failures. Adapting diffusion policies with reinforcement learning is challenging because their iterative denoising structure hinders effective gradient backpropagation, while also making the training of an additional value network computationally expensive and less stable. To address these issues, we propose a reinforcement learning fine-tuning framework tailored for diffusion-based navigation. The method leverages the inherent multi-trajectory sampling mechanism of diffusion models and adopts Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), which estimates relative advantages across sampled trajectories without requiring a separate value network. To preserve pretrained representations while enabling adaptation, we freeze the visual encoder and selectively update the higher decoder layers and action head, enhancing safety-aware behaviors through online environmental feedback. On the PointGoal task in Isaac Sim, our approach improves the Success Rate from 52.0% to 58.7% and SPL from 0.49 to 0.54 on unseen scenes, while reducing collision frequency. Additional experiments show that the fine-tuned policy transfers zero-shot to a real quadruped platform and maintains stable performance in geometrically out-of-distribution environments, suggesting improved adaptability and safe generalization to new domains.

摘要（中文）: 基于扩散模型的机器人导航策略可以通过在大型模仿学习数据集上训练，直接从机器人的视觉观测生成多模态轨迹，绕过传统的定位-建图-规划流程，并实现强大的零样本泛化能力。然而，它们的性能仍然受到离线数据集覆盖范围的限制，并且当部署在未见过的环境中时，分布偏移常常导致累积的轨迹误差和安全攸关的失败。使用强化学习来调整扩散策略具有挑战性，因为它们迭代的去噪结构阻碍了有效的梯度反向传播，同时也使得额外的价值网络的训练在计算上开销大且不稳定。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一种专为基于扩散的导航定制的强化学习微调框架。该方法利用了扩散模型固有的多轨迹采样机制，并采用组相对策略优化（GRPO），该方法估计采样轨迹间的相对优势，而无需单独的价值网络。为了在启用自适应的同时保留预训练的表征，我们冻结了视觉编码器，并选择性地更新较高层的解码器层和动作头，通过在线环境反馈来增强安全意识行为。在Isaac Sim中的PointGoal任务中，我们的方法将未见场景中的成功率从52.0%提高到58.7%，SPL从0.49提高到0.54，同时降低了碰撞频率。额外的实验表明，微调后的策略零样本迁移到一个真实的四足平台上，并在几何上超出分布的环境中保持稳定的性能，表明改进了适应性和对新领域的安全泛化能力。

TLDR: This paper proposes a reinforcement learning fine-tuning framework for diffusion-based robot navigation policies, leveraging Group Relative Policy Optimization and selective parameter updates to improve performance and safety in unseen environments.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于扩散的机器人导航策略的强化学习微调框架，利用群体相对策略优化和选择性参数更新，以提高在未见环境中的性能和安全性。

Authors: Junhe Sheng, Ruofei Bai, Kuan Xu, Ruimeng Liu, Jie Chen, Shenghai Yuan, Wei-Yun Yau, Lihua Xie

SmoothTurn: Learning to Turn Smoothly for Agile Navigation with Quadrupedal Robots

Abstract (English): Quadrupedal robots show great potential for valuable real-world applications such as fire rescue and industrial inspection. Such applications often require urgency and the ability to navigate agilely, which in turn demands the capability to change directions smoothly while running in high speed. Existing approaches for agile navigation typically learn a single-goal reaching policy by encouraging the robot to stay at the target position after reaching there. As a result, when the policy is used to reach sequential goals that require changing directions, it cannot anticipate upcoming maneuvers or maintain momentum across the switch of goals, thereby preventing the robot from fully exploiting its agility potential. In this work, we formulate the task as sequential local navigation, extending the single-goal-conditioned local navigation formulation in prior work. We then introduce SmoothTurn, a learning-based control framework that learns to turn smoothly while running rapidly for agile sequential local navigation. The framework adopts a novel sequential goal-reaching reward, an expanded observation space with a lookahead window for future goals, and an automatic goal curriculum that progressively expands the difficulty of sampled goal sequences based on the goal-reaching performance. The trained policy can be directly deployed on real quadrupedal robots with onboard sensors and computation. Both simulation and real-world empirical results show that SmoothTurn learns an agile locomotion policy that performs smooth turning across goals, with emergent behaviors such as controlling momentum when switching goals, facing towards the future goal in advance, and planning efficient paths. We have provided video demos of the learned motions in the supplementary materials. The source code and trained policies will be made available upon acceptance.

摘要（中文）: 四足机器人在诸如火灾救援和工业检测等具有重要价值的现实应用中展现出巨大潜力。这些应用通常需要紧迫性和敏捷导航能力，这反过来要求机器人能够在高速奔跑的同时平稳地改变方向。现有的敏捷导航方法通常学习一种单目标到达策略，鼓励机器人在到达目标位置后保持在该处。因此，当该策略被用于到达需要改变方向的连续目标时，它无法预测即将到来的动作或在目标切换时保持动量，从而阻止机器人充分发挥其敏捷潜力。在这项工作中，我们将该任务形式化为连续局部导航，扩展了先前工作中单目标条件局部导航的公式。然后，我们引入SmoothTurn，这是一个基于学习的控制框架，它学习在高速奔跑时平稳转弯，以实现敏捷的连续局部导航。该框架采用了一种新颖的连续目标到达奖励、一个扩展的观测空间（具有用于未来目标的前瞻窗口）和一个自动目标课程，该课程基于目标到达性能逐步扩展采样目标序列的难度。训练后的策略可以直接部署在配备车载传感器和计算能力的真实四足机器人上。仿真和真实世界的实验结果均表明，SmoothTurn学习了一种敏捷的运动策略，该策略可在目标之间执行平稳转弯，并具有诸如在切换目标时控制动量、提前面向未来目标以及规划高效路径等涌现行为。我们在补充材料中提供了已学习运动的视频演示。源代码和训练后的策略将在接收后提供。

TLDR: The paper presents SmoothTurn, a learning-based control framework for quadrupedal robots that enables smooth turning and agile sequential navigation by using a novel sequential goal-reaching reward, expanded observation space with a lookahead window for future goals, and an automatic goal curriculum. The learned policy demonstrates smooth turning and efficient path planning in both simulation and real-world experiments.

简要说明: 该论文提出了SmoothTurn，一个基于学习的四足机器人控制框架，通过使用新的顺序目标到达奖励、带有未来目标前瞻窗口的扩展观察空间以及自动目标课程，实现平稳转向和敏捷的顺序导航。 学习到的策略在模拟和真实实验中都表现出平稳的转向和高效的路径规划。

Authors: Zunzhi You, Haolan Guo, Yunke Wang, Chang Xu

FLUX: Accelerating Cross-Embodiment Generative Navigation Policies via Rectified Flow and Static-to-Dynamic Learning

Abstract (English): Autonomous navigation requires a broad spectrum of skills, from static goal-reaching to dynamic social traversal, yet evaluation remains fragmented across disparate protocols. We introduce DynBench, a dynamic navigation benchmark featuring physically valid crowd simulation. Combined with existing static protocols, it supports comprehensive evaluation across six fundamental navigation tasks. Within this framework, we propose FLUX, the first flow-based unified navigation policy. By linearizing probability flow, FLUX replaces iterative denoising with straight-line trajectories, improving per-step inference efficiency by 47% over prior flow-based methods and 29% over diffusion-based ones. Following a static-to-dynamic curriculum, FLUX initially establishes geometric priors and is subsequently refined through reinforcement learning in dynamic social environments. This regime not only strengthens socially-aware navigation but also enhances static task robustness by capturing recovery behaviors through stochastic action distributions. FLUX achieves state-of-the-art performance across all tasks and demonstrates zero-shot sim-to-real transfer on wheeled, quadrupedal, and humanoid platforms without any fine-tuning.

摘要（中文）: 自主导航需要广泛的技能，从静态的目标到达，到动态的社交穿梭，然而，评估仍然分散在不同的协议中。我们引入了DynBench，一个具有物理有效人群模拟的动态导航基准。结合现有的静态协议，它支持对六项基本导航任务的全面评估。在此框架内，我们提出了FLUX，第一个基于流的统一导航策略。通过线性化概率流，FLUX用直线轨迹替换了迭代去噪，在每步推理效率上比之前的基于流的方法提高了47%，比基于扩散的方法提高了29%。遵循从静态到动态的课程，FLUX首先建立几何先验，随后在动态社交环境中通过强化学习进行改进。这种机制不仅加强了具有社交意识的导航，还通过捕获随机动作分布的恢复行为来增强静态任务的鲁棒性。FLUX在所有任务中都实现了最先进的性能，并且在轮式、四足和人形平台上展示了无需任何微调的零射模拟到真实世界的迁移。

TLDR: This paper introduces FLUX, a flow-based navigation policy trained with a static-to-dynamic curriculum, achieving state-of-the-art results in a new dynamic navigation benchmark and demonstrating zero-shot sim-to-real transfer across multiple robot platforms.

简要说明: 本文介绍了FLUX，一种基于流的导航策略，通过静态到动态的课程学习进行训练，在新提出的动态导航benchmark上取得了state-of-the-art的结果，并展示了在多种机器人平台上零样本的sim-to-real迁移能力。

Authors: Zeying Gong, Yangyi Zhong, Yiyi Ding, Tianshuai Hu, Guoyang Zhao, Lingdong Kong, Rong Li, Jiadi You, Junwei Liang

PVI: Plug-in Visual Injection for Vision-Language-Action Models

Abstract (English): VLA architectures that pair a pretrained VLM with a flow-matching action expert have emerged as a strong paradigm for language-conditioned manipulation. Yet the VLM, optimized for semantic abstraction and typically conditioned on static visual observations, tends to attenuate fine-grained geometric cues and often lacks explicit temporal evidence for the action expert. Prior work mitigates this by injecting auxiliary visual features, but existing approaches either focus on static spatial representations or require substantial architectural modifications to accommodate temporal inputs, leaving temporal information underexplored. We propose Plug-in Visual Injection (PVI), a lightweight, encoder-agnostic module that attaches to a pretrained action expert and injects auxiliary visual representations via zero-initialized residual pathways, preserving pretrained behavior with only single-stage fine-tuning. Using PVI, we obtain consistent gains over the base policy and a range of competitive alternative injection strategies, and our controlled study shows that temporal video features (V-JEPA2) outperform strong static image features (DINOv2), with the largest gains on multi-phase tasks requiring state tracking and coordination. Real-robot experiments on long-horizon bimanual cloth folding further demonstrate the practicality of PVI beyond simulation.

摘要（中文）: 将预训练视觉语言模型 (VLM) 与流匹配动作专家相结合的 VLA 架构，已成为一种强大的语言条件操作范式。然而，VLM 针对语义抽象进行了优化，且通常以静态视觉观察为条件，因此往往会减弱细粒度的几何线索，并且通常缺乏动作专家的显式时间证据。先前的工作通过注入辅助视觉特征来缓解这个问题，但现有方法要么侧重于静态空间表示，要么需要对架构进行大量修改才能适应时间输入，从而导致对时间信息的探索不足。我们提出了一种轻量级的、与编码器无关的模块：插件式视觉注入 (PVI)，它可以连接到预训练的动作专家，并通过零初始化的残差路径注入辅助视觉表示，仅通过单阶段微调即可保留预训练的行为。使用 PVI，我们相比于基准策略和一系列有竞争力的替代注入策略，获得了持续的增益，并且我们的对照研究表明，时间视频特征 (V-JEPA2) 优于强大的静态图像特征 (DINOv2)，特别是在需要状态跟踪和协调的多阶段任务中增益最大。在长程双臂布料折叠上的真实机器人实验进一步证明了 PVI 在模拟之外的实用性。

TLDR: This paper introduces Plug-in Visual Injection (PVI), a lightweight module for enhancing Vision-Language-Action models by injecting auxiliary visual representations into the action expert, particularly focusing on incorporating temporal information for improved performance on manipulation tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Plug-in Visual Injection（PVI），一种轻量级模块，通过将辅助视觉表征注入到动作专家中来增强视觉-语言-动作模型，特别关注于结合时间信息以提高操作任务的性能。

Authors: Zezhou Zhang, Songxin Zhang, Xiao Xiong, Junjie Zhang, Zejian Xie, Jingyi Xi, Zunyao Mao, Zan Mao, Zhixin Mai, Zhuoyang Song, Jiaxing Zhang

Show, Don't Tell: Detecting Novel Objects by Watching Human Videos

Abstract (English): How can a robot quickly identify and recognize new objects shown to it during a human demonstration? Existing closed-set object detectors frequently fail at this because the objects are out-of-distribution. While open-set detectors (e.g., VLMs) sometimes succeed, they often require expensive and tedious human-in-the-loop prompt engineering to uniquely recognize novel object instances. In this paper, we present a self-supervised system that eliminates the need for tedious language descriptions and expensive prompt engineering by training a bespoke object detector on an automatically created dataset, supervised by the human demonstration itself. In our approach, "Show, Don't Tell," we show the detector the specific objects of interest during the demonstration, rather than telling the detector about these objects via complex language descriptions. By bypassing language altogether, this paradigm enables us to quickly train bespoke detectors tailored to the relevant objects observed in human task demonstrations. We develop an integrated on-robot system to deploy our "Show, Don't Tell" paradigm of automatic dataset creation and novel object-detection on a real-world robot. Empirical results demonstrate that our pipeline significantly outperforms state-of-the-art detection and recognition methods for manipulated objects, leading to improved task completion for the robot.

摘要（中文）: 如何让机器人能够快速识别和辨认人类示教过程中展示的新物体？ 现有的封闭集物体检测器通常无法胜任这项任务，因为这些物体属于分布外(out-of-distribution)对象。 虽然开放集检测器（例如，VLMs）有时可以成功，但它们通常需要昂贵且繁琐的人工在环(human-in-the-loop)提示工程，才能唯一地识别新的物体实例。在本文中，我们提出了一种自监督系统，该系统通过在自动创建的数据集上训练定制的物体检测器来消除对繁琐的语言描述和昂贵的提示工程的需求，该数据集由人类示教本身监督。 在我们的“展示，而非告知（Show, Don't Tell）”方法中，我们在示教过程中向检测器展示感兴趣的特定对象，而不是通过复杂的语言描述来告知检测器这些对象。 通过完全绕过语言，这种范式使我们能够快速训练定制的检测器，使其专门针对人类任务示教中观察到的相关对象。 我们开发了一个集成的机器人系统，以在真实的机器人上部署我们的“展示，而非告知”范式，用于自动数据集创建和新物体检测。 实验结果表明，我们的流程明显优于用于操作对象的现有检测和识别方法，从而提高了机器人的任务完成率。

TLDR: The paper introduces a self-supervised system called "Show, Don't Tell" that trains a bespoke object detector on human demonstrations, bypassing the need for language descriptions or prompt engineering to detect novel objects, and demonstrating improved task completion on a real robot.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为“展示，而非讲述”的自监督系统，该系统通过人类演示训练定制的对象检测器，无需语言描述或提示工程即可检测新对象，并在真实机器人上展示了改进的任务完成度。

Authors: James Akl, Jose Nicolas Avendano Arbelaez, James Barabas, Jennifer L. AnchorVLA4D: an Anchor-Based Spatial-Temporal Vision-Language-Action Model for Robotic Manipulation

Abstract (English): Since current Vision-Language-Action (VLA) systems suffer from limited spatial perception and the absence of memory throughout manipulation, we investigate visual anchors as a means to enhance spatial and temporal reasoning within VLA policies for robotic manipulation. Conventional VLAs generate actions by conditioning on a single current frame together with a language instruction. However, since the frame is encoded as a 2D image, it does not contain detailed spatial information, and the VLA similarly lacks any means to incorporate past context. As a result, it frequently forgets objects under occlusion and becomes spatially disoriented during the manipulation process. Thus, we propose AnchorVLA4D, a simple spatial-temporal VLA that augments the visual input with an anchor image to preserve the initial scene context throughout execution, and adds a lightweight spatial encoder that jointly processes the anchor and current frames to expose geometric relationships within an episode. Built on a Qwen2.5-VL backbone with a diffusion-based action head, AnchorVLA4D requires no additional sensing modalities (e.g., depth or point clouds) and introduces negligible inference overhead. Combining anchoring with a frozen pretrained spatial encoder yields further gains, realizing a 13.6% improvement on the Simpler WidowX benchmark and confirming the approach on real-world tasks, where it achieved an average success rate of 80%.

摘要（中文）: 当前视觉-语言-动作（VLA）系统在操作过程中受到空间感知能力有限和缺乏记忆的制约，因此我们研究了视觉锚点，旨在增强机器人操作VLA策略中的空间和时间推理能力。传统的VLA通过对单个当前帧和语言指令进行条件约束来生成动作。然而，由于帧被编码为2D图像，它不包含详细的空间信息，并且VLA同样缺乏整合过去上下文的手段。因此，它经常忘记被遮挡的物体，并在操作过程中在空间上迷失方向。为此，我们提出了AnchorVLA4D，一个简单的时空VLA，它通过使用锚点图像来增强视觉输入，从而在整个执行过程中保留初始场景上下文，并添加了一个轻量级的空间编码器，共同处理锚点帧和当前帧，以揭示一个episode内的几何关系。AnchorVLA4D基于Qwen2.5-VL主干网络和一个基于扩散的动作头，不需要额外的传感模态（例如，深度或点云），并且引入的推理开销可以忽略不计。将锚定与冻结的预训练空间编码器相结合可以获得进一步的提升，在Simpler WidowX基准测试中实现了13.6%的改进，并在真实世界任务中验证了该方法，达到了80%的平均成功率。

TLDR: AnchorVLA4D enhances spatial-temporal reasoning in vision-language-action models for robotic manipulation by using an anchor image to maintain initial scene context and a spatial encoder to process geometric relationships, improving performance on manipulation tasks without additional sensing.

简要说明: AnchorVLA4D通过使用锚点图像来保持初始场景上下文，并使用空间编码器来处理几何关系，从而增强了机器人操作的视觉-语言-动作模型中的时空推理能力，无需额外传感即可提高操作任务的性能。

Authors: Juan Zhu, Zhanying Shao, Xiaoqi Li, Ethan Morgan, Jiadong Xu, Hongwei Fan, Hao Dong

Altered Thoughts, Altered Actions: Probing Chain-of-Thought Vulnerabilities in VLA Robotic Manipulation

Abstract (English): Recent Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models increasingly adopt chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning, generating a natural-language plan before decoding motor commands. This internal text channel between the reasoning module and the action decoder has received no adversarial scrutiny. We ask: which properties of this intermediate plan does the action decoder actually rely on, and can targeted corruption of the reasoning trace alone -- with all inputs left intact -- degrade a robot's physical task performance? We design a taxonomy of seven text corruptions organized into three attacker tiers (blind noise, mechanical-semantic, and LLM-adaptive) and apply them to a state-of-the-art reasoning VLA across 40 LIBERO tabletop manipulation tasks. Our results reveal a striking asymmetry: substituting object names in the reasoning trace reduces overall success rate by 8.3~percentage points (pp) -- reaching $-$19.3~pp on goal-conditioned tasks and $-$45~pp on individual tasks -- whereas sentence reordering, spatial-direction reversal, token noise, and even a 70B-parameter LLM crafting plausible-but-wrong plans all have negligible impact (within $\pm$4~pp). This asymmetry indicates that the action decoder depends on entity-reference integrity rather than reasoning quality or sequential structure. Notably, a sophisticated LLM-based attacker underperforms simple mechanical object-name substitution, because preserving plausibility inadvertently retains the entity-grounding structure the decoder needs. A cross-architecture control using a non-reasoning VLA confirms the vulnerability is exclusive to reasoning-augmented models, while instruction-level attacks degrade both architectures -- establishing that the internal reasoning trace is a distinct and stealthy threat vector invisible to input-validation defenses.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型最近越来越多地采用思维链（CoT）推理，即在解码运动指令之前生成一个自然语言计划。推理模块和动作解码器之间的这个内部文本通道尚未受到对抗性审查。我们提出这样的问题：动作解码器实际上依赖于这个中间计划的哪些属性？并且，仅仅针对推理轨迹的定向篡改——在所有输入保持不变的情况下——能否降低机器人的物理任务性能？我们设计了一个包含七种文本篡改的分类，这些篡改被组织成三个攻击者层级（盲噪声、机械-语义和LLM自适应），并将它们应用于最先进的推理型VLA，涵盖40个LIBERO桌面操作任务。我们的结果揭示了一个惊人的不对称性：替换推理轨迹中的对象名称会降低8.3个百分点的整体成功率（目标条件任务上达到$-$19.3个百分点，而单个任务上达到$-$45个百分点），而句子重排序、空间方向颠倒、token噪声，甚至是使用一个700亿参数的LLM来生成看似合理但错误的计划，都几乎没有影响（在$\pm$4个百分点以内）。这种不对称性表明，动作解码器依赖于实体引用的完整性，而不是推理质量或顺序结构。值得注意的是，基于LLM的复杂攻击者性能不如简单的机械对象名称替换，因为保持合理性会无意中保留了解码器所需的实体-grounding结构。使用非推理型VLA的跨架构控制证实了该漏洞仅限于推理增强型模型，而指令级攻击会降低两种架构的性能——表明内部推理轨迹是一种独特的、隐蔽的威胁向量，对输入验证防御是不可见的。

TLDR: This paper identifies a vulnerability in Chain-of-Thought Vision-Language-Action models where substituting object names in the reasoning trace significantly impacts robot performance, suggesting a strong reliance on entity-reference integrity by the action decoder.

简要说明: 该论文发现了一种Chain-of-Thought视觉语言行动模型中的漏洞，即在推理过程中替换对象名称会显著影响机器人性能，这表明行动解码器严重依赖实体参考完整性。

Authors: Tuan Duong Trinh, Naveed Akhtar, Basim Azam

HaltNav: Reactive Visual Halting over Lightweight Topological Priors for Robust Vision-Language Navigation

Abstract (English): Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) is shifting from rigid, step-by-step instruction following toward open-vocabulary, goal-oriented autonomy. Achieving this transition without exhaustive routing prompts requires agents to leverage structural priors. While prior work often assumes computationally heavy 2D/3D metric maps, we instead exploit a lightweight, text-based osmAG (OpenStreetMap Area Graph), a floorplan-level topological representation that is easy to obtain and maintain. However, global planning over a prior map alone is brittle in real-world deployments, where local connectivity can change (e.g., closed doors or crowded passages), leading to execution-time failures. To address this gap, we propose a hierarchical navigation framework HaltNav that couples the robust global planning of osmAG with the local exploration and instruction-grounding capability of VLN. Our approach features an MLLM-based brain module, which is capable of high-level task grounding and obstruction awareness. Conditioned on osmAG, the brain converts the global route into a sequence of localized execution snippets, providing the VLN executor with prior-grounded, goal-centric sub-instructions. Meanwhile, it detects local anomalies via a mechanism we term Reactive Visual Halting (RVH), which interrupts the local control loop, updates osmAG by invalidating the corresponding topology, and triggers replanning to orchestrate a viable detour. To train this halting capability efficiently, we introduce a data synthesis pipeline that leverages generative models to inject realistic obstacles into otherwise navigable scenes, substantially enriching hard negative samples. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our hierarchical framework outperforms several baseline methods without tedious language instructions, and significantly improves robustness for long-horizon vision-language navigation under environmental changes.

摘要（中文）: 视觉语言导航（VLN）正从严格的、逐步的指令遵循转向开放词汇、目标导向的自主性。在没有详尽的路由提示的情况下实现这种转变，要求智能体利用结构先验。虽然先前的工作通常假设计算量大的2D/3D度量地图，但我们转而利用轻量级的、基于文本的osmAG（OpenStreetMap Area Graph），这是一种易于获取和维护的楼层平面级拓扑表示。然而，仅基于先验地图的全局规划在现实世界部署中是脆弱的，局部连通性可能会发生变化（例如，关闭的门或拥挤的通道），从而导致执行时失败。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了一种分层导航框架HaltNav，将osmAG的鲁棒全局规划与VLN的局部探索和指令对齐能力相结合。我们的方法采用一个基于MLLM的大脑模块，该模块能够进行高层次的任务对齐和障碍物感知。在osmAG的条件下，大脑将全局路线转换为一系列局部化的执行片段，为VLN执行器提供基于先验的、以目标为中心的子指令。同时，它通过我们称之为反应式视觉停止（RVH）的机制来检测局部异常，从而中断局部控制回路，通过使相应的拓扑失效来更新osmAG，并触发重新规划以协调可行的绕行方案。为了高效地训练这种停止能力，我们引入了一种数据合成管道，利用生成模型将真实的障碍物注入到原本可导航的场景中，从而大大丰富了困难负样本。大量的实验表明，我们的分层框架在没有繁琐的语言指令的情况下优于几种基线方法，并且在环境变化下显著提高了长程视觉语言导航的鲁棒性。

TLDR: The paper introduces HaltNav, a hierarchical vision-language navigation framework using a lightweight topological map and reactive visual halting to improve robustness in dynamically changing environments.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了HaltNav，一种分层视觉语言导航框架，它使用轻量级的拓扑地图和反应式视觉停止（reactive visual halting）来提高在动态变化环境中的鲁棒性。

Authors: Pingcong Li, Zihui Yu, Bichi Zhang, Sören Schwertfeger

Learning Athletic Humanoid Tennis Skills from Imperfect Human Motion Data

Abstract (English): Human athletes demonstrate versatile and highly-dynamic tennis skills to successfully conduct competitive rallies with a high-speed tennis ball. However, reproducing such behaviors on humanoid robots is difficult, partially due to the lack of perfect humanoid action data or human kinematic motion data in tennis scenarios as reference. In this work, we propose LATENT, a system that Learns Athletic humanoid TEnnis skills from imperfect human motioN daTa. The imperfect human motion data consist only of motion fragments that capture the primitive skills used when playing tennis rather than precise and complete human-tennis motion sequences from real-world tennis matches, thereby significantly reducing the difficulty of data collection. Our key insight is that, despite being imperfect, such quasi-realistic data still provide priors about human primitive skills in tennis scenarios. With further correction and composition, we learn a humanoid policy that can consistently strike incoming balls under a wide range of conditions and return them to target locations, while preserving natural motion styles. We also propose a series of designs for robust sim-to-real transfer and deploy our policy on the Unitree G1 humanoid robot. Our method achieves surprising results in the real world and can stably sustain multi-shot rallies with human players. Project page: https://zzk273.github.io/LATENT/

摘要（中文）: 人类运动员展现出多功能且高度动态的网球技能，以成功地进行高速网球对打。然而，在人形机器人上重现这种行为颇具难度，部分原因在于缺乏完美的网球场景下的人形动作数据或人类运动学数据作为参考。在本文中，我们提出了LATENT，一个从不完善的人类运动数据中学习运动型人形网球技能的系统。不完善的人类运动数据仅包含捕捉网球运动中使用的原始技能的运动片段，而非来自真实网球比赛的精确且完整的人类网球运动序列，从而显著降低了数据收集的难度。我们的关键洞见在于，尽管不完善，但这种准真实数据仍然提供了关于人类在网球场景中原始技能的先验知识。 通过进一步的修正和组合，我们学习到了一种人形机器人策略，该策略能够在各种条件下持续击打来球并将其返回到目标位置，同时保持自然的运动风格。我们还提出了一系列针对鲁棒的从模拟到真实迁移的设计，并将我们的策略部署在宇树G1人形机器人上。我们的方法在现实世界中取得了令人惊讶的成果，并且可以与人类球员稳定地进行多拍对打。项目主页：https://zzk273.github.io/LATENT/

TLDR: The paper introduces LATENT, a system that learns athletic tennis skills for humanoid robots from imperfect human motion fragments using RL, achieving successful sim-to-real transfer and multi-shot rallies with humans on a Unitree G1.

Authors: Zhikai Zhang, Haofei Lu, Yunrui Lian, Ziqing Chen, Yun Liu, Chenghuai Lin, Han Xue, Zicheng Zeng, Zekun Qi, Shaolin Zheng, Qing Luan, Jingbo Wang, Junliang Xing, He Wang, Li Yi

TacVLA: Contact-Aware Tactile Fusion for Robust Vision-Language-Action Manipulation

Abstract (English): Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have demonstrated significant advantages in robotic manipulation. However, their reliance on vision and language often leads to suboptimal performance in tasks involving visual occlusion, fine-grained manipulation, and physical contact. To address these challenges, we propose TacVLA, a fine-tuned VLA model by incorporating tactile modalities into the transformer-based policy to enhance fine-grained manipulation capabilities. Specifically, we introduce a contact-aware gating mechanism that selectively activates tactile tokens only when contact is detected, enabling adaptive multimodal fusion while avoiding irrelevant tactile interference. The fused visual, language, and tactile tokens are jointly processed within the transformer architecture to strengthen cross-modal grounding during contact-rich interaction. Extensive experiments on constraint-locked disassembly, in-box picking and robustness evaluations demonstrate that our model outperforms baselines, improving the performance by averaging 20% success rate in disassembly, 60% in in-box picking and 2.1x improvement in scenarios with visual occlusion. Videos are available at https://sites.google.com/view/tacvla and code will be released.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型已经在机器人操控中展示出显著优势。然而，它们对视觉和语言的依赖常常导致在涉及视觉遮挡、精细操作和物理接触的任务中表现欠佳。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了TacVLA，通过将触觉模态融入基于Transformer的策略中，对VLA模型进行微调，从而提升精细操作能力。具体来说，我们引入了一种接触感知门控机制，仅在检测到接触时才选择性地激活触觉tokens，在避免无关触觉干扰的同时，实现自适应的多模态融合。融合的视觉、语言和触觉tokens在Transformer架构中联合处理，以增强富接触交互过程中的跨模态对齐。在约束锁定拆卸、盒内拾取和鲁棒性评估的大量实验表明，我们的模型优于基线模型，在拆卸任务中成功率平均提高20%，盒内拾取任务提高60%，在视觉遮挡场景中提高2.1倍。项目视频见https://sites.google.com/view/tacvla，代码即将发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces TacVLA, a vision-language-action model that incorporates tactile feedback with a contact-aware gating mechanism to improve robotic manipulation, particularly in scenarios with visual occlusion or fine-grained interactions, demonstrating significant performance gains over baselines.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了TacVLA，一种结合触觉反馈的视觉-语言-动作模型，通过接触感知门控机制来改善机器人操作，尤其是在视觉遮挡或精细交互的场景中，并展示了相对于基线的显著性能提升。

Authors: Kaidi Zhang, Heng Zhang, Zhengtong Xu, Zhiyuan Zhang, Md Rakibul Islam Prince, Xiang Li, Xiaojing Han, Yuhao Zhou, Arash Ajoudani, Yu She

Autonomous Integration and Improvement of Robotic Assembly using Skill Graph Representations

Abstract (English): Robotic assembly systems traditionally require substantial manual engineering effort to integrate new tasks, adapt to new environments, and improve performance over time. This paper presents a framework for autonomous integration and continuous improvement of robotic assembly systems based on Skill Graph representations. A Skill Graph organizes robot capabilities as verb-based skills, explicitly linking semantic descriptions (verbs and nouns) with executable policies, pre-conditions, post-conditions, and evaluators. We show how Skill Graphs enable rapid system integration by supporting semantic-level planning over skills, while simultaneously grounding execution through well-defined interfaces to robot controllers and perception modules. After initial deployment, the same Skill Graph structure supports systematic data collection and closed-loop performance improvement, enabling iterative refinement of skills and their composition. We demonstrate how this approach unifies system configuration, execution, evaluation, and learning within a single representation, providing a scalable pathway toward adaptive and reusable robotic assembly systems. The code is at https://github.com/intelligent-control-lab/AIDF.

摘要（中文）: 机器人装配系统传统上需要大量的人工工程工作来集成新任务、适应新环境以及随时间推移提高性能。本文提出了一种用于机器人装配系统自主集成和持续改进的框架，该框架基于技能图 (Skill Graph) 表示。技能图将机器人能力组织成基于动词的技能，明确地将语义描述（动词和名词）与可执行策略、前置条件、后置条件和评估器联系起来。我们展示了技能图如何通过支持基于技能的语义级别规划来实现快速系统集成，同时通过与机器人控制器和感知模块的明确定义的接口来实现执行落地。在初始部署之后，相同的技能图结构支持系统的数据收集和闭环性能改进，从而能够迭代地改进技能及其组合。我们演示了这种方法如何在一个统一的表示中统一系统配置、执行、评估和学习，为自适应和可重用的机器人装配系统提供可扩展的途径。代码位于 https://github.com/intelligent-control-lab/AIDF。

TLDR: The paper introduces a Skill Graph framework for autonomous integration and improvement of robotic assembly systems by unifying system configuration, execution, evaluation, and learning within a single representation.

Authors: Peiqi Yu, Philip Huang, Chaitanya Chawla, Guanya Shi, Jiaoyang Li, Changliu Liu

CarPLAN: Context-Adaptive and Robust Planning with Dynamic Scene Awareness for Autonomous Driving

Abstract (English): Imitation learning (IL) is widely used for motion planning in autonomous driving due to its data efficiency and access to real-world driving data. For safe and robust real-world driving, IL-based planning requires capturing the complex driving contexts inherent in real-world data and enabling context-adaptive decision-making, rather than relying solely on expert trajectory imitation. In this paper, we propose CarPLAN, a novel IL-based motion planning framework that explicitly enhances driving context understanding and enables adaptive planning across diverse traffic scenarios. Our contributions are twofold: We introduce Displacement-Aware Predictive Encoding (DPE) to improve the model's spatial awareness by predicting future displacement vectors between the Autonomous Vehicle (AV) and surrounding scene elements. This allows the planner to account for relational spacing when generating trajectories. In addition to the standard imitation loss, we incorporate an augmented loss term that captures displacement prediction errors, ensuring planning decisions consider relative distances from other agents. To improve the model's ability to handle diverse driving contexts, we propose Context-Adaptive Multi-Expert Decoder (CMD), which leverages the Mixture of Experts (MoE) framework. CMD dynamically selects the most suitable expert decoders based on scene structure at each Transformer layer, enabling adaptive and context-aware planning in dynamic environments. We evaluate CarPLAN on the nuPlan benchmark and demonstrate state-of-the-art performance across all closed-loop simulation metrics. In particular, CarPLAN exhibits robust performance on challenging scenarios such as Test14-Hard, validating its effectiveness in complex driving conditions. Additional experiments on the Waymax benchmark further demonstrate its generalization capability across different benchmark settings.

摘要（中文）: 模仿学习（IL）因其数据效率和获取真实世界驾驶数据的便利性而被广泛应用于自动驾驶中的运动规划。为了实现安全稳健的真实世界驾驶，基于IL的规划需要捕捉真实世界数据中固有的复杂驾驶环境，并实现环境自适应决策，而不是仅仅依赖于专家轨迹模仿。在本文中，我们提出CarPLAN，一种新颖的基于IL的运动规划框架，它显式地增强了驾驶环境理解能力，并能够在各种交通场景中进行自适应规划。我们的贡献有两方面：我们引入了位移感知预测编码（DPE），通过预测自动驾驶汽车（AV）与周围场景元素之间的未来位移向量来提高模型的空间感知能力。这使得规划器在生成轨迹时能够考虑关系间距。除了标准的模仿损失外，我们还引入了一个增强的损失项，它捕获位移预测误差，确保规划决策考虑到与其他车辆的相对距离。为了提高模型处理各种驾驶环境的能力，我们提出了环境自适应多专家解码器（CMD），它利用了专家混合（MoE）框架。CMD基于每个Transformer层的场景结构动态选择最合适的专家解码器，从而在动态环境中实现自适应和环境感知的规划。我们在nuPlan基准上评估了CarPLAN，并在所有闭环仿真指标上展示了最先进的性能。特别是在Test14-Hard等具有挑战性的场景中，CarPLAN表现出稳健的性能，验证了其在复杂驾驶条件下的有效性。在Waymax基准上的额外实验进一步证明了其在不同基准设置中的泛化能力。

TLDR: CarPLAN is a novel imitation learning-based motion planning framework for autonomous driving that enhances context understanding and enables adaptive planning using Displacement-Aware Predictive Encoding and a Context-Adaptive Multi-Expert Decoder.

简要说明: CarPLAN是一种新颖的基于模仿学习的自动驾驶运动规划框架，它通过使用位移感知预测编码和上下文自适应多专家解码器来增强上下文理解并实现自适应规划。

Authors: Junyong Yun, Jungho Kim, ByungHyun Lee, Dongyoung Lee, Sehwan Choi, Seunghyeop Nam, Kichun Jo, Jun Won Choi

From Woofs to Words: Towards Intelligent Robotic Guide Dogs with Verbal Communication

Abstract (English): Assistive robotics is an important subarea of robotics that focuses on the well-being of people with disabilities. A robotic guide dog is an assistive quadruped robot that helps visually impaired people in obstacle avoidance and navigation. Enabling language capabilities for robotic guide dogs goes beyond naively adding an existing dialog system onto a mobile robot. The novel challenges include grounding language in the dynamically changing environment and improving spatial awareness for the human handler. To address those challenges, we develop a novel dialog system for robotic guide dogs that uses LLMs to verbalize both navigational plans and scenes. The goal is to enable verbal communication for collaborative decision-making within the handler-robot team. In experiments, we conducted a human study to evaluate different verbalization strategies and a simulation study to assess the efficiency and accuracy in navigation tasks.

Authors: Yohei Hayamizu, David DeFazio, Hrudayangam Mehta, Zainab Altaweel, Jacqueline Choe, Chao Lin, Jake Juettner, Furui Xiao, Jeremy Blackburn, Shiqi Zhang

Red-Teaming Vision-Language-Action Models via Quality Diversity Prompt Generation for Robust Robot Policies

Abstract (English): Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have significant potential to enable general-purpose robotic systems for a range of vision-language tasks. However, the performance of VLA-based robots is highly sensitive to the precise wording of language instructions, and it remains difficult to predict when such robots will fail. To improve the robustness of VLAs to different wordings, we present Q-DIG (Quality Diversity for Diverse Instruction Generation), which performs red-teaming by scalably identifying diverse natural language task descriptions that induce failures while remaining task-relevant. Q-DIG integrates Quality Diversity (QD) techniques with Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to generate a broad spectrum of adversarial instructions that expose meaningful vulnerabilities in VLA behavior. Our results across multiple simulation benchmarks show that Q-DIG finds more diverse and meaningful failure modes compared to baseline methods, and that fine-tuning VLAs on the generated instructions improves task success rates. Furthermore, results from a user study highlight that Q-DIG generates prompts judged to be more natural and human-like than those from baselines. Finally, real-world evaluations of Q-DIG prompts show results consistent with simulation, and fine-tuning VLAs on the generated prompts further success rates on unseen instructions. Together, these findings suggest that Q-DIG is a promising approach for identifying vulnerabilities and improving the robustness of VLA-based robots. Our anonymous project website is at qdigvla.github.io.

摘要（中文）: 视觉-语言-动作 (VLA) 模型在实现适用于各种视觉-语言任务的通用机器人系统方面具有巨大的潜力。 然而，基于 VLA 的机器人的性能对语言指令的精确措辞高度敏感，并且预测此类机器人何时失效仍然很困难。 为了提高 VLA 对不同措辞的鲁棒性，我们提出了 Q-DIG (多样化指令生成中的质量多样性)，它通过可扩展地识别多样化的自然语言任务描述来执行红队演练，这些描述会导致失败，同时保持与任务的相关性。 Q-DIG 将质量多样性 (QD) 技术与视觉-语言模型 (VLM) 集成，以生成广泛的对抗性指令，从而暴露 VLA 行为中具有意义的漏洞。 我们在多个模拟基准测试中的结果表明，与基线方法相比，Q-DIG 能够找到更多样化和有意义的失效模式，并且在生成的指令上微调 VLA 可以提高任务成功率。 此外，用户研究的结果表明，Q-DIG 生成的提示被认为比基线的提示更自然和更像人类。 最后，Q-DIG 提示的真实世界评估显示出与模拟一致的结果，并且在生成的提示上微调 VLA 可以进一步提高未见指令上的成功率。 总之，这些发现表明，Q-DIG 是一种很有前途的方法，可以识别漏洞并提高基于 VLA 的机器人的鲁棒性。 我们的匿名项目网站位于 qdigvla.github.io。

TLDR: The paper introduces Q-DIG, a Quality Diversity based method for red-teaming Vision-Language-Action models by generating diverse and adversarial natural language instructions to improve the robustness of robotic systems. Fine-tuning on the generated prompts improves task success rates in both simulation and real-world settings.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为Q-DIG的方法，它基于质量多样性，通过生成多样化的对抗性自然语言指令来对视觉-语言-动作模型进行红队测试，从而提高机器人的鲁棒性。 在生成的提示上进行微调可以提高仿真和现实环境中的任务成功率。

Authors: Siddharth Srikanth, Freddie Liang, Sophie Hsu, Varun Bhatt, Shihan Zhao, Henry Chen, Bryon Tjanaka, Minjune Hwang, Akanksha Saran, Daniel Seita, Aaquib Tabrez, Stefanos Nikolaidis

Robots that redesign themselves through kinematic self-destruction

Abstract (English): Every robot built to date was predesigned by an external process, prior to deployment. Here we show a robot that actively participates in its own design during its lifetime. Starting from a randomly assembled body, and using only proprioceptive feedback, the robot dynamically ``sculpts'' itself into a new design through kinematic self-destruction: identifying redundant links within its body that inhibit its locomotion, and then thrashing those links against the surface until they break at the joint and fall off the body. It does so using a single autoregressive sequence model, a universal controller that learns in simulation when and how to simplify a robot's body through self-destruction and then adaptively controls the reduced morphology. The optimized policy successfully transfers to reality and generalizes to previously unseen kinematic trees, generating forward locomotion that is more effective than otherwise equivalent policies that randomly remove links or cannot remove any. This suggests that self-designing robots may be more successful than predesigned robots in some cases, and that kinematic self-destruction, though reductive and irreversible, could provide a general adaptive strategy for a wide range of robots.

摘要（中文）: 迄今为止，所有制造的机器人都经过外部流程预先设计，然后在部署前完成。本文中，我们展示了一种在其生命周期内主动参与自身设计的机器人。它从随机组装的身体开始，仅利用本体感受反馈，通过运动学自毁动态地“雕塑”自身形成新的设计：识别其体内抑制运动的多余连接，然后将这些连接撞击表面，直到其在关节处断裂并从身体上脱落。它使用一个自回归序列模型，一种通用控制器，该控制器在模拟中学习何时以及如何通过自毁简化机器人的身体，然后自适应地控制简化的形态。优化后的策略成功转移到现实，并推广到先前未见过的运动学树，产生比随机移除连接或无法移除任何连接的等效策略更有效的前进运动。这表明，在某些情况下，自设计机器人可能比预设计机器人更成功，并且运动学自毁虽然具有还原性和不可逆性，但可以为各种机器人提供通用的自适应策略。

TLDR: This paper introduces a robot that can redesign itself by identifying and breaking off redundant links through a process called kinematic self-destruction, guided by a learned autoregressive sequence model, demonstrating improved locomotion compared to robots with fixed designs.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种可以通过运动学自毁过程重新设计自身的机器人，该过程通过学习的自回归序列模型识别并断开多余的链接。实验表明，与固定设计的机器人相比，这种机器人具有更好的运动性能。

Authors: Chen Yu, Sam Kriegman

Visual-ERM: Reward Modeling for Visual Equivalence

Abstract (English): Vision-to-code tasks require models to reconstruct structured visual inputs, such as charts, tables, and SVGs, into executable or structured representations with high visual fidelity. While recent Large Vision Language Models (LVLMs) achieve strong results via supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning remains challenging due to misaligned reward signals. Existing rewards either rely on textual rules or coarse visual embedding similarity, both of which fail to capture fine-grained visual discrepancies and are vulnerable to reward hacking. We propose Visual Equivalence Reward Model (Visual-ERM), a multimodal generative reward model that provides fine-grained, interpretable, and task-agnostic feedback to evaluate vision-to-code quality directly in the rendered visual space. Integrated into RL, Visual-ERM improves Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct by +8.4 on chart-to-code and yields consistent gains on table and SVG parsing (+2.7, +4.1 on average), and further strengthens test-time scaling via reflection and revision. We also introduce VisualCritic-RewardBench (VC-RewardBench), a benchmark for judging fine-grained image-to-image discrepancies on structured visual data, where Visual-ERM at 8B decisively outperforms Qwen3-VL-235B-Instruct and approaches leading closed-source models. Our results suggest that fine-grained visual reward supervision is both necessary and sufficient for vision-to-code RL, regardless of task specificity.

摘要（中文）: 视觉到代码任务要求模型将结构化视觉输入，例如图表、表格和SVG，重构为具有高视觉保真度的可执行或结构化表示。虽然最近的大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）通过监督微调取得了显著成果，但由于奖励信号的不对齐，强化学习仍然具有挑战性。现有的奖励要么依赖于文本规则，要么依赖于粗糙的视觉嵌入相似性，这两种方式都无法捕捉细粒度的视觉差异，并且容易受到奖励黑客的影响。我们提出了一种视觉等价性奖励模型（Visual-ERM），这是一种多模态生成式奖励模型，它提供细粒度、可解释且与任务无关的反馈，以直接在渲染的视觉空间中评估视觉到代码的质量。集成到强化学习中，Visual-ERM在图表到代码任务上使Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct提升+8.4，并在表格和SVG解析上产生一致的收益（平均+2.7，+4.1），并通过反思和修正进一步加强了测试时缩放。我们还引入了VisualCritic-RewardBench（VC-RewardBench），这是一个用于判断结构化视觉数据上细粒度图像到图像差异的基准，在该基准上，8B规模的Visual-ERM果断地优于Qwen3-VL-235B-Instruct，并接近领先的闭源模型。我们的结果表明，无论任务具体性如何，细粒度的视觉奖励监督对于视觉到代码强化学习来说都是必要且充分的。

TLDR: This paper introduces Visual-ERM, a multimodal generative reward model for vision-to-code tasks that uses fine-grained visual feedback, improving RL performance on chart, table, and SVG parsing and outperforming large VLMs on a new benchmark.

简要说明: 本文介绍了Visual-ERM，一种多模态生成奖励模型，用于视觉到代码任务，它使用细粒度的视觉反馈，提高了在图表、表格和SVG解析上的强化学习性能，并在新的基准测试中优于大型视觉语言模型。

Authors: Ziyu Liu, Shengyuan Ding, Xinyu Fang, Xuanlang Dai, Penghui Yang, Jianze Liang, Jiaqi Wang, Kai Chen, Dahua Lin, Yuhang Zang

Steve-Evolving: Open-World Embodied Self-Evolution via Fine-Grained Diagnosis and Dual-Track Knowledge Distillation

Abstract (English): Open-world embodied agents must solve long-horizon tasks where the main bottleneck is not single-step planning quality but how interaction experience is organized and evolved. To this end, we present Steve-Evolving, a non-parametric self-evolving framework that tightly couples fine-grained execution diagnosis with dual-track knowledge distillation in a closed loop. The method follows three phases: Experience Anchoring, Experience Distillation, and Knowledge-Driven Closed-Loop Control. In detail, Experience Anchoring solidifies each subgoal attempt into a structured experience tuple with a fixed schema (pre-state, action, diagnosis-result, and post-state) and organizes it in a three-tier experience space with multi-dimensional indices (e.g., condition signatures, spatial hashing, and semantic tags) plus rolling summarization for efficient and auditable recall. To ensure sufficient information density for attribution, the execution layer provides compositional diagnosis signals beyond binary outcomes, including state-difference summaries, enumerated failure causes, continuous indicators, and stagnation/loop detection. Moreover, successful trajectories of Experience Distillation are generalized into reusable skills with explicit preconditions and verification criteria, while failures are distilled into executable guardrails that capture root causes and forbid risky operations at both subgoal and task granularities. Besides, Knowledge-Driven Closed-Loop Control retrieved skills and guardrails are injected into an LLM planner, and diagnosis-triggered local replanning updates the active constraints online, forming a continual evolution process without any model parameter updates. Experiments on the long-horizon suite of Minecraft MCU demonstrate consistent improvements over static-retrieval baselines.

摘要（中文）: 开放世界具身智能体必须解决长时程任务，而主要瓶颈不在于单步规划的质量，而在于交互经验的组织和演化方式。为此，我们提出 Steve-Evolving，一个非参数自演化框架，它将细粒度执行诊断与双轨知识提炼紧密结合在一个闭环中。该方法遵循三个阶段：经验锚定、经验提炼和知识驱动的闭环控制。具体而言，经验锚定将每个子目标尝试固化为具有固定模式（前置状态、动作、诊断结果和后置状态）的结构化经验元组，并将其组织在一个具有多维索引（例如，条件签名、空间哈希和语义标签）的三层经验空间中，以及用于高效和可审计召回的滚动摘要。为了确保足够的归因信息密度，执行层提供超出二元结果的组合式诊断信号，包括状态差异摘要、枚举的失败原因、连续指标以及停滞/循环检测。此外，经验提炼的成功轨迹被推广为具有显式先决条件和验证标准的可重用技能，而失败则被提炼为可执行的护栏，用于捕获根本原因并禁止次目标和任务粒度的风险操作。此外，知识驱动的闭环控制将检索到的技能和护栏注入到 LLM 规划器中，并且诊断触发的局部重规划在线更新活跃的约束，形成一个没有模型参数更新的持续演化过程。在 Minecraft MCU 的长时程套件上进行的实验表明，相对于静态检索基线，性能得到了持续改进。

TLDR: The paper introduces Steve-Evolving, a non-parametric self-evolving framework for open-world embodied agents that couples fine-grained execution diagnosis with dual-track knowledge distillation, demonstrating improvements on long-horizon Minecraft tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Steve-Evolving，一个用于开放世界具身智能体的非参数自演化框架，它将细粒度的执行诊断与双轨知识蒸馏相结合，并在长期Minecraft任务中展示了了改进。

Authors: Zhengwei Xie, Zhisheng Chen, Ziyan Weng, Tingyu Wu, Chenglong Li, Vireo Zhang, Kun Wang

Geometry-Guided Camera Motion Understanding in VideoLLMs

Abstract (English): Camera motion is a fundamental geometric signal that shapes visual perception and cinematic style, yet current video-capable vision-language models (VideoLLMs) rarely represent it explicitly and often fail on fine-grained motion primitives. We address this gap with a framework of $\textbf{benchmarking}$, $\textbf{diagnosis}$, and $\textbf{injection}$. We curate $\textbf{CameraMotionDataset}$, a large-scale synthetic dataset with explicit camera control, formulate camera motion as constraint-aware multi-label recognition, and construct a VQA benchmark--$\textbf{CameraMotionVQA}$. Across diverse off-the-shelf VideoLLMs, we observe substantial errors in recognizing camera motion primitives. Probing experiments on a Qwen2.5-VL vision encoder suggest that camera motion cues are weakly represented, especially in deeper ViT blocks, helping explain the observed failure modes. To bridge this gap without costly training or fine-tuning, we propose a lightweight, model-agnostic pipeline that extracts geometric camera cues from 3D foundation models (3DFMs), predicts constrained motion primitives with a temporal classifier, and injects them into downstream VideoLLM inference via structured prompting. Experiments demonstrate improved motion recognition and more camera-aware model responses, highlighting geometry-driven cue extraction and structured prompting as practical steps toward a camera-aware VideoLLM and VLA system. The dataset and benchmark is publicly available at https://hf.co/datasets/fengyee/camera-motion-dataset-and-benchmark.

摘要（中文）: 相机运动是塑造视觉感知和电影风格的基本几何信号，然而，目前的视频-语言模型（VideoLLMs）很少显式地表示它，并且经常在细粒度的运动基元上失效。我们用一个$\textbf{基准测试}$、$\textbf{诊断}$和$\textbf{注入}$的框架来解决这一差距。我们策划了一个$\textbf{CameraMotionDataset}$，这是一个具有显式相机控制的大规模合成数据集，将相机运动形式化为约束感知的多标签识别，并构建了一个VQA基准--$\textbf{CameraMotionVQA}$。在各种现成的VideoLLMs上，我们观察到在识别相机运动基元方面存在大量错误。对Qwen2.5-VL视觉编码器的探针实验表明，相机运动线索的表示很弱，尤其是在更深的ViT块中，这有助于解释观察到的失效模式。为了在没有昂贵的训练或微调的情况下弥合这一差距，我们提出了一个轻量级的、模型无关的流程，该流程从3D基础模型（3DFMs）中提取几何相机线索，用时间分类器预测受约束的运动基元，并通过结构化提示将其注入到下游VideoLLM推理中。实验表明，运动识别得到了改善，并且模型的响应更具相机感知能力，突出了几何驱动的线索提取和结构化提示是构建相机感知的VideoLLM和VLA系统的切实步骤。该数据集和基准测试已在https://hf.co/datasets/fengyee/camera-motion-dataset-and-benchmark上公开。

TLDR: This paper introduces a new benchmark and method for improving camera motion understanding in VideoLLMs by extracting and injecting geometric camera cues from 3D foundation models via structured prompting, leading to improved motion recognition and camera-aware responses.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种新的基准测试和方法，通过从3D基础模型中提取和注入几何相机信息，并通过结构化提示改进VideoLLM中相机运动理解，从而提高运动识别和相机感知能力。

Authors: Haoan Feng, Sri Harsha Musunuri, Guan-Ming Su

Beyond Final Answers: CRYSTAL Benchmark for Transparent Multimodal Reasoning Evaluation

Abstract (English): We introduce **CRYSTAL** (*__C__lear __R__easoning via __Y__ielded __S__teps, __T__raceability and __L__ogic*), a diagnostic benchmark with 6,372 instances that evaluates multimodal reasoning through verifiable intermediate steps. We propose two complementary metrics: *Match F1*, which scores step-level precision and recall via semantic similarity matching, and *Ordered Match F1*, which further penalizes disordered reasoning chains. References are constructed through a Delphi-inspired pipeline where four independent MLLMs generate trajectories, aggregated via semantic clustering and validated through human quality gates. Evaluation of 20 MLLMs, including commercial frontier systems not used during benchmark construction, reveals systematic failures invisible to accuracy: universal cherry-picking (precision far exceeds recall), non-monotonic scaling trade-offs, and disordered reasoning where no competitive model preserves more than 60% of matched steps in correct order. Beyond evaluation, we propose the **Causal Process Reward (CPR)**, a multiplicative reward that couples answer correctness with step-level alignment, and **CPR-Curriculum**, which progressively increases reasoning difficulty during training. CPR-Curriculum achieves +32% Match F1 via GRPO where additive reward strategies fail, improving reasoning without manual step annotation.

摘要（中文）: 我们引入 **CRYSTAL** (*__C__lear __R__easoning via __Y__ielded __S__teps, __T__raceability and __L__ogic*，即*通过可验证步骤、可追溯性和逻辑实现的清晰推理*)，这是一个包含6372个实例的诊断基准，旨在通过可验证的中间步骤评估多模态推理能力。 我们提出了两个互补的指标：*匹配 F1*(Match F1)，通过语义相似性匹配来评估步骤级别的精确率和召回率；以及*有序匹配 F1*(Ordered Match F1)，进一步惩罚无序的推理链。参考文献通过类 Delphi 流程构建，该流程由四个独立的 MLLM 生成轨迹，通过语义聚类聚合，并通过人工质量门验证。对 20 个 MLLM (包括在基准构建过程中未使用的商业前沿系统) 的评估揭示了准确率无法体现的系统性缺陷：普遍存在的选择性采摘 (精确率远超召回率)、非单调的缩放权衡，以及无序的推理，其中没有有竞争力的模型能以正确的顺序保留超过 60% 的匹配步骤。除了评估，我们还提出了 **因果过程奖励 (Causal Process Reward, CPR)**，这是一种将答案正确性与步骤级别对齐相结合的乘法奖励，以及 **CPR 课程学习 (CPR-Curriculum)**，它在训练过程中逐渐增加推理难度。 通过GRPO，CPR 课程学习实现了 +32% 的匹配 F1，而加性奖励策略则失败了，无需手动步骤标注即可提高推理能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces CRYSTAL, a benchmark for evaluating multimodal reasoning through verifiable intermediate steps, along with metrics (Match F1, Ordered Match F1) and a reward shaping method (CPR) and curriculum learning approach (CPR-Curriculum) to improve reasoning in MLLMs.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了CRYSTAL，一个通过可验证的中间步骤评估多模态推理的基准，以及指标（Match F1、Ordered Match F1）和一个奖励塑造方法（CPR）和课程学习方法（CPR-Curriculum）来改进MLLM中的推理。
