Authors: Wayner Barrios, SouYoung Jin

ARL-Tangram: Unleash the Resource Efficiency in Agentic Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Agentic reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a transformative workload in cloud clusters, enabling large language models (LLMs) to solve complex problems through interactions with real world. However, unlike traditional RL, agentic RL demands substantial external cloud resources, e.g., CPUs for code execution and GPUs for reward models, that exist outside the primary training cluster. Existing agentic RL framework typically rely on static over-provisioning, i.e., resources are often tied to long-lived trajectories or isolated by tasks, which leads to severe resource inefficiency. We propose the action-level orchestration, and incorporate it into ARL-Tangram, a unified resource management system that enables fine-grained external resource sharing and elasticity. ARL-Tangram utilizes a unified action-level formulation and an elastic scheduling algorithm to minimize action completion time (ACT) while satisfying heterogeneous resource constraints. Further, heterogeneous resource managers are tailored to efficiently support the action-level execution on resources with heterogeneous characteristics and topologies. Evaluation on real-world agentic RL tasks demonstrates that ARL-Tangram improves average ACT by up to 4.3$\times$, speeds up the step duration of RL training by up to 1.5$\times$, and saves the external resources by up to 71.2$\%$. This system has been deployed to support the training of the MiMo series models.

摘要（中文）: 代理强化学习(RL)已成为云集群中一种变革性的工作负载，它使大型语言模型(LLM)能够通过与现实世界的交互来解决复杂问题。然而，与传统强化学习不同，代理强化学习需要大量的外部云资源，例如，用于代码执行的CPU和用于奖励模型的GPU，这些资源存在于主要训练集群之外。现有的代理强化学习框架通常依赖于静态过度配置，即资源通常绑定到长期存在的轨迹或被任务隔离，从而导致严重的资源效率低下。 我们提出了动作级编排，并将其整合到 ARL-Tangram 中，这是一个统一的资源管理系统，能够实现细粒度的外部资源共享和弹性。ARL-Tangram 利用统一的动作级公式和弹性调度算法，在满足异构资源约束的同时，最小化动作完成时间(ACT)。此外，异构资源管理器经过定制，可有效地支持在具有异构特性和拓扑结构的资源上进行动作级执行。在真实世界的代理强化学习任务中的评估表明，ARL-Tangram 将平均ACT提高了高达4.3倍，将RL训练的步长持续时间加快了高达1.5倍，并节省了高达71.2%的外部资源。该系统已部署以支持 MiMo 系列模型的训练。

TLDR: The paper introduces ARL-Tangram, a resource management system for agentic RL that optimizes resource allocation and reduces execution time by action-level orchestration and elastic scheduling, resulting in significant resource savings and performance improvements on real-world tasks and enabling the training of models like MiMo series.

简要说明: 本文介绍了ARL-Tangram，一种用于智能体强化学习的资源管理系统，通过动作级编排和弹性调度来优化资源分配并缩短执行时间，从而在实际任务中显著节省资源并提高性能，并支持MiMo系列模型的训练。

Authors: Bangjun Xiao, Yihao Zhao, Xiangwei Deng, Shihua Yu, Yuxing Xiang, Huaqiu Liu, Qiying Wang, Liang Zhao, Hailin Zhang, Xuanzhe Liu, Xin Jin, Fuli Luo

Thinking in Streaming Video

Abstract (English): Real-time understanding of continuous video streams is essential for interactive assistants and multimodal agents operating in dynamic environments. However, most existing video reasoning approaches follow a batch paradigm that defers reasoning until the full video context is observed, resulting in high latency and growing computational cost that are incompatible with streaming scenarios. In this paper, we introduce ThinkStream, a framework for streaming video reasoning based on a Watch--Think--Speak paradigm that enables models to incrementally update their understanding as new video observations arrive. At each step, the model performs a short reasoning update and decides whether sufficient evidence has accumulated to produce a response. To support long-horizon streaming, we propose Reasoning-Compressed Streaming Memory (RCSM), which treats intermediate reasoning traces as compact semantic memory that replaces outdated visual tokens while preserving essential context. We further train the model using a Streaming Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards scheme that aligns incremental reasoning and response timing with the requirements of streaming interaction. Experiments on multiple streaming video benchmarks show that ThinkStream significantly outperforms existing online video models while maintaining low latency and memory usage. Code, models and data will be released at https://github.com/johncaged/ThinkStream

摘要（中文）: 本文介绍了一种名为ThinkStream的框架，用于流式视频推理。在动态环境中运行的交互式助手和多模态智能体需要实时理解连续视频流。然而，现有的大多数视频推理方法都遵循批处理模式，即延迟推理，直到观察到完整的视频上下文，从而导致高延迟和不断增长的计算成本，这与流式场景不兼容。ThinkStream基于Watch-Think-Speak范式，使模型能够在新的视频观测到达时逐步更新其理解。在每个步骤中，模型执行一个简短的推理更新，并决定是否积累了足够的证据来产生响应。为了支持长期的流式传输，我们提出了一种推理压缩流式内存（RCSM），将中间推理轨迹视为紧凑的语义记忆，从而替换过时的视觉标记，同时保留必要的上下文。我们进一步使用一种带有可验证奖励的流式强化学习方案来训练模型，该方案使增量推理和响应时间与流式交互的需求相一致。在多个流式视频基准测试上的实验表明，ThinkStream显著优于现有的在线视频模型，同时保持了低延迟和内存使用率。代码、模型和数据将在https://github.com/johncaged/ThinkStream上发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces ThinkStream, a novel framework for real-time streaming video reasoning that utilizes incremental updates, compressed memory, and streaming reinforcement learning to achieve low latency and memory usage. It significantly outperforms existing online video models on streaming benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为ThinkStream的新框架，用于实时流视频推理，它利用增量更新、压缩记忆和流强化学习来实现低延迟和内存使用。在流基准测试中，它的性能明显优于现有的在线视频模型。

Authors: Zikang Liu, Longteng Guo, Handong Li, Ru Zhen, Xingjian He, Ruyi Ji, Xiaoming Ren, Yanhao Zhang, Haonan Lu, Jing Liu

Efficient and Interpretable Multi-Agent LLM Routing via Ant Colony Optimization

Abstract (English): Large Language Model (LLM)-driven Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) have demonstrated strong capability in complex reasoning and tool use, and heterogeneous agent pools further broaden the quality--cost trade-off space. Despite these advances, real-world deployment is often constrained by high inference cost, latency, and limited transparency, which hinders scalable and efficient routing. Existing routing strategies typically rely on expensive LLM-based selectors or static policies, and offer limited controllability for semantic-aware routing under dynamic loads and mixed intents, often resulting in unstable performance and inefficient resource utilization. To address these limitations, we propose AMRO-S, an efficient and interpretable routing framework for Multi-Agent Systems (MAS). AMRO-S models MAS routing as a semantic-conditioned path selection problem, enhancing routing performance through three key mechanisms: First, it leverages a supervised fine-tuned (SFT) small language model for intent inference, providing a low-overhead semantic interface for each query; second, it decomposes routing memory into task-specific pheromone specialists, reducing cross-task interference and optimizing path selection under mixed workloads; finally, it employs a quality-gated asynchronous update mechanism to decouple inference from learning, optimizing routing without increasing latency. Extensive experiments on five public benchmarks and high-concurrency stress tests demonstrate that AMRO-S consistently improves the quality--cost trade-off over strong routing baselines, while providing traceable routing evidence through structured pheromone patterns.

摘要（中文）: 由大型语言模型（LLM）驱动的多智能体系统（MAS）已展现出在复杂推理和工具使用方面的强大能力，而异构智能体池进一步拓宽了质量-成本权衡空间。尽管取得了这些进展，但实际部署往往受到高推理成本、延迟和有限的透明度的制约，这阻碍了可扩展和高效的路由。现有的路由策略通常依赖于昂贵的基于LLM的选择器或静态策略，并且在动态负载和混合意图下，针对语义感知路由的可控性有限，经常导致不稳定的性能和低效的资源利用。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了AMRO-S，一种高效且可解释的用于多智能体系统（MAS）的路由框架。AMRO-S将MAS路由建模为语义条件下的路径选择问题，并通过三个关键机制增强路由性能：首先，它利用一个经过监督精调（SFT）的小型语言模型进行意图推断，为每个查询提供了一个低开销的语义接口；其次，它将路由记忆分解为特定于任务的信息素专家，减少跨任务干扰，并在混合工作负载下优化路径选择；最后，它采用质量门控异步更新机制来解耦推理和学习，从而优化路由而不会增加延迟。在五个公共基准测试和高并发压力测试中的大量实验表明，AMRO-S始终优于强大的路由基线，从而改善了质量-成本权衡，同时通过结构化的信息素模式提供可追踪的路由依据。

TLDR: The paper introduces AMRO-S, an efficient and interpretable routing framework for multi-agent LLM systems that uses a small language model for intent inference and ant colony optimization for route selection, demonstrating improved performance and interpretability compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了AMRO-S，一个为多智能体LLM系统设计的高效且可解释的路由框架。该框架利用小型语言模型进行意图推断，并使用蚁群优化算法进行路由选择，与现有方法相比，性能和可解释性均有提升。

Authors: Xudong Wang, Chaoning Zhang, Jiaquan Zhang, Chenghao Li, Qigan Sun, Sung-Ho Bae, Peng Wang, Ning Xie, Jie Zou, Yang Yang, Hengtao Shen

Finite Difference Flow Optimization for RL Post-Training of Text-to-Image Models

Abstract (English): Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a standard technique for post-training diffusion-based image synthesis models, as it enables learning from reward signals to explicitly improve desirable aspects such as image quality and prompt alignment. In this paper, we propose an online RL variant that reduces the variance in the model updates by sampling paired trajectories and pulling the flow velocity in the direction of the more favorable image. Unlike existing methods that treat each sampling step as a separate policy action, we consider the entire sampling process as a single action. We experiment with both high-quality vision language models and off-the-shelf quality metrics for rewards, and evaluate the outputs using a broad set of metrics. Our method converges faster and yields higher output quality and prompt alignment than previous approaches.

摘要（中文）: 强化学习(RL)已成为后训练扩散图像合成模型的标准技术，因为它能够从奖励信号中学习，从而明确地改善诸如图像质量和提示对齐等期望的方面。在本文中，我们提出了一种在线RL变体，它通过采样配对轨迹并将流动速度拉向更有利图像的方向来减少模型更新的方差。与将每个采样步骤视为单独策略行动的现有方法不同，我们将整个采样过程视为一个单一行动。我们利用高质量的视觉语言模型和现成的质量指标作为奖励进行实验，并使用广泛的指标集评估输出结果。我们的方法收敛速度更快，并且比之前的方法产生更高的输出质量和提示对齐度。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel online RL method for post-training text-to-image models that optimizes the entire sampling process as a single action, demonstrating faster convergence and improved output quality/prompt alignment compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新的在线强化学习方法，用于文本到图像模型的后训练，将整个采样过程优化为一个单一的动作，与现有方法相比，表现出更快的收敛速度和更高的输出质量/提示对齐度。

Authors: David McAllister, Miika Aittala, Tero Karras, Janne Hellsten, Angjoo Kanazawa, Timo Aila, Samuli Laine

ToolTree: Efficient LLM Agent Tool Planning via Dual-Feedback Monte Carlo Tree Search and Bidirectional Pruning

Abstract (English): Large Language Model (LLM) agents are increasingly applied to complex, multi-step tasks that require interaction with diverse external tools across various domains. However, current LLM agent tool planning methods typically rely on greedy, reactive tool selection strategies that lack foresight and fail to account for inter-tool dependencies. In this paper, we present ToolTree, a novel Monte Carlo tree search-inspired planning paradigm for tool planning. ToolTree explores possible tool usage trajectories using a dual-stage LLM evaluation and bidirectional pruning mechanism that enables the agent to make informed, adaptive decisions over extended tool-use sequences while pruning less promising branches before and after the tool execution. Empirical evaluations across both open-set and closed-set tool planning tasks on 4 benchmarks demonstrate that ToolTree consistently improves performance while keeping the highest efficiency, achieving an average gain of around 10\% compared to the state-of-the-art planning paradigm.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型（LLM）智能体正日益被应用于复杂、多步骤的任务中，这些任务需要与跨越多个领域的各种外部工具进行交互。然而，当前的LLM智能体工具规划方法通常依赖于贪婪的、反应式的工具选择策略，缺乏前瞻性，并且未能考虑到工具间的依赖关系。在本文中，我们提出ToolTree，一种受蒙特卡洛树搜索启发的全新工具规划范式。ToolTree利用双阶段LLM评估和双向剪枝机制来探索可能的工具使用轨迹，这使得智能体能够在扩展的工具使用序列中做出知情、自适应的决策，同时在工具执行前后剪除不太有希望的分支。在开放集和闭合集工具规划任务的4个基准测试上的实证评估表明，ToolTree始终如一地提高了性能，同时保持了最高的效率，与最先进的规划范式相比，平均增益约为10%。

TLDR: ToolTree introduces a Monte Carlo Tree Search-based tool planning method for LLM agents, utilizing dual-stage LLM evaluation and bidirectional pruning to improve performance and efficiency in complex, multi-step tasks.

简要说明: ToolTree 提出了一种基于蒙特卡洛树搜索的 LLM 代理工具规划方法，利用双阶段 LLM 评估和双向剪枝来提高复杂多步骤任务中的性能和效率。

Authors: Shuo Yang, Soyeon Caren Han, Yihao Ding, Shuhe Wang, Eduard Hoy

Seeing Eye to Eye: Enabling Cognitive Alignment Through Shared First-Person Perspective in Human-AI Collaboration

Abstract (English): Despite advances in multimodal AI, current vision-based assistants often remain inefficient in collaborative tasks. We identify two key gulfs: a communication gulf, where users must translate rich parallel intentions into verbal commands due to the channel mismatch , and an understanding gulf, where AI struggles to interpret subtle embodied cues. To address these, we propose Eye2Eye, a framework that leverages first-person perspective as a channel for human-AI cognitive alignment. It integrates three components: (1) joint attention coordination for fluid focus alignment, (2) revisable memory to maintain evolving common ground, and (3) reflective feedback allowing users to clarify and refine AI's understanding. We implement this framework in an AR prototype and evaluate it through a user study and a post-hoc pipeline evaluation. Results show that Eye2Eye significantly reduces task completion time and interaction load while increasing trust, demonstrating its components work in concert to improve collaboration.

摘要（中文）: 尽管多模态人工智能取得了进展，但目前基于视觉的助手在协作任务中仍然效率低下。我们发现了两个关键鸿沟：一个沟通鸿沟，由于通道不匹配，用户必须将丰富的并行意图转化为口头指令；以及一个理解鸿沟，人工智能难以解读微妙的具身提示。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了Eye2Eye，一个利用第一人称视角作为人机认知对齐通道的框架。它集成了三个组成部分：（1）用于流畅焦点对齐的联合注意力协调；（2）用于维护不断演变的共同基础的可修订的记忆；以及（3）允许用户澄清和完善人工智能理解的反思性反馈。我们在一个AR原型中实现了该框架，并通过用户研究和事后流水线评估对其进行了评估。结果表明，Eye2Eye显著减少了任务完成时间和交互负荷，同时提高了信任度，证明了其组件协同工作以改善协作。

TLDR: The paper introduces Eye2Eye, a framework using a shared first-person perspective via AR to improve human-AI collaboration by addressing communication and understanding gaps through joint attention, revisable memory, and reflective feedback, demonstrating improved task completion and trust.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了 Eye2Eye，一个通过 AR 使用共享第一人称视角来改善人机协作的框架。它通过联合注意力、可修改的记忆和反思性反馈来解决沟通和理解上的差距，并证明了任务完成度和信任度的提高。

Authors: Zhuyu Teng, Pei Chen, Yichen Cai, Ruoqing Lu, Zhaoqu Jiang, Jiayang Li, Weitao You, Lingyun Sun

Spend Less, Reason Better: Budget-Aware Value Tree Search for LLM Agents

Abstract (English): Test-time scaling has become a dominant paradigm for improving LLM agent reliability, yet current approaches treat compute as an abundant resource, allowing agents to exhaust token and tool budgets on redundant steps or dead-end trajectories. Existing budget-aware methods either require expensive fine-tuning or rely on coarse, trajectory-level heuristics that cannot intervene mid-execution. We propose the Budget-Aware Value Tree (BAVT), a training-free inference-time framework that models multi-hop reasoning as a dynamic search tree guided by step-level value estimation within a single LLM backbone. Another key innovation is a budget-conditioned node selection mechanism that uses the remaining resource ratio as a natural scaling exponent over node values, providing a principled, parameter-free transition from broad exploration to greedy exploitation as the budget depletes. To combat the well-known overconfidence of LLM self-evaluation, BAVT employs a residual value predictor that scores relative progress rather than absolute state quality, enabling reliable pruning of uninformative or redundant tool calls. We further provide a theoretical convergence guarantee, proving that BAVT reaches a terminal answer with probability at least $1-ε$ under an explicit finite budget bound. Extensive evaluations on four multi-hop QA benchmarks across two model families demonstrate that BAVT consistently outperforms parallel sampling baselines. Most notably, BAVT under strict low-budget constraints surpasses baseline performance at $4\times$ the resource allocation, establishing that intelligent budget management fundamentally outperforms brute-force compute scaling.

摘要（中文）: 测试时缩放已成为提高LLM代理可靠性的主流范式，但现有方法将计算资源视为无限供应，导致代理在冗余步骤或死胡同轨迹上耗尽token和工具预算。现有的预算感知方法要么需要昂贵的微调，要么依赖于粗略的、轨迹级别的启发式方法，无法在执行过程中进行干预。我们提出了预算感知值树（BAVT），一个无需训练的推理时框架，它将多跳推理建模为动态搜索树，该搜索树由单个LLM骨干网络内的步骤级别的值估计引导。另一项关键创新是预算条件节点选择机制，它使用剩余资源比率作为节点值的自然缩放指数，从而在预算耗尽时，提供了一种原则性的、无参数的从广泛探索到贪婪利用的过渡。为了解决LLM自我评估中众所周知的过度自信问题，BAVT采用残差值预测器，它对相对进度进行评分，而不是绝对状态质量，从而能够可靠地剪枝无信息或冗余的工具调用。我们进一步提供了理论收敛保证，证明在明确的有限预算约束下，BAVT以至少$1-ε$的概率达到最终答案。对跨越两个模型系列的四个多跳问答基准进行的大量评估表明，BAVT始终优于并行采样基线。最值得注意的是，BAVT在严格的低预算约束下，超过了资源分配为$4\times$时的基线性能，这表明智能预算管理从根本上优于蛮力计算缩放。

TLDR: The paper introduces Budget-Aware Value Tree (BAVT), a training-free inference-time framework that uses value tree search and budget-conditioned node selection to improve LLM agent reliability within a limited budget, outperforming brute-force compute scaling methods on multi-hop QA tasks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为Budget-Aware Value Tree (BAVT)的无需训练的推理时框架，它利用价值树搜索和预算条件节点选择来提高LLM代理在有限预算内的可靠性，并在多跳QA任务中优于蛮力计算扩展方法。

Authors: Yushu Li, Wenlong Deng, Jiajin Li, Xiaoxiao Li

FastDSAC: Unlocking the Potential of Maximum Entropy RL in High-Dimensional Humanoid Control

Abstract (English): Scaling Maximum Entropy Reinforcement Learning (RL) to high-dimensional humanoid control remains a formidable challenge, as the ``curse of dimensionality'' induces severe exploration inefficiency and training instability in expansive action spaces. Consequently, recent high-throughput paradigms have largely converged on deterministic policy gradients combined with massive parallel simulation. We challenge this compromise with FastDSAC, a framework that effectively unlocks the potential of maximum entropy stochastic policies for complex continuous control. We introduce Dimension-wise Entropy Modulation (DEM) to dynamically redistribute the exploration budget and enforce diversity, alongside a continuous distributional critic tailored to ensure value fidelity and mitigate high-dimensional value overestimation. Extensive evaluations on HumanoidBench and other continuous control tasks demonstrate that rigorously designed stochastic policies can consistently match or outperform deterministic baselines, achieving notable gains of 180\% and 400\% on the challenging \textit{Basketball} and \textit{Balance Hard} tasks.

摘要（中文）: 将最大熵强化学习（RL）扩展到高维人形机器人控制仍然是一项艰巨的挑战，因为“维数灾难”会在广阔的动作空间中导致严重的探索低效和训练不稳定。因此，最近的高吞吐量范式主要收敛于确定性策略梯度与大规模并行模拟相结合。我们利用FastDSAC框架挑战这种折衷方案，该框架有效地释放了最大熵随机策略用于复杂连续控制的潜力。我们引入了维度熵调制（DEM）来动态地重新分配探索预算并强制多样性，以及一个定制的连续分布critic，以确保价值保真度并减轻高维价值高估。在HumanoidBench和其他连续控制任务上的广泛评估表明，经过严格设计的随机策略能够始终如一地匹配或优于确定性基线，在具有挑战性的\textit{篮球}和\textit{平衡困难}任务上实现了180％和400％的显著收益。

TLDR: FastDSAC addresses the challenge of scaling maximum entropy RL to high-dimensional humanoid control using Dimension-wise Entropy Modulation and a continuous distributional critic, achieving significant performance gains compared to deterministic baselines in complex tasks.

简要说明: FastDSAC通过维度熵调制和连续分布评论家解决了最大熵RL在高维度人形机器人控制中的扩展难题。在复杂的任务中，与确定性基线相比，FastDSAC取得了显著的性能提升。

Authors: Jun Xue, Junze Wang, Xinming Zhang, Shanze Wang, Yanjun Chen, Wei Zhang

AgentDrift: Unsafe Recommendation Drift Under Tool Corruption Hidden by Ranking Metrics in LLM Agents

Abstract (English): Tool-augmented LLM agents increasingly serve as multi-turn advisors in high-stakes domains, yet their evaluation relies on ranking-quality metrics that measure what is recommended but not whether it is safe for the user. We introduce a paired-trajectory protocol that replays real financial dialogues under clean and contaminated tool-output conditions across seven LLMs (7B to frontier) and decomposes divergence into information-channel and memory-channel mechanisms. Across the seven models tested, we consistently observe the evaluation-blindness pattern: recommendation quality is largely preserved under contamination (utility preservation ratio approximately 1.0) while risk-inappropriate products appear in 65-93% of turns, a systematic safety failure poorly reflected by standard NDCG. Safety violations are predominantly information-channel-driven, emerge at the first contaminated turn, and persist without self-correction over 23-step trajectories; no agent across 1,563 contaminated turns explicitly questions tool-data reliability. Even narrative-only corruption (biased headlines, no numerical manipulation) induces significant drift while completely evading consistency monitors. A safety-penalized NDCG variant (sNDCG) reduces preservation ratios to 0.51-0.74, indicating that much of the evaluation gap becomes visible once safety is explicitly measured. These results motivate considering trajectory-level safety monitoring, beyond single-turn quality, for deployed multi-turn agents in high-stakes settings.

摘要（中文）: 工具增强的LLM Agent越来越多地在高风险领域担任多轮顾问，但对其评估依赖于排序质量指标，该指标衡量的是推荐内容，而不是对用户是否安全。我们引入了一种配对轨迹协议，该协议在干净和受污染的工具输出条件下，跨七个LLM（7B到前沿模型）重放真实的金融对话，并将偏差分解为信息通道和记忆通道机制。在经过测试的七个模型中，我们一致观察到评估盲区模式：推荐质量在很大程度上在污染条件下得以保持（效用保持率约为1.0），而风险不适宜的产品出现在65-93%的轮次中，这是一个标准NDCG难以反映的系统性安全故障。安全违规主要由信息通道驱动，出现在第一个受污染的回合中，并在23步轨迹中持续存在，而没有自我纠正；在1,563个受污染的回合中，没有任何Agent明确质疑工具数据的可靠性。即使是纯叙事性腐败（有偏见的新闻标题，没有数值操纵）也会导致显著的漂移，同时完全逃避一致性监控。一种安全惩罚的NDCG变体（sNDCG）将保持率降低到0.51-0.74，表明一旦明确测量安全性，大部分评估差距就会变得可见。这些结果促使在高风险环境中部署的多轮Agent，除了单轮质量之外，还应考虑轨迹级别的安全监控。

TLDR: The paper identifies a critical safety flaw in tool-augmented LLM agents used in financial advisory: recommendation quality metrics don't reflect the introduction of unsafe products due to corrupted tool outputs, potentially leading to significant safety violations without agent self-correction.

简要说明: 该论文指出，在金融咨询中使用的工具增强型LLM Agent存在严重的安全缺陷： 推荐质量指标无法反映由损坏的工具输出导致的不安全产品引入，这可能导致重大安全违规，且Agent无法自我纠正。

Authors: Zekun Wu, Adriano Koshiyama, Sahan Bulathwela, Maria Perez-Ortiz

VQQA: An Agentic Approach for Video Evaluation and Quality Improvement

Abstract (English): Despite rapid advancements in video generation models, aligning their outputs with complex user intent remains challenging. Existing test-time optimization methods are typically either computationally expensive or require white-box access to model internals. To address this, we present VQQA (Video Quality Question Answering), a unified, multi-agent framework generalizable across diverse input modalities and video generation tasks. By dynamically generating visual questions and using the resulting Vision-Language Model (VLM) critiques as semantic gradients, VQQA replaces traditional, passive evaluation metrics with human-interpretable, actionable feedback. This enables a highly efficient, closed-loop prompt optimization process via a black-box natural language interface. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VQQA effectively isolates and resolves visual artifacts, substantially improving generation quality in just a few refinement steps. Applicable to both text-to-video (T2V) and image-to-video (I2V) tasks, our method achieves absolute improvements of +11.57% on T2V-CompBench and +8.43% on VBench2 over vanilla generation, significantly outperforming state-of-the-art stochastic search and prompt optimization techniques.

摘要（中文）: 尽管视频生成模型取得了快速进展，使其输出与复杂用户意图对齐仍然具有挑战性。现有的测试时优化方法通常计算成本高昂，或者需要对模型内部进行白盒访问。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了VQQA（视频质量问答），一个统一的、多代理框架，可以推广到不同的输入模态和视频生成任务中。通过动态生成视觉问题并将由此产生的视觉-语言模型 (VLM) 的评论作为语义梯度，VQQA 使用人类可解释的、可操作的反馈代替了传统的、被动的评估指标。这通过黑盒自然语言接口实现了一个高效的闭环提示优化过程。大量实验表明，VQQA 可以有效地隔离和解决视觉伪影，在几个精炼步骤中显着提高生成质量。我们的方法适用于文本到视频 (T2V) 和图像到视频 (I2V) 任务，在 T2V-CompBench 上实现了 +11.57% 的绝对改进，在 VBench2 上实现了 +8.43% 的绝对改进，显著优于最先进的随机搜索和提示优化技术。

TLDR: The paper introduces VQQA, a multi-agent framework using Vision-Language Model critiques as semantic gradients for efficient, black-box video generation prompt optimization, demonstrating significant improvements in video quality.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了VQQA，一个多智能体框架，它使用视觉-语言模型评论作为语义梯度，用于高效的黑盒视频生成提示优化，并展示了视频质量的显著提升。

Authors: Yiwen Song, Tomas Pfister, Yale Song

Out of Sight, Out of Mind? Evaluating State Evolution in Video World Models

Abstract (English): Evolutions in the world, such as water pouring or ice melting, happen regardless of being observed. Video world models generate "worlds" via 2D frame observations. Can these generated "worlds" evolve regardless of observation? To probe this question, we design a benchmark to evaluate whether video world models can decouple state evolution from observation. Our benchmark, STEVO-Bench, applies observation control to evolving processes via instructions of occluder insertion, turning off the light, or specifying camera "lookaway" trajectories. By evaluating video models with and without camera control for a diverse set of naturally-occurring evolutions, we expose their limitations in decoupling state evolution from observation. STEVO-Bench proposes an evaluation protocol to automatically detect and disentangle failure modes of video world models across key aspects of natural state evolution. Analysis of STEVO-Bench results provide new insight into potential data and architecture bias of present-day video world models. Project website: https://glab-caltech.github.io/STEVOBench/. Blog: https://ziqi-ma.github.io/blog/2026/outofsight/

摘要（中文）: 世界上的演变，例如水流或冰融化，无论是否被观察都会发生。视频世界模型通过 2D 帧观测生成“世界”。这些生成的“世界”能否独立于观测而演变？为了探究这个问题，我们设计了一个基准来评估视频世界模型是否能将状态演变与观测解耦。我们的基准，STEVO-Bench，通过遮挡物插入、关灯或指定相机“视线移开”轨迹等指令，将观测控制应用于演变过程。通过针对各种自然发生的演变，评估具有和不具有相机控制的视频模型，我们揭示了它们在将状态演变与观测解耦方面的局限性。STEVO-Bench 提出了一个评估协议，以自动检测和解耦视频世界模型在自然状态演变的关键方面上的失效模式。对 STEVO-Bench 结果的分析为当前视频世界模型的潜在数据和架构偏见提供了新的见解。项目网站：https://glab-caltech.github.io/STEVOBench/。 博客：https://ziqi-ma.github.io/blog/2026/outofsight/

TLDR: This paper introduces STEVO-Bench, a benchmark for evaluating whether video world models can decouple state evolution from observation by testing their ability to maintain realistic world states even when occluded or unobserved.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个名为STEVO-Bench的基准测试，用于评估视频世界模型是否能够将状态演变与观察分离，通过测试它们在被遮挡或未被观察时维持真实世界状态的能力。

Authors: Ziqi Ma, Mengzhan Liufu, Georgia Gkioxari

Towards Spatio-Temporal World Scene Graph Generation from Monocular Videos

Abstract (English): Spatio-temporal scene graphs provide a principled representation for modeling evolving object interactions, yet existing methods remain fundamentally frame-centric: they reason only about currently visible objects, discard entities upon occlusion, and operate in 2D. To address this, we first introduce ActionGenome4D, a dataset that upgrades Action Genome videos into 4D scenes via feed-forward 3D reconstruction, world-frame oriented bounding boxes for every object involved in actions, and dense relationship annotations including for objects that are temporarily unobserved due to occlusion or camera motion. Building on this data, we formalize World Scene Graph Generation (WSGG), the task of constructing a world scene graph at each timestamp that encompasses all interacting objects in the scene, both observed and unobserved. We then propose three complementary methods, each exploring a different inductive bias for reasoning about unobserved objects: PWG (Persistent World Graph), which implements object permanence via a zero-order feature buffer; MWAE (Masked World Auto-Encoder), which reframes unobserved-object reasoning as masked completion with cross-view associative retrieval; and 4DST (4D Scene Transformer), which replaces the static buffer with differentiable per-object temporal attention enriched by 3D motion and camera-pose features. We further design and evaluate the performance of strong open-source Vision-Language Models on the WSGG task via a suite of Graph RAG-based approaches, establishing baselines for unlocalized relationship prediction. WSGG thus advances video scene understanding toward world-centric, temporally persistent, and interpretable scene reasoning.

摘要（中文）: 时空场景图为建模演化的物体交互提供了一种原则性的表示方法，但现有方法在本质上仍然以帧为中心：它们仅对当前可见的物体进行推理，遮挡后即丢弃实体，并在2D空间中运行。为了解决这个问题，我们首先引入ActionGenome4D，该数据集通过前馈3D重建，将Action Genome视频升级为4D场景，为参与动作的每个物体提供世界坐标系下的包围盒，并提供密集的关联关系标注，包括因遮挡或相机运动而暂时无法观察到的物体。在此数据的基础上，我们形式化了世界场景图生成（WSGG）任务，即在每个时间戳构建一个世界场景图，其中包含场景中所有交互的物体，无论是观察到的还是未观察到的。然后，我们提出了三种互补的方法，每种方法都探索了不同的归纳偏置来推理未观察到的物体：PWG（持久世界图），它通过零阶特征缓冲区实现物体的永久性；MWAE（掩码世界自编码器），它将未观察到的物体推理重新定义为具有跨视角关联检索的掩码补全；以及4DST（4D场景Transformer），它用可微分的基于物体的时序注意力替换了静态缓冲区，该注意力通过3D运动和相机姿态特征进行丰富。我们进一步设计和评估了强大的开源视觉-语言模型在WSGG任务上的性能，通过一套基于图RAG的方法，建立了非定位关联关系预测的基线。因此，WSGG将视频场景理解提升到以世界为中心、时间上持久且可解释的场景推理。

TLDR: This paper introduces ActionGenome4D, a dataset for spatio-temporal scene graph generation from monocular videos, and proposes three methods (PWG, MWAE, and 4DST) for reasoning about unobserved objects, along with baselines using Graph RAG-based Vision-Language Models.

简要说明: 本文介绍了ActionGenome4D，一个用于单目视频时空场景图生成的数据集。提出了三种方法（PWG、MWAE和4DST），用于推理未观察到的对象。同时，使用基于图RAG的视觉-语言模型建立了基线。

Authors: Rohith Peddi, Saurabh, Shravan Shanmugam, Likhitha Pallapothula, Yu Xiang, Parag Singla, Vibhav Gogate

Reasoning over Video: Evaluating How MLLMs Extract, Integrate, and Reconstruct Spatiotemporal Evidence

Abstract (English): The growing interest in embodied agents increases the demand for spatiotemporal video understanding, yet existing benchmarks largely emphasize extractive reasoning, where answers can be explicitly presented within spatiotemporal events. It remains unclear whether multimodal large language models can instead perform abstractive spatiotemporal reasoning, which requires integrating observations over time, combining dispersed cues, and inferring implicit spatial and contextual structure. To address this gap, we formalize abstractive spatiotemporal reasoning from videos by introducing a structured evaluation taxonomy that systematically targets its core dimensions and construct a controllable, scenario-driven synthetic egocentric video dataset tailored to evaluate abstractive spatiotemporal reasoning capabilities, spanning object-, room-, and floor-plan-level scenarios. Based on this framework, we present VAEX-BENCH, a benchmark comprising five abstractive reasoning tasks together with their extractive counterparts. Our extensive experiments compare the performance of state-of-the-art MLLMs under extractive and abstractive settings, exposing their limitations on abstractive tasks and providing a fine-grained analysis of the underlying bottlenecks. The dataset will be released soon.

摘要（中文）: 对具身智能体日益增长的兴趣提高了社会对时空视频理解的需求，然而现有的基准测试主要强调抽取式推理，即答案可以明确地呈现在时空事件中。多模态大型语言模型是否能执行抽象时空推理仍然不清楚，这种推理需要整合随时间的观察结果，组合分散的线索，并推断隐含的空间和上下文结构。为了解决这个差距，我们通过引入一个系统地针对其核心维度的结构化评估分类法，形式化了视频中的抽象时空推理，并构建了一个可控的、场景驱动的合成第一人称视角视频数据集，该数据集专门用于评估抽象时空推理能力，涵盖物体、房间和楼层平面图级别的场景。基于这个框架，我们提出了VAEX-BENCH，一个包含五个抽象推理任务及其对应的抽取式推理任务的基准测试。我们广泛的实验比较了最先进的MLLM在抽取式和抽象式设置下的性能，揭示了它们在抽象任务上的局限性，并对潜在的瓶颈进行了细粒度的分析。该数据集即将发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces VAEX-BENCH, a new benchmark to evaluate the abstractive spatiotemporal reasoning capabilities of MLLMs on egocentric videos, revealing limitations not captured by existing extractive reasoning benchmarks.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了VAEX-BENCH，一个新的基准测试，用于评估多模态大型语言模型在以自我为中心的视频中进行抽象时空推理的能力，揭示了现有提取式推理基准测试无法捕捉到的局限性。

Authors: Seunghwan Bang, Hwanjun Song

Topo-R1: Detecting Topological Anomalies via Vision-Language Models

Abstract (English): Topological correctness is crucial for tubular structures such as blood vessels, nerve fibers, and road networks. Existing topology-preserving methods rely on domain-specific ground truth, which is costly and rarely transfers across domains. When deployed to a new domain without annotations, a key question arises: how can we detect topological anomalies without ground-truth supervision? We reframe this as topological anomaly detection, a structured visual reasoning task requiring a model to locate and classify topological errors in predicted segmentation masks. Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are natural candidates; however, we find that state-of-the-art VLMs perform nearly at random, lacking the fine-grained, topology-aware perception needed to identify sparse connectivity errors in dense structures. To bridge this gap, we develop an automated data-curation pipeline that synthesizes diverse topological anomalies with verifiable annotations across progressively difficult levels, thereby constructing the first large-scale, multi-domain benchmark for this task. We then introduce Topo-R1, a framework that endows VLMs with topology-aware perception via two-stage training: supervised fine-tuning followed by reinforcement learning with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Central to our approach is a topology-aware composite reward that integrates type-aware Hungarian matching for structured error classification, spatial localization scoring, and a centerline Dice (clDice) reward that directly penalizes connectivity disruptions, thereby jointly incentivizing semantic precision and structural fidelity. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Topo-R1 establishes a new paradigm for annotation-free topological quality assessment, consistently outperforming general-purpose VLMs and supervised baselines across all evaluation protocols.

摘要（中文）: 拓扑结构的正确性对于诸如血管、神经纤维和道路网络等管状结构至关重要。现有的拓扑保持方法依赖于领域特定的真值，这既昂贵又很少能跨领域迁移。当部署到没有标注的新领域时，一个关键问题出现了：如何在没有真值监督的情况下检测拓扑异常？我们将此重新定义为拓扑异常检测，这是一个结构化视觉推理任务，要求模型定位并分类预测分割掩码中的拓扑错误。视觉-语言模型(VLMs)是自然的候选者；然而，我们发现最先进的VLMs表现几乎是随机的，缺乏识别密集结构中稀疏连接错误所需的细粒度、拓扑感知的能力。为了弥合这一差距，我们开发了一个自动数据管理流程，该流程合成了具有可验证标注的各种拓扑异常，并逐步提高难度等级，从而构建了第一个大规模、多领域的此任务基准。然后，我们引入了Topo-R1，这是一个通过两阶段训练赋予VLMs拓扑感知能力的框架：有监督微调，然后是使用组相对策略优化(GRPO)的强化学习。我们方法的核心是一个拓扑感知的复合奖励，它集成了用于结构化误差分类的类型感知匈牙利匹配、空间定位评分和一个直接惩罚连通性中断的中心线Dice(clDice)奖励，从而共同激励语义精度和结构保真度。大量实验表明，Topo-R1为无标注拓扑质量评估建立了一个新范例，始终优于通用VLMs和跨所有评估协议的有监督基线模型。

TLDR: This paper introduces Topo-R1, a framework that improves Vision-Language Models' (VLMs) ability to detect topological anomalies in tubular structures by using an automated data-curation pipeline and a two-stage training process with reinforcement learning and a topology-aware reward function.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Topo-R1，一个通过自动数据管理流程，以及两阶段训练过程（使用强化学习和拓扑感知奖励函数）来提高视觉-语言模型（VLMs）检测管状结构中拓扑异常能力的框架。

Authors: Meilong Xu, Qingqiao Hu, Xiaoling Hu, Shahira Abousamra, Xin Yu, Weimin Lyu, Kehan Qi, Dimitris Samaras, Chao Chen

Test-Time Attention Purification for Backdoored Large Vision Language Models

Abstract (English): Despite the strong multimodal performance, large vision-language models (LVLMs) are vulnerable during fine-tuning to backdoor attacks, where adversaries insert trigger-embedded samples into the training data to implant behaviors that can be maliciously activated at test time. Existing defenses typically rely on retraining backdoored parameters (e.g., adapters or LoRA modules) with clean data, which is computationally expensive and often degrades model performance. In this work, we provide a new mechanistic understanding of backdoor behaviors in LVLMs: the trigger does not influence prediction through low-level visual patterns, but through abnormal cross-modal attention redistribution, where trigger-bearing visual tokens steal attention away from the textual context - a phenomenon we term attention stealing. Motivated by this, we propose CleanSight, a training-free, plug-and-play defense that operates purely at test time. CleanSight (i) detects poisoned inputs based on the relative visual-text attention ratio in selected cross-modal fusion layers, and (ii) purifies the input by selectively pruning the suspicious high-attention visual tokens to neutralize the backdoor activation. Extensive experiments show that CleanSight significantly outperforms existing pixel-based purification defenses across diverse datasets and backdoor attack types, while preserving the model's utility on both clean and poisoned samples.

摘要（中文）: 尽管大型视觉语言模型(LVLMs)具有强大的多模态性能，但在微调过程中容易受到后门攻击。攻击者将嵌入触发器的样本插入到训练数据中，植入可在测试时恶意激活的行为。现有的防御措施通常依赖于使用干净数据重新训练被植入后门的参数（例如，适配器或LoRA模块），这计算成本高昂且常常会降低模型性能。在这项工作中，我们对LVLMs中后门行为提供了一种新的机制性理解：触发器并不通过低级视觉模式影响预测，而是通过异常的跨模态注意力重新分配，即携带触发器的视觉tokens从文本上下文中窃取注意力——我们称之为注意力窃取现象。受此启发，我们提出了CleanSight，一种无需训练、即插即用的防御方法，它完全在测试时运行。CleanSight (i)基于选定的跨模态融合层中的视觉-文本相对注意力比率来检测受污染的输入，并且(ii)通过选择性地剪枝可疑的高注意力视觉tokens来净化输入，从而中和后门激活。大量的实验表明，CleanSight在各种数据集和后门攻击类型中都明显优于现有的基于像素的净化防御方法，同时保持了模型在干净和受污染样本上的效用。

TLDR: The paper proposes CleanSight, a training-free defense against backdoor attacks in LVLMs that identifies and neutralizes poisoned inputs by pruning suspicious visual tokens based on abnormal cross-modal attention redistribution.

简要说明: 该论文提出CleanSight，一种无需训练的防御LVLM中后门攻击的方法。通过识别和中和可疑的视觉token，基于异常的跨模态注意力重新分配，来检测并对抗被污染的输入。

Authors: Zhifang Zhang, Bojun Yang, Shuo He, Weitong Chen, Wei Emma Zhang, Olaf Maennel, Lei Feng, Miao Xu

Composing Driving Worlds through Disentangled Control for Adversarial Scenario Generation

Abstract (English): A major challenge in autonomous driving is the "long tail" of safety-critical edge cases, which often emerge from unusual combinations of common traffic elements. Synthesizing these scenarios is crucial, yet current controllable generative models provide incomplete or entangled guidance, preventing the independent manipulation of scene structure, object identity, and ego actions. We introduce CompoSIA, a compositional driving video simulator that disentangles these traffic factors, enabling fine-grained control over diverse adversarial driving scenarios. To support controllable identity replacement of scene elements, we propose a noise-level identity injection, allowing pose-agnostic identity generation across diverse element poses, all from a single reference image. Furthermore, a hierarchical dual-branch action control mechanism is introduced to improve action controllability. Such disentangled control enables adversarial scenario synthesis-systematically combining safe elements into dangerous configurations that entangled generators cannot produce. Extensive comparisons demonstrate superior controllable generation quality over state-of-the-art baselines, with a 17% improvement in FVD for identity editing and reductions of 30% and 47% in rotation and translation errors for action control. Furthermore, downstream stress-testing reveals substantial planner failures: across editing modalities, the average collision rate of 3s increases by 173%.

摘要（中文）: 自动驾驶领域的一个主要挑战是安全攸关的“长尾”边缘案例，这些案例通常源于常见交通要素的异常组合。合成这些场景至关重要，然而，当前可控生成模型提供的引导不完整或存在纠缠，阻碍了对场景结构、物体身份和自车行为的独立操控。我们引入了CompoSIA，一种组合式驾驶视频模拟器，它解耦了这些交通因素，从而能够对各种对抗性驾驶场景进行细粒度控制。为了支持场景元素的可控身份替换，我们提出了一种噪声水平身份注入方法，从而允许基于单个参考图像，跨越不同的元素姿态进行与姿态无关的身份生成。此外，我们引入了一种分层双分支行为控制机制，以提高行为可控性。这种解耦控制能够实现对抗性场景合成——系统性地将安全要素组合成纠缠生成器无法产生的危险配置。广泛的比较表明，在可控生成质量上优于最先进的基线，在身份编辑的FVD指标上提升了17%，在行为控制的旋转和位移误差上分别降低了30%和47%。此外，下游压力测试揭示了显著的规划器故障：在各种编辑模式下，3秒的平均碰撞率增加了173%。

TLDR: The paper introduces CompoSIA, a compositional driving video simulator with disentangled control over scene structure, object identity, and ego actions, designed for generating adversarial driving scenarios and improving autonomous driving safety testing.

Authors: Yifan Zhan, Zhengqing Chen, Qingjie Wang, Zhuo He, Muyao Niu, Xiaoyang Guo, Wei Yin, Weiqiang Ren, Qian Zhang, Yinqiang Zheng

Adaptive Vision-Language Model Routing for Computer Use Agents

Abstract (English): Computer Use Agents (CUAs) translate natural-language instructions into Graphical User Interface (GUI) actions such as clicks, keystrokes, and scrolls by relying on a Vision-Language Model (VLM) to interpret screenshots and predict grounded tool calls. However, grounding accuracy varies dramatically across VLMs, while current CUA systems typically route every action to a single fixed model regardless of difficulty. We propose \textbf{Adaptive VLM Routing} (AVR), a framework that inserts a lightweight semantic routing layer between the CUA orchestrator and a pool of VLMs. For each tool call, AVR estimates action difficulty from multimodal embeddings, probes a small VLM to measure confidence, and routes the action to the cheapest model whose predicted accuracy satisfies a target reliability threshold. For \textit{warm} agents with memory of prior UI interactions, retrieved context further narrows the capability gap between small and large models, allowing many actions to be handled without escalation. We formalize routing as a cost--accuracy trade-off, derive a threshold-based policy for model selection, and evaluate AVR using ScreenSpot-Pro grounding data together with the OpenClaw agent routing benchmark. Across these settings, AVR projects inference cost reductions of up to 78\% while staying within 2 percentage points of an all-large-model baseline. When combined with the Visual Confused Deputy guardrail, AVR also escalates high-risk actions directly to the strongest available model, unifying efficiency and safety within a single routing framework. Materials are also provided Model, benchmark, and code: https://github.com/vllm-project/semantic-router.

摘要（中文）: 计算机使用代理（CUAs）依赖视觉-语言模型（VLM）来解释屏幕截图并预测基于内容的工具调用，从而将自然语言指令翻译成图形用户界面（GUI）动作，例如点击、按键和滚动。然而，不同VLM之间的内容定位准确率差异巨大，而当前的CUA系统通常将每个动作都路由到单个固定模型，而不考虑其难易程度。我们提出了\textbf{自适应VLM路由}（AVR），该框架在CUA编排器和VLM池之间插入一个轻量级的语义路由层。对于每个工具调用，AVR从多模态嵌入中估计动作难度，探测一个小型VLM以衡量置信度，并将动作路由到成本最低且预测准确率满足目标可靠性阈值的模型。对于具有先前UI交互记忆的\textit{热} 代理，检索到的上下文进一步缩小了小型模型和大型模型之间的能力差距，从而允许在无需升级的情况下处理许多动作。我们将路由形式化为成本-准确率的权衡，推导出基于阈值的模型选择策略，并使用ScreenSpot-Pro内容定位数据以及OpenClaw代理路由基准对AVR进行评估。在这些设置中，AVR预测推理成本降低高达78\%，同时保持在全大型模型基线的2个百分点以内。当与Visual Confused Deputy护栏结合使用时，AVR还将高风险动作直接升级到最强大的可用模型，从而在一个单一的路由框架内统一了效率和安全性。代码、模型和基准测试材料已提供：https://github.com/vllm-project/semantic-router。

TLDR: This paper introduces Adaptive VLM Routing (AVR), a framework for Computer Use Agents that intelligently routes GUI actions to different VLMs based on difficulty and risk, achieving significant cost reductions with minimal accuracy loss.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种自适应 VLM 路由 (AVR) 框架，用于计算机使用代理，该框架能够根据难度和风险智能地将 GUI 操作路由到不同的 VLM，从而在极小精度损失的情况下实现显著的成本降低。

Authors: Xunzhuo Liu, Bowei He, Xue Liu, Andy Luo, Haichen Zhang, Huamin Chen

Generalized Recognition of Basic Surgical Actions Enables Skill Assessment and Vision-Language-Model-based Surgical Planning

Abstract (English): Artificial intelligence, imaging, and large language models have the potential to transform surgical practice, training, and automation. Understanding and modeling of basic surgical actions (BSA), the fundamental unit of operation in any surgery, is important to drive the evolution of this field. In this paper, we present a BSA dataset comprising 10 basic actions across 6 surgical specialties with over 11,000 video clips, which is the largest to date. Based on the BSA dataset, we developed a new foundation model that conducts general-purpose recognition of basic actions. Our approach demonstrates robust cross-specialist performance in experiments validated on datasets from different procedural types and various body parts. Furthermore, we demonstrate downstream applications enabled by the BAS foundation model through surgical skill assessment in prostatectomy using domain-specific knowledge, and action planning in cholecystectomy and nephrectomy using large vision-language models. Multinational surgeons' evaluation of the language model's output of the action planning explainable texts demonstrated clinical relevance. These findings indicate that basic surgical actions can be robustly recognized across scenarios, and an accurate BSA understanding model can essentially facilitate complex applications and speed up the realization of surgical superintelligence.

摘要（中文）: 人工智能、影像技术和大型语言模型具有变革外科实践、培训和自动化的潜力。理解和建模基本外科动作（BSA），即任何外科手术中的基本操作单元，对于推动该领域的发展至关重要。在本文中，我们提出了一个BSA数据集，囊括6个外科专业的10种基本动作，包含超过11,000个视频片段，是目前为止最大的数据集。基于BSA数据集，我们开发了一个新的基础模型，用于进行通用目的的基本动作识别。我们的方法在经过不同手术类型和各种身体部位数据集验证的实验中，展示了强大的跨专业性能。此外，我们通过在根治性前列腺切除术中使用领域特定知识进行外科技能评估，以及在胆囊切除术和肾切除术中使用大型视觉语言模型进行动作规划，来展示由BSA基础模型实现的下游应用。多国外科医生对语言模型的动作规划可解释文本输出的评估证明了其临床相关性。这些发现表明，基本外科动作可以在各种场景中得到稳健的识别，而一个精确的BSA理解模型可以从根本上促进复杂应用，并加速外科超智能的实现。

Thinking in Dynamics: How Multimodal Large Language Models Perceive, Track, and Reason Dynamics in Physical 4D World

Abstract (English): Humans inhabit a physical 4D world where geometric structure and semantic content evolve over time, constituting a dynamic 4D reality (spatial with temporal dimension). While current Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) excel in static visual understanding, can they also be adept at "thinking in dynamics", i.e., perceive, track and reason about spatio-temporal dynamics in evolving scenes? To systematically assess their spatio-temporal reasoning and localized dynamics perception capabilities, we introduce Dyn-Bench, a large-scale benchmark built from diverse real-world and synthetic video datasets, enabling robust and scalable evaluation of spatio-temporal understanding. Through multi-stage filtering from massive 2D and 4D data sources, Dyn-Bench provides a high-quality collection of dynamic scenes, comprising 1k videos, 7k visual question answering (VQA) pairs, and 3k dynamic object grounding pairs. We probe general, spatial and region-level MLLMs to express how they think in dynamics both linguistically and visually, and find that existing models cannot simultaneously maintain strong performance in both spatio-temporal reasoning and dynamic object grounding, often producing inconsistent interpretations of motion and interaction. Notably, conventional prompting strategies (e.g., chain-of-thought or caption-based hints) provide limited improvement, whereas structured integration approaches, including Mask-Guided Fusion and Spatio-Temporal Textual Cognitive Map (ST-TCM), significantly enhance MLLMs' dynamics perception and spatio-temporal reasoning in the physical 4D world. Code and benchmark are available at https://dyn-bench.github.io/.

摘要（中文）: 人类居住在一个物理的四维世界中，其中几何结构和语义内容随时间演变，构成了动态的四维现实（空间维度加上时间维度）。虽然目前的多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）在静态视觉理解方面表现出色，但它们也能擅长“动态思考”吗？即感知、追踪和推理演变场景中的时空动态？为了系统地评估其时空推理和局部动态感知能力，我们引入了Dyn-Bench，一个基于各种真实世界和合成视频数据集构建的大规模基准，能够对时空理解进行稳健且可扩展的评估。通过对海量二维和四维数据源进行多阶段过滤，Dyn-Bench提供了高质量的动态场景集合，包括1000个视频、7000个视觉问答（VQA）对和3000个动态对象定位对。我们探测了通用、空间和区域级的多模态大型语言模型，以阐述它们如何用语言和视觉方式进行动态思考，并发现现有模型无法同时保持在时空推理和动态对象定位方面的强大性能，常常对运动和交互产生不一致的解释。值得注意的是，传统的提示策略（例如，思维链或基于标题的提示）提供的改进有限，而结构化集成方法，包括掩码引导融合和时空文本认知地图（ST-TCM），显著增强了多模态大型语言模型在物理四维世界中的动态感知和时空推理能力。代码和基准可在https://dyn-bench.github.io/获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces Dyn-Bench, a new benchmark to evaluate the ability of MLLMs to perceive, track, and reason about spatio-temporal dynamics in 4D physical environments, revealing limitations in current models and proposing structured integration approaches to improve performance.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Dyn-Bench，一个新的基准测试，用于评估MLLM在4D物理环境中感知、跟踪和推理时空动态的能力，揭示了当前模型的局限，并提出了结构化的集成方法来提高性能。

Authors: Yuzhi Huang, Kairun Wen, Rongxin Gao, Dongxuan Liu, Yibin Lou, Jie Wu, Jing Xu, Jian Zhang, Zheng Yang, Yunlong Lin, Chenxin Li, Panwang Pan, Junbin Lu, Jingyan Jiang, Xinghao Ding, Yue Huang, Zhi Wang

AVION: Aerial Vision-Language Instruction from Offline Teacher to Prompt-Tuned Network

Abstract (English): Adapting vision-language models to remote sensing imagery remains challenging due to two key factors: limited semantic coverage in textual representations and insufficient adaptability of visual features. These issues are particularly significant in aerial scenes, which involve various visual appearances and fine-grained object distinctions. We propose AVION, a knowledge distillation framework tailored for remote sensing adaptation of vision-language models. The teacher module constructs semantically rich textual prototypes by collecting descriptions from a large language model and verifying validity using remote sensing image features. The student module integrates lightweight and learnable prompts into both vision and language encoders, guided by the teacher to align embeddings and their cross-modal relationships. Once trained, the student operates independently during inference. Experiments on six optical remote sensing benchmarks show that AVION improves few-shot classification and base-class accuracy without degrading generalization to novel categories. It also enhances mean recall for cross-modal retrieval, with minimal additional trainable parameters.

摘要（中文）: 将视觉-语言模型适配到遥感影像仍然具有挑战性，原因在于两个关键因素：文本表示中语义覆盖范围有限以及视觉特征的适应性不足。这些问题在高空场景中尤为突出，因为高空场景涉及各种视觉外观和细粒度的物体区分。我们提出了AVION，这是一种为视觉-语言模型遥感适配定制的知识蒸馏框架。教师模块通过从大型语言模型收集描述并使用遥感图像特征验证有效性来构建语义丰富的文本原型。学生模块将轻量级且可学习的提示集成到视觉和语言编码器中，由教师引导以对齐嵌入及其跨模态关系。训练完成后，学生在推理期间独立运行。在六个光学遥感基准上的实验表明，AVION在不降低对新类别泛化能力的前提下，提高了少样本分类和基类准确率。它还在最小化可训练参数的情况下，增强了跨模态检索的平均召回率。

TLDR: The paper introduces AVION, a knowledge distillation framework for adapting vision-language models to remote sensing imagery by using a teacher module (LLM-generated textual prototypes) and a student module (prompt-tuned network), which improves few-shot classification and cross-modal retrieval with minimal parameters.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种名为AVION的知识蒸馏框架，通过使用教师模块（LLM生成的文本原型）和学生模块（提示调优的网络）将视觉-语言模型适应于遥感图像处理，从而在少量参数下提高了少样本分类和跨模态检索的性能。

Authors: Yu Hu, Jianyang Gu, Hao Liu, Yue Cao, Jozsef Hamari, Zheng Liu, Mohsen Zardadi

Do You See What I Am Pointing At? Gesture-Based Egocentric Video Question Answering

Abstract (English): Understanding and answering questions based on a user's pointing gesture is essential for next-generation egocentric AI assistants. However, current Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) struggle with such tasks due to the lack of gesture-rich data and their limited ability to infer fine-grained pointing intent from egocentric video. To address this, we introduce EgoPointVQA, a dataset and benchmark for gesture-grounded egocentric question answering, comprising 4000 synthetic and 400 real-world videos across multiple deictic reasoning tasks. Built upon it, we further propose Hand Intent Tokens (HINT), which encodes tokens derived from 3D hand keypoints using an off-the-shelf reconstruction model and interleaves them with the model input to provide explicit spatial and temporal context for interpreting pointing intent. We show that our model outperforms others in different backbones and model sizes. In particular, HINT-14B achieves 68.1% accuracy, on average over 6 tasks, surpassing the state-of-the-art, InternVL3-14B, by 6.6%. To further facilitate the open research, we will release the code, model, and dataset. Project page: https://yuuraa.github.io/papers/choi2026egovqa

摘要（中文）: 基于用户指向手势理解和回答问题对于下一代以自我为中心的AI助手至关重要。然而，当前的多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）在这类任务中表现不佳，原因是缺乏富含手势的数据以及它们从以自我为中心的视频中推断细粒度指向意图的能力有限。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了EgoPointVQA，一个用于手势定位的以自我为中心视觉问答的数据集和基准，包含4000个合成视频和400个真实世界视频，涵盖多个指示推理任务。在此基础上，我们进一步提出了手部意图令牌（HINT），它使用现成的重建模型编码从3D手部关键点导出的令牌，并将其与模型输入交错排列，从而为解释指向意图提供明确的空间和时间上下文。我们表明，我们的模型在不同的骨干网络和模型大小中都优于其他模型。 特别是，HINT-14B在6个任务上的平均准确率达到68.1%，超越了最先进的InternVL3-14B，提升了6.6%。为了进一步促进开放研究，我们将发布代码、模型和数据集。项目页面：https://yuuraa.github.io/papers/choi2026egovqa

Authors: Yura Choi, Roy Miles, Rolandos Alexandros Potamias, Ismail Elezi, Jiankang Deng, Stefanos Zafeiriou

Surg-R1: A Hierarchical Reasoning Foundation Model for Scalable and Interpretable Surgical Decision Support with Multi-Center Clinical Validation

Abstract (English): Surgical scene understanding demands not only accurate predictions but also interpretable reasoning that surgeons can verify against clinical expertise. However, existing surgical vision-language models generate predictions without reasoning chains, and general-purpose reasoning models fail on compositional surgical tasks without domain-specific knowledge. We present Surg-R1, a surgical Vision-Language Model that addresses this gap through hierarchical reasoning trained via a four-stage pipeline. Our approach introduces three key contributions: (1) a three-level reasoning hierarchy decomposing surgical interpretation into perceptual grounding, relational understanding, and contextual reasoning; (2) the largest surgical chain-of-thought dataset with 320,000 reasoning pairs; and (3) a four-stage training pipeline progressing from supervised fine-tuning to group relative policy optimization and iterative self-improvement. Evaluation on SurgBench, comprising six public benchmarks and six multi-center external validation datasets from five institutions, demonstrates that Surg-R1 achieves the highest Arena Score (64.9%) on public benchmarks versus Gemini 3.0 Pro (46.1%) and GPT-5.1 (37.9%), outperforming both proprietary reasoning models and specialized surgical VLMs on the majority of tasks spanning instrument localization, triplet recognition, phase recognition, action recognition, and critical view of safety assessment, with a 15.2 percentage point improvement over the strongest surgical baseline on external validation.

摘要（中文）: 手术场景理解不仅需要精确的预测，还需要外科医生能够根据临床经验验证的可解释的推理。然而，现有的手术视觉-语言模型在生成预测时缺乏推理链，而通用推理模型在没有领域特定知识的情况下，难以处理组合式手术任务。我们提出了Surg-R1，一种手术视觉-语言模型，通过四阶段流程训练的分层推理来弥补这一差距。我们的方法引入了三个关键贡献：（1）一个三级推理层级，将手术解释分解为感知基础、关系理解和情景推理；（2）最大的手术思维链数据集，包含32万个推理对；（3）一个四阶段训练流程，从监督微调，到群体相对策略优化，再到迭代自提升。在SurgBench上的评估（包括六个公共基准和一个来自五个机构的六中心外部验证数据集）表明，Surg-R1在公共基准上获得了最高的Arena Score（64.9%），而Gemini 3.0 Pro为46.1%，GPT-5.1为37.9%，在仪器定位、三元组识别、阶段识别、动作识别和安全视野评估等大多数任务上，优于专有推理模型和专业手术VLM，并且在外部验证中比最强的手术基线提高了15.2个百分点。

TLDR: Surg-R1 is a surgical vision-language model with a hierarchical reasoning approach and a large, domain-specific chain-of-thought dataset, achieving state-of-the-art results on various surgical tasks.

Authors: Jian Jiang, Chenxi Lin, Yiming Gu, Zengyi Qin, Zhitao Zeng, Kun Yuan, Yonghao Long, Xiang Xia, Cheng Yuan, Yuqi Wang, Zijie Yue, Kunyi Yang, Yuting Zhang, Zhu Zhuo, Dian Qin, Xin Wang, NG Chi Fai, Brian Anthony, Daguang Xu, Guy Rosman, Ozanan Meireles, Zizhen Zhang, Nicolas Padoy, Hesheng Wang, Qi Dou, Yueming Jin, Yutong Ban

A Neuro-Symbolic Framework Combining Inductive and Deductive Reasoning for Autonomous Driving Planning

Abstract (English): Existing end-to-end autonomous driving models rely heavily on purely data-driven inductive reasoning. This "black-box" nature leads to a lack of interpretability and absolute safety guarantees in complex, long-tail scenarios. To overcome this bottleneck, we propose a novel neuro-symbolic trajectory planning framework that seamlessly integrates rigorous deductive reasoning into end-to-end neural networks. Specifically, our framework utilizes a Large Language Model (LLM) to dynamically extract scene rules and employs an Answer Set Programming (ASP) solver for deterministic logical arbitration, generating safe and traceable discrete driving decisions. To bridge the gap between discrete symbols and continuous trajectories, we introduce a decision-conditioned decoding mechanism that transforms high-level logical decisions into learnable embedding vectors, simultaneously constraining the planning query and the physical initial velocity of a differentiable Kinematic Bicycle Model (KBM). By combining KBM-generated physical baseline trajectories with neural residual corrections, our approach inherently guarantees kinematic feasibility while ensuring a high degree of transparency. On the nuScenes benchmark, our method comprehensively outperforms the state-of-the-art baseline MomAD, reducing the L2 mean error to 0.57 m, decreasing the collision rate to 0.075%, and optimizing trajectory prediction consistency (TPC) to 0.47 m.

摘要（中文）: 现有的端到端自动驾驶模型严重依赖纯粹的数据驱动式归纳推理。这种“黑盒”特性导致在复杂、长尾场景中缺乏可解释性和绝对安全保障。为了克服这一瓶颈，我们提出了一种新颖的神经符号轨迹规划框架，该框架将严谨的演绎推理无缝集成到端到端神经网络中。具体而言，我们的框架利用大型语言模型 (LLM) 动态提取场景规则，并采用答案集编程 (ASP) 求解器进行确定性逻辑仲裁，从而生成安全且可追溯的离散驾驶决策。为了弥合离散符号和连续轨迹之间的差距，我们引入了一种决策条件解码机制，将高级逻辑决策转化为可学习的嵌入向量，同时约束规划查询和可微运动学自行车模型 (KBM) 的物理初始速度。通过将 KBM 生成的物理基线轨迹与神经残差校正相结合，我们的方法在本质上保证了运动学可行性，同时确保了高度的透明性。在 nuScenes 基准测试中，我们的方法全面优于最先进的基线 MomAD，将 L2 平均误差降低至 0.57 米，将碰撞率降低至 0.075%，并将轨迹预测一致性 (TPC) 优化至 0.47 米。

TLDR: This paper introduces a neuro-symbolic autonomous driving planning framework that integrates LLMs for scene rule extraction and ASP solvers for logical arbitration, enhancing safety and interpretability compared to end-to-end models, and demonstrates improved performance on the nuScenes benchmark.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种神经符号自动驾驶规划框架，结合了LLM用于场景规则提取和ASP求解器用于逻辑仲裁，与端到端模型相比，提高了安全性和可解释性，并在nuScenes benchmark上展示了改进的性能。

Authors: Hongyan Wei, Wael AbdAlmageed

PISmith: Reinforcement Learning-based Red Teaming for Prompt Injection Defenses

Abstract (English): Prompt injection poses serious security risks to real-world LLM applications, particularly autonomous agents. Although many defenses have been proposed, their robustness against adaptive attacks remains insufficiently evaluated, potentially creating a false sense of security. In this work, we propose PISmith, a reinforcement learning (RL)-based red-teaming framework that systematically assesses existing prompt-injection defenses by training an attack LLM to optimize injected prompts in a practical black-box setting, where the attacker can only query the defended LLM and observe its outputs. We find that directly applying standard GRPO to attack strong defenses leads to sub-optimal performance due to extreme reward sparsity -- most generated injected prompts are blocked by the defense, causing the policy's entropy to collapse before discovering effective attack strategies, while the rare successes cannot be learned effectively. In response, we introduce adaptive entropy regularization and dynamic advantage weighting to sustain exploration and amplify learning from scarce successes. Extensive evaluation on 13 benchmarks demonstrates that state-of-the-art prompt injection defenses remain vulnerable to adaptive attacks. We also compare PISmith with 7 baselines across static, search-based, and RL-based attack categories, showing that PISmith consistently achieves the highest attack success rates. Furthermore, PISmith achieves strong performance in agentic settings on InjecAgent and AgentDojo against both open-source and closed-source LLMs (e.g., GPT-4o-mini and GPT-5-nano). Our code is available at https://github.com/albert-y1n/PISmith.

摘要（中文）: 提示注入对现实世界中的LLM应用，特别是自主代理，构成了严重的安全风险。虽然已经提出了许多防御措施，但它们对抗自适应攻击的鲁棒性仍未得到充分评估，这可能会产生一种虚假的安全感。在这项工作中，我们提出了PISmith，一个基于强化学习（RL）的红队框架，通过训练一个攻击LLM来优化注入的提示，从而在实际的黑盒设置中系统地评估现有的提示注入防御措施。在这种设置中，攻击者只能查询受防御的LLM并观察其输出。我们发现，直接应用标准GRPO来攻击强防御措施会导致次优性能，这是由于极端的奖励稀疏性——大多数生成的注入提示会被防御措施阻止，导致策略的熵在发现有效的攻击策略之前就崩溃，而罕见的成功也无法有效地学习。作为回应，我们引入了自适应熵正则化和动态优势加权，以维持探索并放大从稀缺的成功中学习的效果。在13个基准数据集上的广泛评估表明，最先进的提示注入防御措施仍然容易受到自适应攻击。我们还将PISmith与静态、基于搜索和基于RL的攻击类别中的7个基线进行比较，结果表明PISmith始终能够实现最高的攻击成功率。此外，PISmith在InjecAgent和AgentDojo上的代理环境中，针对开源和闭源LLM（例如，GPT-4o-mini和GPT-5-nano）都取得了强大的性能。我们的代码可在 https://github.com/albert-y1n/PISmith 获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces PISmith, a reinforcement learning-based red-teaming framework that effectively identifies vulnerabilities in prompt injection defenses for LLMs, especially in agentic settings, by using techniques to overcome reward sparsity in black-box evaluations.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种基于强化学习的红队框架PISmith，通过克服黑盒评估中的奖励稀疏问题，有效识别LLM提示注入防御中的漏洞，尤其是在Agent设置中。

Authors: Chenlong Yin, Runpeng Geng, Yanting Wang, Jinyuan Jia

Test-time RL alignment exposes task familiarity artifacts in LLM benchmarks

Abstract (English): Direct evaluation of LLMs on benchmarks can be misleading because comparatively strong performance may reflect task familiarity rather than capability. The train-before-test approach controls for task familiarity by giving each model task-relevant training before evaluation, originally through supervised finetuning. However, suitable training data is often hard to come by, and evaluation results vary with the data chosen. In this paper, we propose a two-stage test-time reinforcement learning (RL) alignment method for train-before-test. First, RL with a single sample provides a first alignment of the model to the task format, and second, test-time RL with majority-voting reward aligns the model to the benchmark distribution. Our test-time RL alignment method aligns similarly well as SFT-based train-before test, but without requiring a task-specific training set. On a domain-specific benchmark without training data, we show that direct evaluation underestimates base models which perform substantially better once aligned, yielding a more faithful evaluation of their capabilities. Moreover, for reasoning tasks, the performance gap between fine-tuned models and their base models largely disappears after alignment, suggesting that many gains from RLVR/SFT reported in the literature are not a difference in reasoning capability, but rather artifacts of task familiarity.

摘要（中文）: 直接在基准测试上评估大型语言模型(LLM)可能具有误导性，因为相对较好的性能可能反映的是任务熟悉度而非能力。先训练后测试方法通过在评估之前给予每个模型与任务相关的训练来控制任务熟悉度，最初是通过监督微调实现。然而，合适的训练数据通常难以获得，且评估结果会随所选数据而变化。在本文中，我们提出了一种用于先训练后测试的两阶段测试时强化学习(RL)对齐方法。首先，使用单一样本的强化学习提供模型对任务格式的初步对齐，其次，使用多数投票奖励的测试时强化学习将模型与基准分布对齐。我们的测试时强化学习对齐方法与基于监督微调(SFT)的先训练后测试一样能良好对齐，但不需要任务特定的训练集。在一个没有训练数据的特定领域基准测试中，我们表明直接评估低估了未经对齐的基础模型，这些模型在对齐后表现显著更好，从而更真实地评估了它们的能力。此外，对于推理任务，微调模型和它们的基础模型之间的性能差距在对齐后几乎消失，这表明文献中报道的来自RLVR/SFT的许多增益并不是推理能力的差异，而是任务熟悉度的人为因素。

TLDR: The paper introduces a test-time RL alignment method to address task familiarity artifacts in LLM benchmarks, showing that direct evaluation can underestimate the true capabilities of base models and overestimate the gains from fine-tuning.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种测试时强化学习对齐方法，以解决LLM基准测试中的任务熟悉度伪影。研究表明，直接评估可能会低估基础模型的真实能力，并高估微调带来的提升。

Authors: Kun Wang, Reinhard Heckel

Panoramic Multimodal Semantic Occupancy Prediction for Quadruped Robots

Abstract (English): Panoramic imagery provides holistic 360° visual coverage for perception in quadruped robots. However, existing occupancy prediction methods are mainly designed for wheeled autonomous driving and rely heavily on RGB cues, limiting their robustness in complex environments. To bridge this gap, (1) we present PanoMMOcc, the first real-world panoramic multimodal occupancy dataset for quadruped robots, featuring four sensing modalities across diverse scenes. (2) We propose a panoramic multimodal occupancy perception framework, VoxelHound, tailored for legged mobility and spherical imaging. Specifically, we design (i) a Vertical Jitter Compensation (VJC) module to mitigate severe viewpoint perturbations caused by body pitch and roll during mobility, enabling more consistent spatial reasoning, and (ii) an effective Multimodal Information Prompt Fusion (MIPF) module that jointly leverages panoramic visual cues and auxiliary modalities to enhance volumetric occupancy prediction. (3) We establish a benchmark based on PanoMMOcc and provide detailed data analysis to enable systematic evaluation of perception methods under challenging embodied scenarios. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VoxelHound achieves state-of-the-art performance on PanoMMOcc (+4.16%} in mIoU). The dataset and code will be publicly released to facilitate future research on panoramic multimodal 3D perception for embodied robotic systems at https://github.com/SXDR/PanoMMOcc, along with the calibration tools released at https://github.com/losehu/CameraLiDAR-Calib.

摘要（中文）: 全景图像为四足机器人感知提供了全面的360°视觉覆盖。 然而，现有的占据预测方法主要为轮式自动驾驶设计，并且严重依赖RGB线索，这限制了它们在复杂环境中的鲁棒性。 为了弥合这一差距，(1) 我们提出了 PanoMMOcc，这是首个面向四足机器人的真实世界全景多模态占据数据集，它在不同的场景中包含了四种感知模态。(2) 我们提出了一个全景多模态占据感知框架 VoxelHound，专为足式移动和球面成像设计。 具体来说，我们设计了 (i) 一个垂直抖动补偿 (VJC) 模块，用于缓解移动过程中因机身俯仰和侧倾引起的严重视点扰动，从而实现更一致的空间推理，以及 (ii) 一个有效的多模态信息提示融合 (MIPF) 模块，该模块联合利用全景视觉线索和辅助模态来增强体素占据预测。(3) 我们基于 PanoMMOcc 建立了一个基准，并提供了详细的数据分析，以方便对具有挑战性的具身场景下的感知方法进行系统评估。 大量实验表明，VoxelHound 在 PanoMMOcc 上实现了最先进的性能（mIoU 提升 +4.16%）。 该数据集和代码将在 https://github.com/SXDR/PanoMMOcc 上公开发布，以促进未来对具身机器人系统的全景多模态 3D 感知的研究，同时校准工具将在 https://github.com/losehu/CameraLiDAR-Calib 上发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces PanoMMOcc, a new panoramic multimodal occupancy dataset for quadruped robots, and VoxelHound, a novel perception framework leveraging multimodal information for improved occupancy prediction in challenging embodied environments.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个名为PanoMMOcc的四足机器人全景多模态语义占用预测数据集，以及VoxelHound，一个新型感知框架，该框架利用多模态信息来改善具有挑战性的具身环境中的占用预测效果。

Authors: Guoqiang Zhao, Zhe Yang, Sheng Wu, Fei Teng, Mengfei Duan, Yuanfan Zheng, Kai Luo, Kailun Yang

Efficient Real-World Autonomous Racing via Attenuated Residual Policy Optimization

Abstract (English): Residual policy learning (RPL), in which a learned policy refines a static base policy using deep reinforcement learning (DRL), has shown strong performance across various robotic applications. Its effectiveness is particularly evident in autonomous racing, a domain that serves as a challenging benchmark for real-world DRL. However, deploying RPL-based controllers introduces system complexity and increases inference latency. We address this by introducing an extension of RPL named attenuated residual policy optimization ($α$-RPO). Unlike standard RPL, $α$-RPO yields a standalone neural policy by progressively attenuating the base policy, which initially serves to bootstrap learning. Furthermore, this mechanism enables a form of privileged learning, where the base policy is permitted to use sensor modalities not required for final deployment. We design $α$-RPO to integrate seamlessly with PPO, ensuring that the attenuated influence of the base controller is dynamically compensated during policy optimization. We evaluate $α$-RPO by building a framework for 1:10-scaled autonomous racing around it. In both simulation and zero-shot real-world transfer to Roboracer cars, $α$-RPO not only reduces system complexity but also improves driving performance compared to baselines - demonstrating its practicality for robotic deployment. Our code is available at: https://github.com/raphajaner/arpo_racing.

摘要（中文）: 残差策略学习（RPL）利用深度强化学习（DRL）优化静态基础策略，在各种机器人应用中表现出强大的性能。尤其在自主赛车领域，这一领域是真实世界DRL的一个具有挑战性的基准，其有效性尤为明显。然而，部署基于RPL的控制器会引入系统复杂性并增加推理延迟。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了RPL的扩展，称为衰减残差策略优化（$α$-RPO）。与标准RPL不同，$α$-RPO通过逐步衰减基础策略来产生一个独立的神经策略，该基础策略最初用于引导学习。此外，这种机制实现了一种特权学习的形式，允许基础策略使用最终部署不需要的传感器模态。我们设计了$α$-RPO，使其与PPO无缝集成，确保在策略优化过程中动态补偿基础控制器的衰减影响。我们通过围绕它构建的1:10比例自主赛车框架来评估$α$-RPO。在仿真和 Roboracer 汽车的零样本真实世界迁移中，$α$-RPO 不仅降低了系统复杂性，而且与基线相比还提高了驾驶性能，证明了其在机器人部署中的实用性。 我们的代码可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/raphajaner/arpo_racing。

TLDR: The paper introduces Attenuated Residual Policy Optimization ($α$-RPO), an extension of Residual Policy Learning, for efficient real-world autonomous racing. $α$-RPO simplifies deployment and improves performance by progressively attenuating the base policy and enabling privileged learning.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了衰减残差策略优化（$α$-RPO），它是残差策略学习的扩展，用于高效的真实世界自动驾驶竞赛。$α$-RPO通过逐步衰减基础策略并实现特权学习，简化了部署并提高了性能。

Authors: Raphael Trumpp, Denis Hoornaert, Mirco Theile, Marco Caccamo

Easy-IIL: Reducing Human Operational Burden in Interactive Imitation Learning via Assistant Experts

Abstract (English): Interactive Imitation Learning (IIL) typically relies on extensive human involvement for both offline demonstration and online interaction. Prior work primarily focuses on reducing human effort in passive monitoring rather than active operation. Interestingly, structured model-based imitation approaches achieve comparable performance with significantly fewer demonstrations than end-to-end imitation learning policies in the low-data regime. However, these methods are typically surpassed by end-to-end policies as the data increases. Leveraging this insight, we propose Easy-IIL, a framework that utilizes off-the-shelf model-based imitation methods as an assistant expert to replace active human operation for the majority of data collection. The human expert only provides a single demonstration to initialize the assistant expert and intervenes in critical states where the task is approaching failure. Furthermore, Easy-IIL can maintain IIL performance by preserving both offline and online data quality. Extensive simulation and real-world experiments demonstrate that Easy-IIL significantly reduces human operational burden while maintaining performance comparable to mainstream IIL baselines. User studies further confirm that Easy-IIL reduces subjective workload on the human expert. Project page: https://sites.google.com/view/easy-iil

摘要（中文）: 交互式模仿学习（IIL）通常依赖于大量的人力投入，包括离线演示和在线交互。以往的研究主要集中于减少被动监控中的人力，而非主动操作。有趣的是，在低数据状态下，结构化的基于模型的模仿方法能够以明显少于端到端模仿学习策略的演示数据实现相当的性能。然而，随着数据量的增加，这些方法通常会被端到端策略超越。基于这一洞察，我们提出了Easy-IIL，一个框架，它利用现成的基于模型的模仿方法作为辅助专家，来替代大部分数据收集过程中的主动人工操作。人类专家仅提供一次演示来初始化辅助专家，并在任务接近失败的关键状态进行干预。此外，Easy-IIL能够同时保持离线和在线数据的质量，从而维持IIL性能。大量的模拟和真实世界实验表明，Easy-IIL在保持与主流IIL基线相当的性能的同时，显著降低了人类操作负担。用户研究进一步证实，Easy-IIL降低了人类专家的主观工作量。项目主页：https://sites.google.com/view/easy-iil

TLDR: Easy-IIL reduces human operational burden in interactive imitation learning by using a model-based imitation assistant expert for data collection, intervening with the human expert only at critical failure states.

简要说明: Easy-IIL 通过使用基于模型的模仿助手专家进行数据收集，减少了交互式模仿学习中的人工操作负担，仅在关键失败状态下才人工介入。

Authors: Chengjie Zhang, Chao Tang, Wenlong Dong, Dehao Huang, Aoxiang Gu, Hong Zhang

Conflict Mitigation in Shared Environments using Flow-Aware Multi-Agent Path Finding

Abstract (English): Deploying multi-robot systems in environments shared with dynamic and uncontrollable agents presents significant challenges, especially for large robot fleets. In such environments, individual robot operations can be delayed due to unforeseen conflicts with uncontrollable agents. While existing research primarily focuses on preserving the completeness of Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) solutions considering delays, there is limited emphasis on utilizing additional environmental information to enhance solution quality in the presence of other dynamic agents. To this end, we propose Flow-Aware Multi-Agent Path Finding (FA-MAPF), a novel framework that integrates learned motion patterns of uncontrollable agents into centralized MAPF algorithms. Our evaluation, conducted on a diverse set of benchmark maps with simulated uncontrollable agents and on a real-world map with recorded human trajectories, demonstrates the effectiveness of FA-MAPF compared to state-of-the-art baselines. The experimental results show that FA-MAPF can consistently reduce conflicts with uncontrollable agents, up to 55%, without compromising task efficiency.

摘要（中文）: 在与动态且不可控的智能体共享的环境中部署多机器人系统带来了显著挑战，对于大型机器人群尤其如此。在这样的环境中，由于与不可控智能体之间不可预见的冲突，单个机器人的操作可能会被延迟。虽然现有研究主要关注于在考虑延迟的情况下保持多智能体路径规划（MAPF）解决方案的完备性，但对于利用额外的环境信息来提升存在其他动态智能体时的解决方案质量的关注有限。为此，我们提出了一种流感知多智能体路径规划（FA-MAPF），这是一种将不可控智能体的学习到的运动模式集成到集中式MAPF算法中的新颖框架。我们的评估，在包含模拟的不可控智能体的各种基准地图以及包含记录的人类轨迹的真实地图上进行，证明了FA-MAPF相对于最先进的基线的有效性。实验结果表明，FA-MAPF可以持续减少与不可控智能体的冲突，高达55%，而不会牺牲任务效率。

TLDR: The paper introduces Flow-Aware Multi-Agent Path Finding (FA-MAPF), which integrates learned motion patterns of uncontrollable agents into centralized MAPF algorithms to reduce conflicts in shared environments. Experimental results show a significant reduction in conflicts without compromising task efficiency.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了流感知多智能体路径规划（FA-MAPF），它将不可控智能体的学习运动模式集成到集中式MAPF算法中，以减少共享环境中的冲突。实验结果表明，在不影响任务效率的情况下，冲突显著减少。

Authors: Lukas Heuer, Yufei Zhu, Luigi Palmieri, Andrey Rudenko, Anna Mannucci, Sven Koenig, Martin Magnusson

Skill-informed Data-driven Haptic Nudges for High-dimensional Human Motor Learning

Abstract (English): In this work, we propose a data-driven skill-informed framework to design optimal haptic nudge feedback for high-dimensional novel motor learning tasks. We first model the stochastic dynamics of human motor learning using an Input-Output Hidden Markov Model (IOHMM), which explicitly decouples latent skill evolution from observable kinematic emissions. Leveraging this predictive model, we formulate the haptic nudge feedback design problem as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP). This allows us to derive an optimal nudging policy that minimizes long-term performance cost, implicitly guiding the learner toward robust regions of the skill space. We validated our approach through a human-subject study ($N=30$) using a high-dimensional hand-exoskeleton task. Results demonstrate that participants trained with the POMDP-derived policy exhibited significantly accelerated task performance compared to groups receiving heuristic-based feedback or no feedback. Furthermore, synergy analysis revealed that the POMDP group discovered efficient low-dimensional motor representations more rapidly.

摘要（中文）: 在这项工作中，我们提出了一种数据驱动的、技能知情的框架，用于设计针对高维新型运动学习任务的最佳触觉轻推反馈。我们首先使用输入-输出隐马尔可夫模型(IOHMM)来建模人类运动学习的随机动态，该模型将潜在技能演化与可观察的运动学发射显式解耦。利用这个预测模型，我们将触觉轻推反馈设计问题表述为一个部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程(POMDP)。这使得我们能够推导出最优的轻推策略，该策略最小化长期性能成本，隐式地引导学习者朝着技能空间的稳健区域前进。我们通过一项使用高维手部外骨骼任务的人体实验（N=30）验证了我们的方法。结果表明，与接受基于启发式反馈或无反馈的组相比，使用基于POMDP导出的策略训练的参与者表现出显著加速的任务性能。此外，协同分析表明，POMDP组更快地发现了高效的低维运动表征。

TLDR: The paper presents a skill-informed, data-driven haptic nudge framework that leverages an Input-Output Hidden Markov Model and POMDP to optimize haptic feedback for high-dimensional motor learning, achieving accelerated task performance and efficient motor representation learning in human subjects.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种技能驱动的、数据驱动的触觉提示框架，该框架利用输入-输出隐马尔可夫模型和 POMDP 来优化高维运动学习的触觉反馈，在人类受试者中实现了加速的任务执行和高效的运动表示学习。

Authors: Ankur Kamboj, Rajiv Ranganathan, Xiaobo Tan, Vaibhav Srivastava

COAD: Constant-Time Planning for Continuous Goal Manipulation with Compressed Library and Online Adaptation

Abstract (English): In many robotic manipulation tasks, the robot repeatedly solves motion-planning problems that differ mainly in the location of the goal object and its associated obstacle, while the surrounding workspace remains fixed. Prior works have shown that leveraging experience and offline computation can accelerate repeated planning queries, but they lack guarantees of covering the continuous task space and require storing large libraries of solutions. In this work, we present COAD, a framework that provides constant-time planning over a continuous goal-parameterized task space. COAD discretizes the continuous task space into finitely many Task Coverage Regions. Instead of planning and storing solutions for every region offline, it constructs a compressed library by only solving representative root problems. Other problems are handled through fast adaptation from these root solutions. At query time, the system retrieves a root motion in constant time and adapts it to the desired goal using lightweight adaptation modules such as linear interpolation, Dynamic Movement Primitives, or simple trajectory optimization. We evaluate the framework on various manipulators and environments in simulation and the real world, showing that COAD achieves substantial compression of the motion library while maintaining high success rates and sub-millisecond-level queries, outperforming baseline methods in both efficiency and path quality. The source code is available at https://github.com/elpis-lab/CoAd.

摘要（中文）: 在许多机器人操作任务中，机器人会重复求解运动规划问题，这些问题主要区别在于目标物体及其相关障碍物的位置，而周围的工作空间保持不变。先前的工作表明，利用经验和离线计算可以加速重复规划查询，但它们缺乏覆盖连续任务空间的保证，并且需要存储大量的解决方案库。在这项工作中，我们提出了COAD，一种在连续目标参数化任务空间上提供恒定时间规划的框架。COAD将连续任务空间离散化为有限数量的任务覆盖区域。它不是离线规划和存储每个区域的解决方案，而是通过仅求解具有代表性的根问题来构建一个压缩库。其他问题通过对这些根解决方案进行快速适应来处理。在查询时，系统会在恒定时间内检索一个根运动，并使用轻量级的适应模块（如线性插值、动态运动原语或简单的轨迹优化）将其适应到所需的目标。我们在模拟和现实世界中对各种机械臂和环境评估了该框架，结果表明，COAD实现了运动库的显著压缩，同时保持了高成功率和亚毫秒级的查询速度，在效率和路径质量方面都优于基线方法。源代码可在https://github.com/elpis-lab/CoAd 获取。

TLDR: COAD enables constant-time motion planning for robotic manipulation by compressing motion libraries and adapting solutions online, achieving fast query times and high success rates.

简要说明: COAD通过压缩运动库和在线调整解决方案，实现了机器人操作的恒定时间运动规划，从而实现了快速查询时间和高成功率。

Authors: Adil Shiyas, Zhuoyun Zhong, Constantinos Chamzas

Predictive and adaptive maps for long-term visual navigation in changing environments

Abstract (English): In this paper, we compare different map management techniques for long-term visual navigation in changing environments. In this scenario, the navigation system needs to continuously update and refine its feature map in order to adapt to the environment appearance change. To achieve reliable long-term navigation, the map management techniques have to (i) select features useful for the current navigation task, (ii) remove features that are obsolete, (iii) and add new features from the current camera view to the map. We propose several map management strategies and evaluate their performance with regard to the robot localisation accuracy in long-term teach-and-repeat navigation. Our experiments, performed over three months, indicate that strategies which model cyclic changes of the environment appearance and predict which features are going to be visible at a particular time and location, outperform strategies which do not explicitly model the temporal evolution of the changes.

摘要（中文）: 本文比较了在变化环境中用于长期视觉导航的不同地图管理技术。在这种场景下，导航系统需要持续更新和优化其特征地图，以适应环境外观的变化。为了实现可靠的长期导航，地图管理技术必须能够：(i) 选择对当前导航任务有用的特征，(ii) 删除已过时的特征，(iii) 并将当前相机视野中的新特征添加到地图中。我们提出了几种地图管理策略，并评估了它们在长期示教-复现导航中机器人定位精度的性能。我们进行了为期三个月的实验，结果表明，对环境外观的周期性变化进行建模并预测特定时间和地点可见特征的策略，优于未明确对变化的时间演变进行建模的策略。

TLDR: This paper explores map management strategies for long-term visual navigation in dynamically changing environments, demonstrating that predictive models of environmental changes outperform non-predictive approaches in maintaining localization accuracy.

简要说明: 本文探讨了在动态变化环境中用于长期视觉导航的地图管理策略，证明了预测环境变化的模型在保持定位精度方面优于非预测方法。

Authors: Lucie Halodova, Eliska Dvorakova, Filip Majer, Tomas Vintr, Oscar Martinez Mozos, Feras Dayoub, Tomas Krajnik

Beyond Motion Imitation: Is Human Motion Data Alone Sufficient to Explain Gait Control and Biomechanics?

Abstract (English): With the growing interest in motion imitation learning (IL) for human biomechanics and wearable robotics, this study investigates how additional foot-ground interaction measures, used as reward terms, affect human gait kinematics and kinetics estimation within a reinforcement learning-based IL framework. Results indicate that accurate reproduction of forward kinematics alone does not ensure biomechanically plausible joint kinetics. Adding foot-ground contacts and contact forces to the IL reward terms enables the prediction of joint moments in forward walking simulation, which are significantly closer to those computed by inverse dynamics. This finding highlights a fundamental limitation of motion-only IL approaches, which may prioritize kinematics matching over physical consistency. Incorporating kinetic constraints, particularly ground reaction force and center of pressure information, significantly enhances the realism of internal and external kinetics. These findings suggest that, when imitation learning is applied to human-related research domains such as biomechanics and wearable robot co-design, kinetics-based reward shaping is necessary to achieve physically consistent gait representations.

摘要（中文）: 随着人们对用于人体生物力学和可穿戴机器人运动模仿学习(IL)的兴趣日益增长，本研究探讨了额外的足底-地面交互测量指标，作为奖励项，如何在基于强化学习的IL框架内影响人体步态的运动学和动力学估计。结果表明，仅准确地重现正向运动学并不能确保生物力学上合理的关节动力学。将足底-地面接触和接触力添加到IL奖励项中，能够预测正向行走模拟中的关节力矩，这些关节力矩与反动力学计算的力矩显著接近。这一发现突出了仅基于运动的IL方法的一个根本局限性，即这种方法可能优先考虑运动学匹配而非物理一致性。纳入动力学约束，特别是地面反作用力和压力中心信息，显著增强了内部和外部动力学的真实性。这些发现表明，当模仿学习应用于人体相关的研究领域，如生物力学和可穿戴机器人协同设计时，基于动力学的奖励塑造对于实现物理上一致的步态表征是必要的。

TLDR: This paper shows that imitation learning of human gait solely from motion data leads to biomechanically implausible joint kinetics. Incorporating foot-ground interaction forces as reward terms significantly improves the realism of the simulated gait.

简要说明: 该论文指出，单纯从运动数据模仿学习人类步态会导致生物力学上不合理的关节动力学。将足底与地面的作用力作为奖励项可以显著提高模拟步态的真实性。
