Authors: Xinyi Liu, Jangwhan Ahn, Edgar Lobaton, Jennie Si, He Huang

GNN-DIP: Neural Corridor Selection for Decomposition-Based Motion Planning

Abstract (English): Motion planning through narrow passages remains a core challenge: sampling-based planners rarely place samples inside these narrow but critical regions, and even when samples land inside a passage, the straight-line connections between them run close to obstacle boundaries and are frequently rejected by collision checking. Decomposition-based planners resolve both issues by partitioning free space into convex cells -- every passage is captured exactly as a cell boundary, and any path within a cell is collision-free by construction. However, the number of candidate corridors through the cell graph grows combinatorially with environment complexity, creating a bottleneck in corridor selection. We present GNN-DIP, a framework that addresses this by integrating a Graph Neural Network (GNN) with a two-phase Decomposition-Informed Planner (DIP). The GNN predicts portal scores on the cell adjacency graph to bias corridor search toward near-optimal regions while preserving completeness. In 2D, Constrained Delaunay Triangulation (CDT) with the Funnel algorithm yields exact shortest paths within corridors; in 3D, Slab convex decomposition with portal-face sampling provides near-optimal path evaluation. Benchmarks on 2D narrow-passage scenarios, 3D bottleneck environments with up to 246 obstacles, and dynamic 2D settings show that GNN-DIP achieves 99--100% success rates with 2--280 times speedup over sampling-based baselines.

摘要（中文）: 通过狭窄通道的运动规划仍然是一项核心挑战：基于采样的规划器很少在这些狭窄但关键的区域内放置样本，即使样本落入通道内，它们之间的直线连接也会靠近障碍物边界运行，并且经常被碰撞检测拒绝。基于分解的规划器通过将自由空间划分为凸单元来解决这两个问题——每个通道都被精确地捕获为单元边界，并且单元内的任何路径都通过构造保证无碰撞。然而，通过单元图的候选走廊数量随着环境复杂性的增加呈组合增长，从而在走廊选择中产生瓶颈。我们提出了 GNN-DIP，一种通过将图神经网络 (GNN) 与两阶段分解感知规划器 (DIP) 集成来解决此问题的框架。GNN 预测单元邻接图上的门户分数，以将走廊搜索偏向接近最优区域，同时保持完整性。在 2D 中，使用漏斗算法的约束 Delaunay 三角剖分 (CDT) 可得出走廊内的精确最短路径；在 3D 中，带有门户面采样的平板凸分解提供接近最优的路径评估。在 2D 狭窄通道场景、具有多达 246 个障碍物的 3D 瓶颈环境和动态 2D 环境中的基准测试表明，GNN-DIP 实现了 99-100% 的成功率，并且比基于采样的基线快 2-280 倍。

TLDR: This paper introduces GNN-DIP, a framework that combines Graph Neural Networks with decomposition-based motion planning to efficiently find near-optimal paths through narrow passages, achieving significant speedups compared to sampling-based methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种名为GNN-DIP的框架，该框架结合了图神经网络和基于分解的运动规划，可以高效地找到通过狭窄通道的近优路径，与基于采样的方法相比，实现了显著的加速。

Authors: Peng Xie, Yanlinag Huang, Wenyuan Wu, Amr Alanwar

Hierarchical Dual-Change Collaborative Learning for UAV Scene Change Captioning

Abstract (English): This paper proposes a novel task for UAV scene understanding - UAV Scene Change Captioning (UAV-SCC) - which aims to generate natural language descriptions of semantic changes in dynamic aerial imagery captured from a movable viewpoint. Unlike traditional change captioning that mainly describes differences between image pairs captured from a fixed camera viewpoint over time, UAV scene change captioning focuses on image-pair differences resulting from both temporal and spatial scene variations dynamically captured by a moving camera. The key challenge lies in understanding viewpoint-induced scene changes from UAV image pairs that share only partially overlapping scene content due to viewpoint shifts caused by camera rotation, while effectively exploiting the relative orientation between the two images. To this end, we propose a Hierarchical Dual-Change Collaborative Learning (HDC-CL) method for UAV scene change captioning. In particular, a novel transformer, \emph{i.e.} Dynamic Adaptive Layout Transformer (DALT) is designed to adaptively model diverse spatial layouts of the image pair, where the interrelated features derived from the overlapping and non-overlapping regions are learned within the flexible and unified encoding layer. Furthermore, we propose a Hierarchical Cross-modal Orientation Consistency Calibration (HCM-OCC) method to enhance the model's sensitivity to viewpoint shift directions, enabling more accurate change captioning. To facilitate in-depth research on this task, we construct a new benchmark dataset, named UAV-SCC dataset, for UAV scene change captioning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that the proposed method achieves state-of-the-art performance on this task. The dataset and code will be publicly released upon acceptance of this paper.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种用于无人机场景理解的新任务——无人机场景变化描述（UAV-SCC），旨在生成自然语言描述，阐释从可移动视点捕获的动态航拍图像中语义变化。与传统变化描述主要描述从固定摄像头视点随时间推移的图像对差异不同，无人机场景变化描述侧重于由移动摄像头动态捕获的、时间和空间场景变化共同导致的图像对差异。关键挑战在于理解由无人机图像对中的视点引起的场景变化，这些图像对由于相机旋转导致的视点偏移，仅共享部分重叠的场景内容，同时有效地利用两幅图像之间的相对方向。为此，我们提出了一种用于无人机场景变化描述的分层双重变化协同学习（HDC-CL）方法。特别地，设计了一种新型Transformer，即动态自适应布局Transformer（DALT），以自适应地建模图像对的各种空间布局，其中来自重叠和非重叠区域的相互关联的特征在灵活且统一的编码层中学习。此外，我们提出了一种分层跨模态方向一致性校准（HCM-OCC）方法，以增强模型对视点偏移方向的敏感性，从而实现更准确的变化描述。为了促进对该任务的深入研究，我们构建了一个新的基准数据集，名为UAV-SCC数据集，用于无人机场景变化描述。大量实验表明，所提出的方法在该任务上实现了最先进的性能。数据集和代码将在本文被接收后公开发布。

TLDR: This paper introduces a new task, UAV Scene Change Captioning, and proposes a novel Hierarchical Dual-Change Collaborative Learning (HDC-CL) method with a Dynamic Adaptive Layout Transformer (DALT) and Hierarchical Cross-modal Orientation Consistency Calibration (HCM-OCC) to address the challenges of describing semantic changes in dynamic aerial imagery captured from a moving viewpoint. They also release a new dataset.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一项新任务：无人机场景变化描述 (UAV-SCC)，并提出一种新颖的分层双重变化协同学习 (HDC-CL) 方法，该方法结合了动态自适应布局 Transformer (DALT) 和分层跨模态方向一致性校准 (HCM-OCC)，旨在解决描述从移动视点捕获的动态航拍图像中语义变化所面临的挑战。同时，作者还发布了一个新的数据集。

Authors: Fuhai Chen, Pengpeng Huang, Junwen Wu, Hehong Zhang, Shiping Wang, Xiaoguang Ma, Xuri Ge

Mastering Negation: Boosting Grounding Models via Grouped Opposition-Based Learning

Abstract (English): Current vision-language detection and grounding models predominantly focus on prompts with positive semantics and often struggle to accurately interpret and ground complex expressions containing negative semantics. A key reason for this limitation is the lack of high-quality training data that explicitly captures discriminative negative samples and negation-aware language descriptions. To address this challenge, we introduce D-Negation, a new dataset that provides objects annotated with both positive and negative semantic descriptions. Building upon the observation that negation reasoning frequently appears in natural language, we further propose a grouped opposition-based learning framework that learns negation-aware representations from limited samples. Specifically, our method organizes opposing semantic descriptions from D-Negation into structured groups and formulates two complementary loss functions that encourage the model to reason about negation and semantic qualifiers. We integrate the proposed dataset and learning strategy into a state-of-the-art language-based grounding model. By fine-tuning fewer than 10 percent of the model parameters, our approach achieves improvements of up to 4.4 mAP and 5.7 mAP on positive and negative semantic evaluations, respectively. These results demonstrate that explicitly modeling negation semantics can substantially enhance the robustness and localization accuracy of vision-language grounding models.

摘要（中文）: 当前视觉-语言检测与定位模型主要关注具有积极语义的提示，且通常难以准确解释和定位包含消极语义的复杂表达式。其关键原因在于缺乏高质量的训练数据，该数据能够明确捕获区分性的负样本和感知否定的语言描述。 为应对这一挑战，我们引入了 D-Negation，一个新的数据集，它提供了带有积极和消极语义描述的对象标注。基于否定推理频繁出现在自然语言中的观察，我们进一步提出了一个基于分组对立的学习框架，该框架从有限样本中学习感知否定的表示。具体而言，我们的方法将来自 D-Negation 的对立语义描述组织成结构化的组，并构建了两个互补的损失函数，以鼓励模型推理否定和语义限定语。 我们将所提出的数据集和学习策略集成到最先进的基于语言的定位模型中。通过微调不到 10% 的模型参数，我们的方法在积极和消极语义评估中分别实现了高达 4.4 mAP 和 5.7 mAP 的提升。这些结果表明，显式地建模否定语义可以显著增强视觉-语言定位模型的鲁棒性和定位精度。

TLDR: This paper introduces a new dataset (D-Negation) and a grouped opposition-based learning framework to improve vision-language grounding models' ability to handle negative semantic descriptions, demonstrating significant performance gains by fine-tuning a small portion of model parameters.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一个新的数据集 (D-Negation) 和一个基于分组的对立学习框架，以提高视觉-语言 grounding 模型处理否定语义描述的能力，并通过微调模型的一小部分参数，展示了显著的性能提升。

Authors: Zesheng Yang, Xi Jiang, Bingzhang Hu, Weili Guan, Runmin Cong, Guo-Jun Qi, Feng Zheng

Swap-guided Preference Learning for Personalized Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback

Abstract (English): Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) is a widely used approach to align large-scale AI systems with human values. However, RLHF typically assumes a single, universal reward, which overlooks diverse preferences and limits personalization. Variational Preference Learning (VPL) seeks to address this by introducing user-specific latent variables. Despite its promise, we found that VPL suffers from posterior collapse. While this phenomenon is well known in VAEs, it has not previously been identified in preference learning frameworks. Under sparse preference data and with overly expressive decoders, VPL may cause latent variables to be ignored, reverting to a single-reward model. To overcome this limitation, we propose Swap-guided Preference Learning (SPL). The key idea is to construct fictitious swap annotators and use the mirroring property of their preferences to guide the encoder. SPL introduces three components: (1) swap-guided base regularization, (2) Preferential Inverse Autoregressive Flow (P-IAF), and (3) adaptive latent conditioning. Experiments show that SPL mitigates collapse, enriches user-specific latents, and improves preference prediction. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/cobang0111/SPL

摘要（中文）: 基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）是一种被广泛用于将大规模人工智能系统与人类价值观对齐的方法。然而，RLHF通常假设存在单一的、通用的奖励，这忽略了多样化的偏好并限制了个性化。变分偏好学习（VPL）试图通过引入用户特定的隐变量来解决这个问题。尽管VPL前景广阔，但我们发现它会遭受后验坍塌。虽然这种现象在变分自编码器（VAEs）中广为人知，但之前尚未在偏好学习框架中被识别出来。在稀疏的偏好数据和过度表达的解码器下，VPL可能会导致隐变量被忽略，从而退化为单奖励模型。为了克服这个限制，我们提出了交换引导的偏好学习（SPL）。其核心思想是构建虚构的交换标注者，并利用他们偏好的镜像特性来引导编码器。SPL引入了三个组成部分：（1）交换引导的基础正则化，（2）偏好逆自回归流（P-IAF），以及（3）自适应隐变量条件化。实验表明，SPL减轻了坍塌，丰富了用户特定的隐变量，并提高了偏好预测。我们的代码和数据可在https://github.com/cobang0111/SPL获取。

TLDR: This paper introduces Swap-guided Preference Learning (SPL) to address posterior collapse in Variational Preference Learning (VPL) for personalized RLHF, enhancing user-specific latent representations and preference prediction.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了Swap-guided Preference Learning (SPL)，旨在解决个性化RLHF中Variational Preference Learning (VPL)的后验坍塌问题，从而增强用户特定的潜在表征和偏好预测。

Authors: Gihoon Kim, Euntai Kim

CALF: Communication-Aware Learning Framework for Distributed Reinforcement Learning

Abstract (English): Distributed reinforcement learning policies face network delays, jitter, and packet loss when deployed across edge devices and cloud servers. Standard RL training assumes zero-latency interaction, causing severe performance degradation under realistic network conditions. We introduce CALF (Communication-Aware Learning Framework), which trains policies under realistic network models during simulation. Systematic experiments demonstrate that network-aware training substantially reduces deployment performance gaps compared to network-agnostic baselines. Distributed policy deployments across heterogeneous hardware validate that explicitly modelling communication constraints during training enables robust real-world execution. These findings establish network conditions as a major axis of sim-to-real transfer for Wi-Fi-like distributed deployments, complementing physics and visual domain randomisation.

摘要（中文）: 分布式强化学习策略在跨边缘设备和云服务器部署时，面临网络延迟、抖动和丢包等问题。标准强化学习训练假设零延迟交互，这会导致在真实的联网条件下性能严重下降。我们引入了 CALF（通信感知学习框架），该框架在仿真期间利用真实的网络模型训练策略。系统性的实验表明，与网络无关的基线相比，网络感知训练显著减少了部署性能差距。跨异构硬件的分布式策略部署验证了在训练期间显式建模通信约束能够实现鲁棒的真实世界执行。这些发现确立了网络条件作为类似 Wi-Fi 的分布式部署中从仿真到现实迁移的主要维度，补充了物理和视觉领域的随机化。

TLDR: CALF is a distributed RL framework that trains policies considering realistic network conditions, improving sim-to-real transfer in Wi-Fi-like deployments by addressing network delays, jitter, and packet loss.

简要说明: CALF是一个分布式强化学习框架，它在训练策略时考虑了真实的网路环境，通过解决网络延迟、抖动和丢包问题，提高了在类Wi-Fi部署中的模拟到真实的迁移性能。

Authors: Carlos Purves, Pietro Lio'

ELLA: Generative AI-Powered Social Robots for Early Language Development at Home

Abstract (English): Early language development shapes children's later literacy and learning, yet many families have limited access to scalable, high-quality support at home. Recent advances in generative AI make it possible for social robots to move beyond scripted interactions and engage children in adaptive, conversational activities, but it remains unclear how to design such systems for pre-schoolers and how children engage with them over time in the home. We present ELLA (Early Language Learning Agent), an autonomous, generative AI-powered social robot that supports early language development through interactive storytelling, parent-selected language targets, and scaffolded dialogue. Using a multi-phased, human-centered process, we interviewed parents (n=7) and educators (n=5) and iteratively refined ELLA through twelve in-home design workshops. We then deployed ELLA with ten children for eight days. We report design insights from in-home workshops, characterize children's engagement and behaviors during deployment, and distill design implications for generative AI-powered social robots supporting early language learning at home.

摘要（中文）: 早期语言发展塑造儿童后期的读写能力和学习能力，然而许多家庭在家中获得可扩展、高质量支持的机会有限。生成式人工智能的最新进展使得社交机器人能够超越脚本式互动，与儿童进行自适应的、会话式活动，但如何为学龄前儿童设计此类系统，以及儿童如何随着时间的推移在家中与他们互动，仍然不清楚。我们提出ELLA（早期语言学习代理），这是一个自主的、由生成式人工智能驱动的社交机器人，它通过互动式讲故事、家长选择的语言目标和支架式对话来支持早期语言发展。我们使用多阶段、以人为中心的过程，采访了家长（n=7）和教育工作者（n=5），并通过十二次家庭设计研讨会迭代地改进了ELLA。然后，我们将ELLA部署到十个儿童家庭，为期八天。我们报告了来自家庭研讨会的设计见解，描述了儿童在部署期间的参与度和行为，并提炼了生成式人工智能驱动的社交机器人在家中支持早期语言学习的设计启示。

TLDR: This paper presents ELLA, a generative AI-powered social robot designed to support early language development in preschoolers at home, detailing its development process and initial deployment results.

Authors: Victor Nikhil Antony, Shiye Cao, Shuning Wang, Chien-Ming Huang

Maximum Entropy Exploration Without the Rollouts

Abstract (English): Efficient exploration remains a central challenge in reinforcement learning, serving as a useful pretraining objective for data collection, particularly when an external reward function is unavailable. A principled formulation of the exploration problem is to find policies that maximize the entropy of their induced steady-state visitation distribution, thereby encouraging uniform long-run coverage of the state space. Many existing exploration approaches require estimating state visitation frequencies through repeated on-policy rollouts, which can be computationally expensive. In this work, we instead consider an intrinsic average-reward formulation in which the reward is derived from the visitation distribution itself, so that the optimal policy maximizes steady-state entropy. An entropy-regularized version of this objective admits a spectral characterization: the relevant stationary distributions can be computed from the dominant eigenvectors of a problem-dependent transition matrix. This insight leads to a novel algorithm for solving the maximum entropy exploration problem, EVE (EigenVector-based Exploration), which avoids explicit rollouts and distribution estimation, instead computing the solution through iterative updates, similar to a value-based approach. To address the original unregularized objective, we employ a posterior-policy iteration (PPI) approach, which monotonically improves the entropy and converges in value. We prove convergence of EVE under standard assumptions and demonstrate empirically that it efficiently produces policies with high steady-state entropy, achieving competitive exploration performance relative to rollout-based baselines in deterministic grid-world environments.

摘要（中文）: 高效探索仍然是强化学习中的一个核心挑战，作为数据收集的有效预训练目标，尤其是在外部奖励函数不可用的情况下。探索问题的一个有原则的表述是找到能够最大化其诱导的稳态访问分布熵的策略，从而鼓励状态空间的均匀长期覆盖。 许多现有的探索方法需要通过重复的在线策略回滚来估计状态访问频率，这在计算上可能代价高昂。 在这项工作中，我们考虑一种内在的平均奖励公式，其中的奖励来源于访问分布本身，因此最优策略可以最大化稳态熵。 这个目标的熵正则化版本允许一种谱特征化：相关的平稳分布可以从问题相关的转移矩阵的主导特征向量计算出来。 这一洞察力引导我们提出了一种用于解决最大熵探索问题的新算法，即 EVE（基于特征向量的探索），该算法避免了显式回滚和分布估计，而是通过迭代更新来计算解决方案，类似于基于价值的方法。为了解决原始的非正则化目标，我们采用了一种后验策略迭代 (PPI) 方法，该方法单调地提高熵并在价值上收敛。 我们在标准假设下证明了 EVE 的收敛性，并在确定性网格世界环境中通过实验证明了它能够有效地生成具有高稳态熵的策略，相对于基于回滚的基线，实现了具有竞争力的探索性能。

TLDR: This paper introduces EVE, a novel reinforcement learning algorithm for maximum entropy exploration that avoids costly rollouts by using a spectral characterization derived from eigenvector analysis of a transition matrix, showing competitive performance in grid-world environments.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种新的强化学习算法EVE，用于最大熵探索，该算法通过使用从转移矩阵的特征向量分析中得出的频谱特征来避免昂贵的试玩，并在网格世界环境中表现出竞争性的性能。

Authors: Jacob Adamczyk, Adam Kamoski, Rahul V. Kulkarni

Thermodynamics of Reinforcement Learning Curricula

Abstract (English): Connections between statistical mechanics and machine learning have repeatedly proven fruitful, providing insight into optimization, generalization, and representation learning. In this work, we follow this tradition by leveraging results from non-equilibrium thermodynamics to formalize curriculum learning in reinforcement learning (RL). In particular, we propose a geometric framework for RL by interpreting reward parameters as coordinates on a task manifold. We show that, by minimizing the excess thermodynamic work, optimal curricula correspond to geodesics in this task space. As an application of this framework, we provide an algorithm, "MEW" (Minimum Excess Work), to derive a principled schedule for temperature annealing in maximum-entropy RL.

摘要（中文）: 统计力学与机器学习之间的联系已反复证明卓有成效，为优化、泛化和表征学习提供了深刻见解。本文中，我们遵循这一传统，利用非平衡热力学的成果来形式化强化学习（RL）中的课程学习。具体而言，我们通过将奖励参数解释为任务流形上的坐标，提出了一个RL的几何框架。我们证明了通过最小化过剩热力学功，最优课程对应于该任务空间中的测地线。作为该框架的应用，我们提供了一种算法“MEW”（最小功量），以推导出最大熵RL中温度退火的原则性调度方案。

TLDR: The paper formalizes curriculum learning in reinforcement learning using non-equilibrium thermodynamics, proposing a geometric framework where optimal curricula correspond to geodesics in a task manifold and presents an algorithm for temperature annealing.

简要说明: 该论文使用非平衡热力学形式化了强化学习中的课程学习，提出了一个几何框架，其中最佳课程对应于任务空间中的测地线，并提出了一个用于温度退火的算法。

Authors: Jacob Adamczyk, Juan Sebastian Rojas, Rahul V. Kulkarni

Perceive What Matters: Relevance-Driven Scheduling for Multimodal Streaming Perception

Abstract (English): In modern human-robot collaboration (HRC) applications, multiple perception modules jointly extract visual, auditory, and contextual cues to achieve comprehensive scene understanding, enabling the robot to provide appropriate assistance to human agents intelligently. While executing multiple perception modules on a frame-by-frame basis enhances perception quality in offline settings, it inevitably accumulates latency, leading to a substantial decline in system performance in streaming perception scenarios. Recent work in scene understanding, termed Relevance, has established a solid foundation for developing efficient methodologies in HRC. However, modern perception pipelines still face challenges related to information redundancy and suboptimal allocation of computational resources. Drawing inspiration from the Relevance concept and the information sparsity in HRC events, we propose a novel lightweight perception scheduling framework that efficiently leverages output from previous frames to estimate and schedule necessary perception modules in real-time based on scene context. The experimental results demonstrate that the proposed perception scheduling framework effectively reduces computational latency by up to 27.52% compared to conventional parallel perception pipelines, while also achieving a 72.73% improvement in MMPose activation recall. Additionally, the framework demonstrates high keyframe accuracy, achieving rates of up to 98%. The results validate the framework's capability to enhance real-time perception efficiency without significantly compromising accuracy. The framework shows potential as a scalable and systematic solution for multimodal streaming perception systems in HRC.

摘要（中文）: 在现代人机协作(HRC)应用中，多个感知模块联合提取视觉、听觉和上下文线索，以实现全面的场景理解，从而使机器人能够智能地向人类提供适当的协助。虽然逐帧执行多个感知模块可以在离线环境中提高感知质量，但不可避免地会累积延迟，导致流式感知场景中系统性能大幅下降。最近在场景理解领域的工作，称为“相关性”，为开发HRC中高效方法奠定了坚实的基础。然而，现代感知流水线仍然面临着信息冗余和计算资源分配不佳等方面的挑战。受“相关性”概念和HRC事件中信息稀疏性的启发，我们提出了一种新型的轻量级感知调度框架，该框架有效地利用先前帧的输出来实时估计和调度必要的感知模块，其依据是场景上下文。实验结果表明，与传统的并行感知流水线相比，所提出的感知调度框架可有效降低高达27.52%的计算延迟，同时MMPose激活召回率也提高了72.73%。此外，该框架表现出较高的关键帧准确率，高达98%。结果验证了该框架能够在不显著牺牲准确性的前提下，提高实时感知效率。该框架显示出作为HRC中多模态流式感知系统可扩展和系统性解决方案的潜力。

TLDR: The paper introduces a relevance-driven perception scheduling framework for multimodal streaming perception in HRC that intelligently allocates resources based on scene context, reducing latency and improving performance compared to conventional pipelines.

Authors: Dingcheng Huang, Xiaotong Zhang, Kamal Youcef-Toumi

VIRD: View-Invariant Representation through Dual-Axis Transformation for Cross-View Pose Estimation

Abstract (English): Accurate global localization is crucial for autonomous driving and robotics, but GNSS-based approaches often degrade due to occlusion and multipath effects. As an emerging alternative, cross-view pose estimation predicts the 3-DoF camera pose corresponding to a ground-view image with respect to a geo-referenced satellite image. However, existing methods struggle to bridge the significant viewpoint gap between the ground and satellite views mainly due to limited spatial correspondences. We propose a novel cross-view pose estimation method that constructs view-invariant representations through dual-axis transformation (VIRD). VIRD first applies a polar transformation to the satellite view to establish horizontal correspondence, then uses context-enhanced positional attention on the ground and polar-transformed satellite features to resolve vertical misalignment, explicitly mitigating the viewpoint gap. A view-reconstruction loss is introduced to strengthen the view invariance further, encouraging the derived representations to reconstruct the original and cross-view images. Experiments on the KITTI and VIGOR datasets demonstrate that VIRD outperforms the state-of-the-art methods without orientation priors, reducing median position and orientation errors by 50.7% and 76.5% on KITTI, and 18.0% and 46.8% on VIGOR, respectively.

摘要（中文）: 精确的全局定位对于自动驾驶和机器人技术至关重要，但基于GNSS的方法经常因遮挡和多径效应而性能下降。作为一种新兴的替代方案，跨视角位姿估计预测与带有地理参考的卫星图像相关的地面视角图像对应的3自由度相机位姿。然而，由于空间对应关系有限，现有方法难以弥合地面和卫星视角之间显著的视角差距。我们提出了一种新颖的跨视角位姿估计方法，该方法通过双轴变换（VIRD）构建视角不变表示。VIRD首先对卫星视角应用极坐标变换以建立水平对应关系，然后在地面和极坐标变换后的卫星特征上使用上下文增强的位置注意力来解决垂直方向上的不对齐问题，从而明确地缓解视角差距。引入视角重建损失来进一步加强视角不变性，鼓励导出的表示重建原始图像和跨视角图像。在KITTI和VIGOR数据集上的实验表明，VIRD优于最先进的方法，且无需方向先验，在KITTI上分别将位置和方向的中值误差降低了50.7%和76.5%，在VIGOR上分别降低了18.0%和46.8%。

TLDR: This paper proposes a novel cross-view pose estimation method called VIRD using dual-axis transformation to bridge the viewpoint gap between ground-view and satellite images, achieving state-of-the-art results on KITTI and VIGOR datasets.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种名为VIRD的新颖的跨视角姿态估计方法，该方法使用双轴变换来弥合地面视图和卫星图像之间的视点差距，并在KITTI和VIGOR数据集上实现了最先进的结果。

Authors: Juhye Park, Wooju Lee, Dasol Hong, Changki Sung, Youngwoo Seo, Dongwan Kang, Hyun Myung

SAVA-X: Ego-to-Exo Imitation Error Detection via Scene-Adaptive View Alignment and Bidirectional Cross View Fusion

Abstract (English): Error detection is crucial in industrial training, healthcare, and assembly quality control. Most existing work assumes a single-view setting and cannot handle the practical case where a third-person (exo) demonstration is used to assess a first-person (ego) imitation. We formalize Ego$\rightarrow$Exo Imitation Error Detection: given asynchronous, length-mismatched ego and exo videos, the model must localize procedural steps on the ego timeline and decide whether each is erroneous. This setting introduces cross-view domain shift, temporal misalignment, and heavy redundancy. Under a unified protocol, we adapt strong baselines from dense video captioning and temporal action detection and show that they struggle in this cross-view regime. We then propose SAVA-X, an Align-Fuse-Detect framework with (i) view-conditioned adaptive sampling, (ii) scene-adaptive view embeddings, and (iii) bidirectional cross-attention fusion. On the EgoMe benchmark, SAVA-X consistently improves AUPRC and mean tIoU over all baselines, and ablations confirm the complementary benefits of its components. Code is available at https://github.com/jack1ee/SAVAX.

摘要（中文）: 错误检测在工业培训、医疗保健和装配质量控制中至关重要。现有的大部分工作假设了单视角设置，无法处理使用第三人称(exo)演示来评估第一人称(ego)模仿的实际情况。我们形式化了Ego$\rightarrow$Exo模仿错误检测：给定异步且长度不匹配的ego和exo视频，模型必须在ego时间线上定位程序步骤，并判断每个步骤是否错误。此设置引入了跨视角域漂移、时间不对齐和大量冗余。在一个统一的协议下，我们调整了来自密集视频字幕和时序动作检测的强大基线，并表明它们在这种跨视角机制中表现不佳。然后，我们提出了SAVA-X，一种Align-Fuse-Detect框架，具有（i）视角条件自适应采样，（ii）场景自适应视角嵌入，以及（iii）双向交叉注意力融合。在EgoMe基准测试中，SAVA-X始终优于所有基线的AUPRC和平均tIoU，并且消融实验证实了其组件的互补优势。代码可在https://github.com/jack1ee/SAVAX获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces SAVA-X, a novel framework for detecting errors in ego-to-exo imitation scenarios, addressing challenges like cross-view domain shift and temporal misalignment, and demonstrating improved performance on the EgoMe benchmark.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了SAVA-X，一个用于检测ego-to-exo模仿场景中错误的新框架。该框架解决了跨视角领域偏移和时间不对齐等挑战，并在EgoMe基准测试中表现出改进的性能。

Authors: Xiang Li, Heqian Qiu, Lanxiao Wang, Benliu Qiu, Fanman Meng, Linfeng Xu, Hongliang Li

SAP: Segment Any 4K Panorama

Abstract (English): Promptable instance segmentation is widely adopted in embodied and AR systems, yet the performance of foundation models trained on perspective imagery often degrades on 360° panoramas. In this paper, we introduce Segment Any 4K Panorama (SAP), a foundation model for 4K high-resolution panoramic instance-level segmentation. We reformulate panoramic segmentation as fixed-trajectory perspective video segmentation, decomposing a panorama into overlapping perspective patches sampled along a continuous spherical traversal. This memory-aligned reformulation preserves native 4K resolution while restoring the smooth viewpoint transitions required for stable cross-view propagation. To enable large-scale supervision, we synthesize 183,440 4K-resolution panoramic images with instance segmentation labels using the InfiniGen engine. Trained under this trajectory-aligned paradigm, SAP generalizes effectively to real-world 360° images, achieving +17.2 zero-shot mIoU gain over vanilla SAM2 of different sizes on real-world 4K panorama benchmark.

摘要（中文）: 可提示实例分割已广泛应用于具身和增强现实系统，但基于透视图像训练的基础模型在360°全景图上的性能通常会下降。在本文中，我们引入了Segment Any 4K Panorama (SAP)，这是一个用于4K高分辨率全景实例级分割的基础模型。我们将全景分割重新定义为固定轨迹透视视频分割，将全景图分解为沿连续球面轨迹采样的重叠透视图像块。这种内存对齐的重新定义保留了原生4K分辨率，同时恢复了稳定跨视角传播所需的平滑视点过渡。为了实现大规模监督，我们使用InfiniGen引擎合成了183,440张带有实例分割标签的4K分辨率全景图像。在这一轨迹对齐范式下训练的SAP有效地泛化到真实世界的360°图像，在真实世界的4K全景基准测试中，与不同大小的原始SAM2相比，实现了+17.2的零样本mIoU增益。

TLDR: The paper introduces SAP, a foundation model for high-resolution 4K panoramic instance segmentation, trained on synthesized data using a novel trajectory-aligned paradigm for improved zero-shot performance on real-world panoramas.

Authors: Lutao Jiang, Zidong Cao, Weikai Chen, Xu Zheng, Yuanhuiyi Lyu, Zhenyang Li, Zeyu HU, Yingda Yin, Keyang Luo, Runze Zhang, Kai Yan, Shengju Qian, Haidi Fan, Yifan Peng, Xin Wang, Hui Xiong, Ying-Cong Chen

A Prediction-as-Perception Framework for 3D Object Detection

Abstract (English): Humans combine prediction and perception to observe the world. When faced with rapidly moving birds or insects, we can only perceive them clearly by predicting their next position and focusing our gaze there. Inspired by this, this paper proposes the Prediction-As-Perception (PAP) framework, integrating a prediction-perception architecture into 3D object perception tasks to enhance the model's perceptual accuracy. The PAP framework consists of two main modules: prediction and perception, primarily utilizing continuous frame information as input. Firstly, the prediction module forecasts the potential future positions of ego vehicles and surrounding traffic participants based on the perception results of the current frame. These predicted positions are then passed as queries to the perception module of the subsequent frame. The perceived results are iteratively fed back into the prediction module. We evaluated the PAP structure using the end-to-end model UniAD on the nuScenes dataset. The results demonstrate that the PAP structure improves UniAD's target tracking accuracy by 10% and increases the inference speed by 15%. This indicates that such a biomimetic design significantly enhances the efficiency and accuracy of perception models while reducing computational resource consumption.

摘要（中文）: 人类结合预测和感知来观察世界。面对快速移动的鸟类或昆虫，我们只有预测它们的下一个位置并将视线集中在那里，才能清晰地感知它们。受此启发，本文提出了一种预测即感知 (PAP) 框架，将预测-感知架构集成到3D目标感知任务中，以提高模型的感知精度。PAP框架由预测和感知两个主要模块组成，主要利用连续帧信息作为输入。首先，预测模块基于当前帧的感知结果预测自我车辆和周围交通参与者潜在的未来位置。然后，这些预测的位置将作为查询传递到后续帧的感知模块。感知结果被迭代地反馈到预测模块中。我们在nuScenes数据集上使用端到端模型UniAD评估了PAP结构。结果表明，PAP结构将UniAD的目标跟踪精度提高了10%，并将推理速度提高了15%。这表明，这种仿生设计显著提高了感知模型的效率和精度，同时降低了计算资源消耗。

TLDR: This paper introduces a Prediction-as-Perception (PAP) framework for 3D object detection, inspired by human perception, which uses predicted future positions to enhance perceptual accuracy, showing improvements in tracking and inference speed on the nuScenes dataset.

简要说明: 本文提出了一个用于3D物体检测的“预测即感知”(PAP)框架，该框架受到人类感知的启发，利用预测的未来位置来提高感知精度，并在nuScenes数据集上展示了在跟踪和推理速度方面的提升。

Authors: Song Zhang, Haoyu Chen, Ruibo Wang

A Reduction Algorithm for Markovian Contextual Linear Bandits

Abstract (English): Recent work shows that when contexts are drawn i.i.d., linear contextual bandits can be reduced to single-context linear bandits. This ``contexts are cheap" perspective is highly advantageous, as it allows for sharper finite-time analyses and leverages mature techniques from the linear bandit literature, such as those for misspecification and adversarial corruption. Motivated by applications with temporally correlated availability, we extend this perspective to Markovian contextual linear bandits, where the action set evolves via an exogenous Markov chain. Our main contribution is a reduction that applies under uniform geometric ergodicity. We construct a stationary surrogate action set to solve the problem using a standard linear bandit oracle, employing a delayed-update scheme to control the bias induced by the nonstationary conditional context distributions. We further provide a phased algorithm for unknown transition distributions that learns the surrogate mapping online. In both settings, we obtain a high-probability worst-case regret bound matching that of the underlying linear bandit oracle, with only lower-order dependence on the mixing time.

摘要（中文）: 最近的研究表明，当上下文以独立同分布方式抽取时，线性上下文 Bandit 问题可以简化为单上下文线性 Bandit 问题。这种“上下文廉价”的视角极具优势，因为它允许更精确的有限时间分析，并利用线性 Bandit 文献中成熟的技术，例如针对模型失配和对抗性破坏的技术。受时间相关可用性的应用驱动，我们将这种视角扩展到马尔可夫上下文线性 Bandit 问题，其中动作集可通过外生马尔可夫链演化。我们的主要贡献是一个在一致几何遍历性下适用的简化方法。我们构建一个平稳的代理动作集，利用标准的线性 Bandit 预言机来解决该问题，并采用延迟更新方案来控制由非平稳条件上下文分布引起的偏差。我们进一步提供了一种用于未知转移分布的分阶段算法，该算法可在线学习代理映射。在这两种设置中，我们都获得了与底层线性 Bandit 预言机相匹配的高概率最坏情况遗憾界，且仅对混合时间具有较低阶的依赖性。

TLDR: This paper presents a reduction algorithm for Markovian contextual linear bandits, extending the "contexts are cheap" perspective to scenarios with temporally correlated availability and achieving regret bounds comparable to standard linear bandit oracles.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种马尔科夫上下文线性bandits的降维算法，将“上下文廉价”的观点扩展到具有时间相关可用性的场景，并获得了与标准线性bandit oracles相当的后悔界限。

Authors: Kaan Buyukkalayci, Osama Hanna, Christina Fragouli

InterEdit: Navigating Text-Guided Multi-Human 3D Motion Editing

Abstract (English): Text-guided 3D motion editing has seen success in single-person scenarios, but its extension to multi-person settings is less explored due to limited paired data and the complexity of inter-person interactions. We introduce the task of multi-person 3D motion editing, where a target motion is generated from a source and a text instruction. To support this, we propose InterEdit3D, a new dataset with manual two-person motion change annotations, and a Text-guided Multi-human Motion Editing (TMME) benchmark. We present InterEdit, a synchronized classifier-free conditional diffusion model for TMME. It introduces Semantic-Aware Plan Token Alignment with learnable tokens to capture high-level interaction cues and an Interaction-Aware Frequency Token Alignment strategy using DCT and energy pooling to model periodic motion dynamics. Experiments show that InterEdit improves text-to-motion consistency and edit fidelity, achieving state-of-the-art TMME performance. The dataset and code will be released at https://github.com/YNG916/InterEdit.

摘要（中文）: 文本引导的3D动作编辑在单人场景中已取得成功，但由于配对数据有限以及人际互动的复杂性，其在多人环境中的扩展研究较少。我们引入了多人3D动作编辑的任务，即从源动作和一个文本指令生成目标动作。为了支持该任务，我们提出了InterEdit3D，一个新的数据集，带有手动双人动作变化标注，以及一个文本引导的多人动作编辑（TMME）基准。 我们提出了InterEdit，一个用于TMME的同步无分类器条件扩散模型。它引入了带可学习token的语义感知计划Token对齐，以捕获高层次的互动线索，以及使用DCT和能量池化的交互感知频率Token对齐策略，以建模周期性运动动力学。实验表明，InterEdit提高了文本到动作的一致性和编辑保真度，实现了最先进的TMME性能。数据集和代码将在https://github.com/YNG916/InterEdit发布。

TLDR: The paper introduces a new task, dataset (InterEdit3D), and method (InterEdit) for text-guided multi-person 3D motion editing using a diffusion model with novel alignment strategies for interaction cues and motion dynamics, achieving state-of-the-art performance on their new benchmark.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一项新的任务、数据集 (InterEdit3D) 和方法 (InterEdit)，用于文本引导的多人3D运动编辑。该方法使用扩散模型，并采用新颖的对齐策略来捕捉交互线索和运动动力学，并在新基准测试上实现了最先进的性能。

Authors: Yebin Yang, Di Wen, Lei Qi, Weitong Kong, Junwei Zheng, Ruiping Liu, Yufan Chen, Chengzhi Wu, Kailun Yang, Yuqian Fu, Danda Pani Paudel, Luc Van Gool, Kunyu Peng

Reinforcement Learning for Elliptical Cylinder Motion Control Tasks

Abstract (English): The control of devices with limited input always bring attention to solve by research due to its difficulty and non-trival solution. For instance, the inverted pendulum is benchmarking problem in control theory and machine learning. In this work, we are focused on the elliptical cylinder and its motion under limited torque. The inspiration of the problem is from untethered magnetic devices, which due to distance have to operate with limited input torque. In this work, the main goal is to define the control problem of elliptic cylinder with limited input torque and solve it by Reinforcement Learning. As a classical baseline, we evaluate a two-stage controller composed of an energy-shaping swing-up law and a local Linear Quadratic Regulator (LQR) stabilizer around the target equilibrium. The swing-up controller increases the system's mechanical energy to drive the state toward a neighborhood of the desired equilibrium, a linearization of the nonlinear model yields an LQR that regulates the angle and angular-rate states to the target orientation with bounded input. This swing-up + LQR policy is a strong, interpretable reference for underactuated system and serves a point of comparison to the learned policy under identical limits and parameters. The solution shows that the learning is possible however, the different cases like stabilization in upward position or rotating of half turn are very difficult for increasing mass or ellipses with a strongly unequal perimeter ratio.

摘要（中文）: 对输入受限的设备的控制一直备受研究关注，原因在于其难度和非平凡的解决方案。例如，倒立摆是控制理论和机器学习中的基准问题。在本工作中，我们专注于椭圆柱及其在有限扭矩下的运动。该问题的灵感来自无线磁性设备，由于距离限制，它们必须在有限的输入扭矩下运行。本工作的主要目标是定义具有有限输入扭矩的椭圆柱的控制问题，并通过强化学习解决它。作为经典的基准，我们评估了一个两阶段控制器，由能量整形上摆律和一个围绕目标平衡点的局部线性二次调节器 (LQR) 稳定器组成。上摆控制器增加系统的机械能，以将状态驱动到所需平衡状态的邻域，非线性模型的线性化产生 LQR，该 LQR 使用有界输入将角度和角速度状态调节到目标方向。这种上摆 + LQR 策略是欠驱动系统的强大且可解释的参考，并作为在相同限制和参数下与学习策略进行比较的基准。解决方案表明学习是可行的，然而，对于增加质量或具有强烈不等周长的椭圆，诸如向上位置的稳定或旋转半圈的不同情况非常困难。

TLDR: This paper explores using Reinforcement Learning to control an elliptical cylinder with limited torque, comparing the learned policy against a traditional LQR controller. The results indicate learning is possible but challenging for specific scenarios.

简要说明: 本文探讨了使用强化学习来控制具有有限扭矩的椭圆柱体，并将学习到的策略与传统的LQR控制器进行比较。结果表明学习是可能的，但在特定情况下具有挑战性。

Authors: Pawel Marczewski, Paulina Superczynska, Jakub Bernat, Szymon Szczesny

Learning Geometric and Photometric Features from Panoramic LiDAR Scans for Outdoor Place Categorization

Abstract (English): Semantic place categorization, which is one of the essential tasks for autonomous robots and vehicles, allows them to have capabilities of self-decision and navigation in unfamiliar environments. In particular, outdoor places are more difficult targets than indoor ones due to perceptual variations, such as dynamic illuminance over twenty-four hours and occlusions by cars and pedestrians. This paper presents a novel method of categorizing outdoor places using convolutional neural networks (CNNs), which take omnidirectional depth/reflectance images obtained by 3D LiDARs as the inputs. First, we construct a large-scale outdoor place dataset named Multi-modal Panoramic 3D Outdoor (MPO) comprising two types of point clouds captured by two different LiDARs. They are labeled with six outdoor place categories: coast, forest, indoor/outdoor parking, residential area, and urban area. Second, we provide CNNs for LiDAR-based outdoor place categorization and evaluate our approach with the MPO dataset. Our results on the MPO dataset outperform traditional approaches and show the effectiveness in which we use both depth and reflectance modalities. To analyze our trained deep networks we visualize the learned features.

摘要（中文）: 语义场所分类是自主机器人和车辆的关键任务之一，使其能够生存在陌生的环境中进行自主决策和导航。特别是，由于感知变化，例如全天动态光照和车辆及行人的遮挡，室外场所比室内场所更难成为目标。本文提出了一种使用卷积神经网络（CNN）对室外场所进行分类的新方法，该网络以3D激光雷达获取的全向深度/反射率图像作为输入。首先，我们构建了一个名为多模态全景3D室外（MPO）的大规模室外场所数据集，其中包括由两种不同激光雷达捕获的两种类型的点云。它们被标记为六个室外场所类别：海岸、森林、室内/室外停车场、住宅区和城市区域。其次，我们提供了基于激光雷达的室外场所分类的CNN，并使用MPO数据集评估了我们的方法。我们在MPO数据集上的结果优于传统方法，并表明了同时使用深度和反射率模态的有效性。为了分析我们训练的深度网络，我们可视化了学习到的特征。

TLDR: The paper introduces a new large-scale outdoor place dataset (MPO) and a CNN-based method for outdoor place categorization using LiDAR data, demonstrating improved performance compared to traditional approaches.

Authors: Kazuto Nakashima, Hojung Jung, Yuki Oto, Yumi Iwashita, Ryo Kurazume, Oscar Martinez Mozos

From Experiments to Expertise: Scientific Knowledge Consolidation for AI-Driven Computational Research

Abstract (English): While large language models (LLMs) have transformed AI agents into proficient executors of computational materials science, performing a hundred simulations does not make a researcher. What distinguishes research from routine execution is the progressive accumulation of knowledge -- learning which approaches fail, recognizing patterns across systems, and applying understanding to new problems. However, the prevailing paradigm in AI-driven computational science treats each execution in isolation, largely discarding hard-won insights between runs. Here we present QMatSuite, an open-source platform closing this gap. Agents record findings with full provenance, retrieve knowledge before new calculations, and in dedicated reflection sessions correct erroneous findings and synthesize observations into cross-compound patterns. In benchmarks on a six-step quantum-mechanical simulation workflow, accumulated knowledge reduces reasoning overhead by 67% and improves accuracy from 47% to 3% deviation from literature -- and when transferred to an unfamiliar material, achieves 1% deviation with zero pipeline failures.

摘要（中文）: 大型语言模型 (LLM) 已将人工智能Agent转变为计算材料科学领域的高效执行者，但进行数百次模拟并不能造就一位研究者。研究与常规执行的区别在于知识的逐步积累——学习哪些方法会失败，识别跨系统的模式，并将理解应用于新问题。然而，人工智能驱动的计算科学领域的主流范式将每次执行视为孤立事件，在很大程度上忽略了运行之间来之不易的深刻见解。在此，我们提出了 QMatSuite，一个旨在弥合这一差距的开源平台。Agent记录包含完整溯源的发现，在新计算之前检索知识，并在专门的反思环节中纠正错误的发现，并将观察结果合成为跨化合物的模式。在六步量子力学模拟工作流程的基准测试中，积累的知识将推理开销降低了 67%，并将准确性从与文献偏差的 47% 提高到 3%——并且在转移到不熟悉的材料时，实现了 1% 的偏差，且管道无故障。

TLDR: The paper introduces QMatSuite, a platform that enables AI agents to accumulate and reuse knowledge from computational materials science simulations, leading to significant improvements in efficiency and accuracy.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一个名为QMatSuite的平台，该平台使人工智能代理能够积累并重复利用计算材料科学模拟中的知识，从而显著提高效率和准确性。

Authors: Haonan Huang

Context is all you need: Towards autonomous model-based process design using agentic AI in flowsheet simulations

Abstract (English): Agentic AI systems integrating large language models (LLMs) with reasoning and tooluse capabilities are transforming various domains - in particular, software development. In contrast, their application in chemical process flowsheet modelling remains largely unexplored. In this work, we present an agentic AI framework that delivers assistance in an industrial flowsheet simulation environment. To this end, we show the capabilities of GitHub Copilot (GitHub, Inc., 2026), when using state-of-the-art LLMs, such as Claude Opus 4.6 (Anthropic, PBC, 2026), to generate valid syntax for our in-house process modelling tool Chemasim using the technical documentation and a few commented examples as context. Based on this, we develop a multi-agent system that decomposes process development tasks with one agent solving the abstract problem using engineering knowledge and another agent implementing the solution as Chemasim code. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework for typical flowsheet modelling examples, including (i) a reaction/separation process, (ii) a pressure-swing distillation, and (iii) a heteroazeotropic distillation including entrainer selection. Along these lines, we discuss current limitations of the framework and outline future research directions to further enhance its capabilities.

摘要（中文）: 集成了大型语言模型（LLMs）并具备推理和工具使用能力的自主AI系统正在变革各个领域，尤其是在软件开发领域。相比之下，它们在化学工艺流程模拟建模中的应用仍然在很大程度上未被探索。在这项工作中，我们提出了一个自主AI框架，可在工业流程模拟环境中提供辅助。为此，我们展示了GitHub Copilot（GitHub, Inc., 2026）在使用最先进的LLMs，如Claude Opus 4.6 (Anthropic, PBC, 2026)时，利用技术文档和一些带有注释的示例作为上下文，为我们的内部流程建模工具Chemasim生成有效语法的能力。在此基础上，我们开发了一个多智能体系统，该系统将工艺开发任务分解，其中一个智能体使用工程知识解决抽象问题，另一个智能体将解决方案实现为Chemasim代码。我们通过典型的流程模拟建模案例证明了我们框架的有效性，包括 (i)反应/分离过程，(ii)变压吸附精馏，以及(iii)包含夹带剂选择的非均相共沸精馏。同时，我们讨论了该框架当前的局限性并概述了未来的研究方向，以进一步增强其能力。

TLDR: This paper explores the use of agentic AI, leveraging LLMs like Claude Opus, in chemical process flowsheet modeling within an industrial simulation environment, demonstrating its effectiveness on various flowsheet examples. It proposes a multi-agent system that can both solve abstract problems and implement them as Chemasim code.

Authors: Pascal Schäfer, Lukas J. Krinke, Martin Wlotzka, Norbert Asprion

IGASA: Integrated Geometry-Aware and Skip-Attention Modules for Enhanced Point Cloud Registration

Abstract (English): Point cloud registration (PCR) is a fundamental task in 3D vision and provides essential support for applications such as autonomous driving, robotics, and environmental modeling. Despite its widespread use, existing methods often fail when facing real-world challenges like heavy noise, significant occlusions, and large-scale transformations. These limitations frequently result in compromised registration accuracy and insufficient robustness in complex environments. In this paper, we propose IGASA as a novel registration framework constructed upon a Hierarchical Pyramid Architecture (HPA) designed for robust multi-scale feature extraction and fusion. The framework integrates two pivotal components consisting of the Hierarchical Cross-Layer Attention (HCLA) module and the Iterative Geometry-Aware Refinement (IGAR) module. The HCLA module utilizes skip attention mechanisms to align multi-resolution features and enhance local geometric consistency. Simultaneously, the IGAR module is designed for the fine matching phase by leveraging reliable correspondences established during coarse matching. This synergistic integration within the architecture allows IGASA to adapt effectively to diverse point cloud structures and intricate transformations. We evaluate the performance of IGASA on four widely recognized benchmark datasets including 3D(Lo)Match, KITTI, and nuScenes. Our extensive experiments consistently demonstrate that IGASA significantly surpasses state-of-the-art methods and achieves notable improvements in registration accuracy. This work provides a robust foundation for advancing point cloud registration techniques while offering valuable insights for practical 3D vision applications. The code for IGASA is available in \href{https://github.com/DongXu-Zhang/IGASA}{https://github.com/DongXu-Zhang/IGASA}.

摘要（中文）: 点云配准 (PCR) 是三维视觉中的一项基本任务，为自动驾驶、机器人和环境建模等应用提供重要支持。尽管其应用广泛，但现有方法在面对真实世界的挑战时，如严重噪声、显著遮挡和大规模变换，通常会失效。这些限制经常导致配准精度降低，在复杂环境中鲁棒性不足。在本文中，我们提出 IGASA，一个建立在分层金字塔架构 (HPA) 之上的新型配准框架，该架构旨在实现稳健的多尺度特征提取和融合。该框架集成了两个关键组件，包括分层跨层注意力 (HCLA) 模块和迭代几何感知细化 (IGAR) 模块。HCLA 模块利用跳跃注意力机制来对齐多分辨率特征并增强局部几何一致性。同时，IGAR 模块专为精细匹配阶段设计，通过利用粗匹配期间建立的可靠对应关系。这种架构内的协同集成使 IGASA 能够有效地适应不同的点云结构和复杂的变换。我们在四个广泛认可的基准数据集（包括 3D(Lo)Match、KITTI 和 nuScenes）上评估了 IGASA 的性能。我们的大量实验始终表明，IGASA 显著超过了最先进的方法，并在配准精度方面取得了显著的改进。这项工作为推进点云配准技术提供了坚实的基础，同时为实际的三维视觉应用提供了宝贵的见解。 IGASA 的代码可在 \href{https://github.com/DongXu-Zhang/IGASA}{https://github.com/DongXu-Zhang/IGASA} 中获取。

TLDR: The paper introduces IGASA, a novel point cloud registration framework with integrated modules for robust, geometry-aware multi-scale feature extraction and refinement. It achieves state-of-the-art results on multiple benchmark datasets.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种新的点云配准框架IGASA，它集成了几何感知和跳跃注意力模块，用于鲁棒的多尺度特征提取和细化。在多个基准数据集上取得了最先进的结果。

Authors: Dongxu Zhang, Jihua Zhu, Shiqi Li, Wenbiao Yan, Haoran Xu, Peilin Fan, Huimin Lu

Catalyst4D: High-Fidelity 3D-to-4D Scene Editing via Dynamic Propagation

Abstract (English): Recent advances in 3D scene editing using NeRF and 3DGS enable high-quality static scene editing. In contrast, dynamic scene editing remains challenging, as methods that directly extend 2D diffusion models to 4D often produce motion artifacts, temporal flickering, and inconsistent style propagation. We introduce Catalyst4D, a framework that transfers high-quality 3D edits to dynamic 4D Gaussian scenes while maintaining spatial and temporal coherence. At its core, Anchor-based Motion Guidance (AMG) builds a set of structurally stable and spatially representative anchors from both original and edited Gaussians. These anchors serve as robust region-level references, and their correspondences are established via optimal transport to enable consistent deformation propagation without cross-region interference or motion drift. Complementarily, Color Uncertainty-guided Appearance Refinement (CUAR) preserves temporal appearance consistency by estimating per-Gaussian color uncertainty and selectively refining regions prone to occlusion-induced artifacts. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Catalyst4D achieves temporally stable, high-fidelity dynamic scene editing and outperforms existing methods in both visual quality and motion coherence.

摘要（中文）: 最近在使用NeRF和3DGS进行3D场景编辑方面取得了进展，实现了高质量的静态场景编辑。相比之下，动态场景编辑仍然具有挑战性，因为直接将2D扩散模型扩展到4D的方法通常会产生运动伪影、时间闪烁和不一致的风格传播。我们引入了Catalyst4D，这是一个将高质量3D编辑转移到动态4D高斯场景中的框架，同时保持空间和时间连贯性。其核心是基于锚点的运动引导(AMG)，它从原始和编辑后的高斯分布中构建了一组结构稳定且具有空间代表性的锚点。这些锚点作为鲁棒的区域级参考，并通过最优传输建立它们的对应关系，从而实现一致的变形传播，而不会产生跨区域干扰或运动漂移。作为补充，颜色不确定性引导的外观优化(CUAR)通过估计每个高斯粒子的颜色不确定性并有选择地优化易于产生遮挡伪影的区域，从而保持时间外观一致性。大量的实验表明，Catalyst4D实现了时间稳定的、高保真度的动态场景编辑，并且在视觉质量和运动连贯性方面优于现有方法。

TLDR: Catalyst4D addresses the challenge of dynamic scene editing by introducing Anchor-based Motion Guidance and Color Uncertainty-guided Appearance Refinement to achieve temporally stable and high-fidelity results. It outperforms existing methods in visual quality and motion coherence.

简要说明: Catalyst4D通过引入基于锚点的运动引导和颜色不确定性引导的外观优化，解决了动态场景编辑的挑战，实现了时间上的稳定性和高保真度结果。在视觉质量和运动连贯性方面，该方法优于现有方法。

Relevance: (4/10)

Authors: Shifeng Chen, Yihui Li, Jun Liao, Hongyu Yang, Di Huang

CM-Bench: A Comprehensive Cross-Modal Feature Matching Benchmark Bridging Visible and Infrared Images

Abstract (English): Infrared-visible (IR-VIS) feature matching plays an essential role in cross-modality visual localization, navigation and perception. Along with the rapid development of deep learning techniques, a number of representative image matching methods have been proposed. However, crossmodal feature matching is still a challenging task due to the significant appearance difference. A significant gap for cross-modal feature matching research lies in the absence of standardized benchmarks and metrics for evaluations. In this paper, we introduce a comprehensive cross-modal feature matching benchmark, CM-Bench, which encompasses 30 feature matching algorithms across diverse cross-modal datasets. Specifically, state-of-the-art traditional and deep learning-based methods are first summarized and categorized into sparse, semidense, and dense methods. These methods are evaluated by different tasks including homography estimation, relative pose estimation, and feature-matching-based geo-localization. In addition, we introduce a classification-network-based adaptive preprocessing front-end that automatically selects suitable enhancement strategies before matching. We also present a novel infrared-satellite cross-modal dataset with manually annotated ground-truth correspondences for practical geo-localization evaluation. The dataset and resource will be available at: https://github.com/SLZ98/CM-Bench.

摘要（中文）: 红外-可见光(IR-VIS)特征匹配在跨模态视觉定位、导航和感知中起着至关重要的作用。随着深度学习技术的快速发展，已经提出了许多具有代表性的图像匹配方法。然而，由于显著的外观差异，跨模态特征匹配仍然是一项具有挑战性的任务。跨模态特征匹配研究的一个重要缺口在于缺乏用于评估的标准化的基准和指标。在本文中，我们引入了一个全面的跨模态特征匹配基准，CM-Bench，它涵盖了跨多个不同跨模态数据集的30种特征匹配算法。具体来说，首先总结了最先进的传统方法和基于深度学习的方法，并将其分为稀疏、半稠密和稠密方法。这些方法通过不同的任务进行评估，包括单应性估计、相对位姿估计和基于特征匹配的地理定位。此外，我们引入了一个基于分类网络的自适应预处理前端，可以在匹配之前自动选择合适的增强策略。我们还提出了一个新的红外-卫星跨模态数据集，该数据集具有手动标注的真实对应关系，用于实际的地理定位评估。数据集和资源将在以下网址提供：https://github.com/SLZ98/CM-Bench。

Authors: Liangzheng Sun, Mengfan He, Xingyu Shao, Binbin Li, Zhiqiang Yan, Chunyu Li, Ziyang Meng, Fei Xing

VFM-Recon: Unlocking Cross-Domain Scene-Level Neural Reconstruction with Scale-Aligned Foundation Priors

Abstract (English): Scene-level neural volumetric reconstruction from monocular videos remains challenging, especially under severe domain shifts. Although recent advances in vision foundation models (VFMs) provide transferable generalized priors learned from large-scale data, their scaleambiguous predictions are incompatible with the scale consistency required by volumetric fusion. To address this gap, we present VFMRecon, the first attempt to bridge transferable VFM priors with scaleconsistent requirements in scene-level neural reconstruction. Specifically, we first introduce a lightweight scale alignment stage that restores multiview scale coherence. We then integrate pretrained VFM features into the neural volumetric reconstruction pipeline via lightweight task-specific adapters, which are trained for reconstruction while preserving the crossdomain robustness of pretrained representations. We train our model on ScanNet train split and evaluate on both in-distribution ScanNet test split and out-of-distribution TUM RGB-D and Tanks and Temples datasets. The results demonstrate that our model achieves state-of-theart performance across all datasets domains. In particular, on the challenging outdoor Tanks and Temples dataset, our model achieves an F1 score of 70.1 in reconstructed mesh evaluation, substantially outperforming the closest competitor, VGGT, which only attains 51.8.

摘要（中文）: 从单目视频中进行场景级神经体积重建仍然具有挑战性，尤其是在严重的领域偏移下。尽管视觉基础模型(VFMs)的最新进展提供了从大规模数据中学习的可迁移的通用先验知识，但它们尺度模糊的预测与体积融合所需的尺度一致性不兼容。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了VFMRecon，这是首次尝试将可迁移的VFM先验知识与场景级神经重建中的尺度一致性要求结合起来。具体来说，我们首先引入了一个轻量级的尺度对齐阶段，以恢复多视角的尺度一致性。然后，我们将预训练的VFM特征通过轻量级的特定任务适配器集成到神经体积重建流程中，这些适配器经过训练用于重建，同时保持预训练表示的跨领域鲁棒性。我们在ScanNet训练集上训练我们的模型，并在同分布的ScanNet测试集以及异分布的TUM RGB-D和Tanks and Temples数据集上进行评估。结果表明，我们的模型在所有数据集领域中都实现了最先进的性能。特别是在具有挑战性的室外Tanks and Temples数据集上，我们的模型在重建网格评估中实现了70.1的F1分数，大大优于最接近的竞争对手VGGT，后者仅达到51.8。

TLDR: The paper introduces VFM-Recon, a method to improve scene-level neural volumetric reconstruction from monocular videos by integrating vision foundation model priors with a novel scale alignment stage, achieving state-of-the-art performance across various datasets.

Authors: Yuhang Ming, Tingkang Xi, Xingrui Yang, Lixin Yang, Yong Peng, Cewu Lu, Wanzeng Kong

CVGL: Causal Learning and Geometric Topology

Abstract (English): Cross-view geo-localization (CVGL) aims to estimate the geographic location of a street image by matching it with a corresponding aerial image. This is critical for autonomous navigation and mapping in complex real-world scenarios. However, the task remains challenging due to significant viewpoint differences and the influence of confounding factors. To tackle these issues, we propose the Causal Learning and Geometric Topology (CLGT) framework, which integrates two key components: a Causal Feature Extractor (CFE) that mitigates the influence of confounding factors by leveraging causal intervention to encourage the model to focus on stable, task-relevant semantics; and a Geometric Topology Fusion (GT Fusion) module that injects Bird's Eye View (BEV) road topology into street features to alleviate cross-view inconsistencies caused by extreme perspective changes. Additionally, we introduce a Data-Adaptive Pooling (DA Pooling) module to enhance the representation of semantically rich regions. Extensive experiments on CVUSA, CVACT, and their robustness-enhanced variants (CVUSA-C-ALL and CVACT-C-ALL) demonstrate that CLGT achieves state-of-the-art performance, particularly under challenging real-world corruptions. Our codes are available at https://github.com/oyss-szu/CLGT.

摘要（中文）: 跨视角地理定位（CVGL）旨在通过将街景图像与对应的航拍图像进行匹配来估计街景图像的地理位置。这对于复杂现实场景中的自主导航和地图绘制至关重要。然而，由于显著的视角差异和混淆因素的影响，该任务仍然具有挑战性。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了因果学习和几何拓扑（CLGT）框架，该框架集成了两个关键组件：一个因果特征提取器（CFE），它通过利用因果干预来鼓励模型关注稳定且与任务相关的语义，从而减轻混淆因素的影响；以及一个几何拓扑融合（GT Fusion）模块，它将鸟瞰图（BEV）道路拓扑注入到街景特征中，以减轻由极端视角变化引起的跨视角不一致性。此外，我们引入了一个数据自适应池化（DA Pooling）模块，以增强语义丰富区域的表示。 在CVUSA、CVACT及其鲁棒性增强变体（CVUSA-C-ALL和CVACT-C-ALL）上的大量实验表明，CLGT实现了最先进的性能，尤其是在具有挑战性的现实场景干扰下。我们的代码可在https://github.com/oyss-szu/CLGT获得。

TLDR: This paper introduces a novel framework, CLGT, for cross-view geo-localization, combining causal learning and geometric topology to address viewpoint differences and confounding factors, achieving state-of-the-art results on benchmark datasets.

简要说明: 该论文提出了一种新颖的用于跨视角地理定位的框架 CLGT，结合了因果学习和几何拓扑来解决视角差异和混淆因素，并在基准数据集上取得了最先进的结果。

Authors: Songsong Ouyang, Yingying Zhu

A Spectral Revisit of the Distributional Bellman Operator under the Cramér Metric

Abstract (English): Distributional reinforcement learning (DRL) studies the evolution of full return distributions under Bellman updates rather than focusing on expected values. A classical result is that the distributional Bellman operator is contractive under the Cramér metric, which corresponds to an $L^2$ geometry on differences of cumulative distribution functions (CDFs). While this contraction ensures stability of policy evaluation, existing analyses remain largely metric, focusing on contraction properties without elucidating the structural action of the Bellman update on distributions. In this work, we analyse distributional Bellman dynamics directly at the level of CDFs, treating the Cramér geometry as the intrinsic analytical setting. At this level, the Bellman update acts affinely on CDFs and linearly on differences between CDFs, and its contraction property yields a uniform bound on this linear action. Building on this intrinsic formulation, we construct a family of regularised spectral Hilbert representations that realise the CDF-level geometry by exact conjugation, without modifying the underlying Bellman dynamics. The regularisation affects only the geometry and vanishes in the zero-regularisation limit, recovering the native Cramér metric. This framework clarifies the operator structure underlying distributional Bellman updates and provides a foundation for further functional and operator-theoretic analyses in DRL.

摘要（中文）: 分布强化学习（DRL）研究完整回报分布在贝尔曼更新下的演化，而非聚焦于期望值。一个经典的结论是，分布贝尔曼算子在克拉美（Cramér）度量下是收缩的，这对应于累积分布函数(CDF)差异上的$L^2$几何。虽然这种收缩确保了策略评估的稳定性，但现有的分析主要停留在度量层面，侧重于收缩性质，而没有阐明贝尔曼更新在分布上的结构性作用。在这项工作中，我们在累积分布函数（CDF）层面直接分析分布贝尔曼动力学，将克拉美几何视为内在的分析设定。在这个层面上，贝尔曼更新在CDF上的作用是仿射的，在CDF的差异上的作用是线性的，并且其收缩性质为这种线性作用提供了一致有界性。在此内在公式的基础上，我们构建了一系列正则化的谱希尔伯特表示，通过精确共轭实现CDF层面的几何，而无需修改底层的贝尔曼动力学。正则化仅影响几何，并在零正则化极限下消失，从而恢复原始的克拉美度量。该框架阐明了分布贝尔曼更新的底层算子结构，并为DRL中进一步的泛函和算子理论分析奠定了基础。

TLDR: This paper analyzes distributional Bellman dynamics using the Cramér metric, formulating the Bellman update as an affine transformation on CDFs and introducing regularized spectral Hilbert representations for analysis.

简要说明: 该论文使用Cramér度量分析了分布贝尔曼动态，将贝尔曼更新公式化为CDF上的仿射变换，并引入了正则化谱希尔伯特表示用于分析。

Authors: Keru Wang, Yixin Deng, Yao Lyu, Stephen Redmond, Shengbo Eben Li

A Feasibility-Enhanced Control Barrier Function Method for Multi-UAV Collision Avoidance

Abstract (English): This paper presents a feasibility-enhanced control barrier function (FECBF) framework for multi-UAV collision avoidance. In dense multi-UAV scenarios, the feasibility of the CBF quadratic program (CBF-QP) can be compromised due to internal incompatibility among multiple CBF constraints. To address this issue, we analyze the internal compatibility of CBF constraints and derive a sufficient condition for internal compatibility. Based on this condition, a sign-consistency constraint is introduced to mitigate internal incompatibility. The proposed constraint is incorporated into a decentralized CBF-QP formulation using worst-case estimates and slack variables. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed method significantly reduces infeasibility and improves collision avoidance performance compared with existing baselines in dense scenarios. Additional simulations under varying time delays demonstrate the robustness of the proposed method. Real-world experiments validate the practical applicability of the proposed method.

摘要（中文）: 本文提出了一种可行性增强的控制障碍函数 (FECBF) 框架，用于多无人机避撞。 在密集的无人机群中，由于多个 CBF 约束之间的内部不兼容性，CBF 二次规划 (CBF-QP) 的可行性可能会受到影响。 为了解决这个问题，我们分析了 CBF 约束的内部兼容性，并推导出了内部兼容性的充分条件。 基于此条件，引入了符号一致性约束来减轻内部不兼容性。 所提出的约束通过最坏情况估计和松弛变量被纳入到分散式 CBF-QP 公式中。 仿真结果表明，与现有基线方法相比，该方法在密集场景中显著降低了不可行性，并提高了避撞性能。 在不同时间延迟下的额外仿真证明了该方法的鲁棒性。 真实世界的实验验证了该方法的实际适用性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a Feasibility-Enhanced Control Barrier Function (FECBF) framework for multi-UAV collision avoidance, addressing the infeasibility issues in dense scenarios by introducing a sign-consistency constraint. Both simulations and real-world experiments validate its effectiveness and robustness.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种可行性增强的控制障碍函数（FECBF）框架，用于多无人机避碰。该方法通过引入符号一致性约束来解决密集场景中的不可行性问题，并通过仿真和实际实验验证了其有效性和鲁棒性。

Authors: Qishen Zhong, Junlong Wu, Jian Yang, Guanwei Xiao, Junqi Wu, Zimeng Jiang, Pingan Fang

From Passive Monitoring to Active Defence: Resilient Control of Manipulators Under Cyberattacks

Abstract (English): Cyber-physical robotic systems are vulnerable to false data injection attacks (FDIAs), in which an adversary corrupts sensor signals while evading residual-based passive anomaly detectors such as the chi-squared test. Such stealthy attacks can induce substantial end-effector deviations without triggering alarms. This paper studies the resilience of redundant manipulators to stealthy FDIAs and advances the architecture from passive monitoring to active defence. We formulate a closed-loop model comprising a feedback-linearized manipulator, a steady-state Kalman filter, and a chi-squared-based anomaly detector. Building on this passive monitoring layer, we propose an active control-level defence that attenuates the control input through a monotone function of an anomaly score generated by a novel actuation-projected, measurement-free state predictor. The proposed design provides probabilistic guarantees on nominal actuation loss and preserves closed-loop stability. From the attacker perspective, we derive a convex QCQP for computing one-step optimal stealthy attacks. Simulations on a 6-DOF planar manipulator show that the proposed defence significantly reduces attack-induced end-effector deviation while preserving nominal task performance in the absence of attacks.

摘要（中文）: 网络物理机器人系统易受虚假数据注入攻击(FDIA)的影响，在这种攻击中，攻击者会篡改传感器信号，同时躲避基于残差的被动异常检测器，例如卡方检验。这种隐蔽攻击会导致末端执行器产生显著偏差，而不会触发警报。本文研究了冗余机械臂对隐蔽FDIA的抵抗力，并将架构从被动监控推进到主动防御。我们构建了一个闭环模型，包含反馈线性化的机械臂、稳态卡尔曼滤波器和基于卡方的异常检测器。基于此被动监控层，我们提出了一种主动控制级别防御机制，通过一个基于新型驱动投影、无测量状态预测器生成的异常评分的单调函数来衰减控制输入。所提出的设计提供了关于名义驱动损失的概率保证，并保持了闭环稳定性。从攻击者的角度来看，我们推导出一个凸二次约束二次规划(QCQP)，用于计算一步最优隐蔽攻击。在一个六自由度平面机械臂上的仿真结果表明，所提出的防御机制显著降低了攻击引起的末端执行器偏差，同时在没有攻击的情况下保持了名义任务性能。

TLDR: This paper proposes an active control-level defense mechanism for robotic manipulators against stealthy cyberattacks that bypass traditional anomaly detection, demonstrating reduced end-effector deviation in simulations.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种针对机器人操纵器的主动控制层防御机制，用于应对绕过传统异常检测的隐蔽网络攻击，并在仿真中展示了降低末端执行器偏差的效果。

Authors: Gabriele Gualandi, Alessandro V. Papadopoulos

Route Fragmentation Based on Resource-centric Prioritisation for Efficient Multi-Robot Path Planning in Agricultural Environments

Abstract (English): Agricultural environments present high proportions of spatially dense navigation bottlenecks for long-term navigation and operational planning of agricultural mobile robots. The existing agent-centric multi-robot path planning (MRPP) approaches resolve conflicts from the perspective of agents, rather than from the resources under contention. Further, the density of such contentions limits the capabilities of spatial interleaving, a concept that many planners rely on to achieve high throughput. In this work, two variants of the priority-based Fragment Planner (FP) are presented as resource-centric MRPP algorithms that leverage route fragmentation to enable partial route progression and limit the impact of binary-based waiting. These approaches are evaluated in lifelong simulation over a 3.6km topological map representing a commercial polytunnel environment. Their performances are contrasted against 5 baseline algorithms with varying robotic fleet sizes. The Fragment Planners achieved significant gains in throughput compared with Prioritised Planning (PP) and Priority-Based Search (PBS) algorithms. They further demonstrated a task throughput of 95% of the optimal task throughput over the same time period. This work shows that, for long-term deployment of agricultural robots in corridor-dominant agricultural environments, resource-centric MRPP approaches are a necessity for high-efficacy operational planning.

摘要（中文）: 农业环境呈现出高比例的空间密集导航瓶颈，对农业移动机器人的长期导航和运行规划构成挑战。现有的以智能体为中心的多机器人路径规划（MRPP）方法从智能体的角度而非竞争资源的角度解决冲突。此外，此类竞争的密度限制了空间交错的能力，而许多规划器依赖这种能力来实现高吞吐量。本文提出了优先级碎片规划器（FP）的两种变体作为资源中心型的MRPP算法，利用路线碎片化来实现部分路线推进，并限制基于二元等待的影响。这些方法在一个代表商业多拱温室环境的3.6公里拓扑地图上进行了终身模拟评估。它们的性能与5种具有不同机器人数量的基线算法进行了对比。与优先级规划（PP）和基于优先级的搜索（PBS）算法相比，碎片规划器在吞吐量方面取得了显著提升。它们还表现出在同一时间段内达到最佳任务吞吐量95%的任务吞吐量。这项工作表明，对于走廊主导型农业环境中农业机器人的长期部署而言，资源中心型的MRPP方法对于高效的运行规划是必要的。

TLDR: The paper introduces a resource-centric Multi-Robot Path Planning (MRPP) approach called Fragment Planner (FP) for agricultural robots in bottleneck-prone environments, demonstrating significant throughput gains compared to existing methods.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种资源中心的的多机器人路径规划（MRPP）方法，称为碎片规划器（FP），用于在瓶颈多发的农业环境中，相比于现有方法，展示了显著的吞吐量提升。

Authors: James R. Heselden, Gautham P. Das

Coordinated Manipulation of Hybrid Deformable-Rigid Objects in Constrained Environments

Abstract (English): Coordinated robotic manipulation of deformable linear objects (DLOs), such as ropes and cables, has been widely studied; however, handling hybrid assemblies composed of both deformable and rigid elements in constrained environments remains challenging. This work presents a quasi-static optimization-based manipulation planner that employs a strain-based Cosserat rod model, extending rigid-body formulations to hybrid deformable linear objects (hDLO). The proposed planner exploits the compliance of deformable links to maneuver through constraints while achieving task-space objectives for the object that are unreachable with rigid tools. By leveraging a differentiable model with analytically derived gradients, the method achieves up to a 33x speedup over finite-difference baselines for inverse kinetostatic(IKS) problems. Furthermore, the subsequent trajectory optimization problem, warm-started using the IKS solution, is only practically realizable via analytical derivatives. The proposed algorithm is validated in simulation on various hDLO systems and experimentally on a three-link hDLO manipulated in a constrained environment using a dual-arm robotic system. Experimental results confirm the planner's accuracy, yielding an average deformation error of approximately 3 cm (5% of the deformable link length) between the desired and measured marker positions. Finally, the proposed optimal planner is compared against a sampling-based feasibility planner adapted to the strain-based formulation. The results demonstrate the effectiveness and applicability of the proposed approach for robotic manipulation of hybrid assemblies in constrained environments.

摘要（中文）: 对可变形线性对象（DLO）如绳索和电缆的协同机器人操作已被广泛研究；然而，在约束环境中处理由可变形和刚性元件组成的混合组件仍然具有挑战性。本文提出了一种基于准静态优化的操作规划器，该规划器采用基于应变的 Cosserat 杆模型，将刚体公式扩展到混合可变形线性对象（hDLO）。所提出的规划器利用可变形环节的柔顺性，在约束条件下进行操作，以实现刚性工具无法达到的对象在任务空间中的目标。通过利用具有解析导数的可微模型，该方法在逆静力学（IKS）问题上实现了比有限差分基线高达 33 倍的加速。此外，后续的轨迹优化问题，使用 IKS 解进行预热，仅通过解析导数才能实际实现。所提出的算法在各种 hDLO 系统上进行了仿真验证，并在一个使用双臂机器人系统在约束环境中操作的三环节 hDLO 上进行了实验验证。实验结果证实了规划器的准确性，在期望 Marker 位置和测量 Marker 位置之间产生了大约 3 厘米（可变形环节长度的 5%）的平均变形误差。最后，将所提出的最优规划器与适用于基于应变公式的基于采样的可行性规划器进行了比较。结果证明了所提出的方法在约束环境中对混合组件进行机器人操作的有效性和适用性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a quasi-static optimization-based manipulation planner for hybrid deformable-rigid objects (hDLOs) in constrained environments, demonstrating its effectiveness in simulation and real-world experiments with a dual-arm robot.

Authors: Anees Peringal, Anup Teejo Mathew, Panagiotis liatsis, Federico Renda

Consistent and Efficient MSCKF-based LiDAR-Inertial Odometry with Inferred Cluster-to-Plane Constraints for UAVs

Abstract (English): Robust and accurate navigation is critical for Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) especially for those with stringent Size, Weight, and Power (SWaP) constraints. However, most state-of-the-art (SOTA) LiDAR-Inertial Odometry (LIO) systems still suffer from estimation inconsistency and computational bottlenecks when deployed on such platforms. To address these issues, this paper proposes a consistent and efficient tightly-coupled LIO framework tailored for UAVs. Within the efficient Multi-State Constraint Kalman Filter (MSCKF) framework, we build coplanar constraints inferred from planar features observed across a sliding window. By applying null-space projection to sliding-window coplanar constraints, we eliminate the direct dependency on feature parameters in the state vector, thereby mitigating overconfidence and improving consistency. More importantly, to further boost the efficiency, we introduce a parallel voxel-based data association and a novel compact cluster-to-plane measurement model. This compact measurement model losslessly reduces observation dimensionality and significantly accelerating the update process. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that our method outperforms most state-of-the-art (SOTA) approaches by providing a superior balance of consistency and efficiency. It exhibits improved robustness in degenerate scenarios, achieves the lowest memory usage via its map-free nature, and runs in real-time on resource-constrained embedded platforms (e.g., NVIDIA Jetson TX2).

摘要（中文）: 稳健且精确的导航对于无人机（UAV）至关重要，特别是对于那些具有严格尺寸、重量和功耗（SWaP）约束的无人机。然而，大多数最先进的（SOTA）激光雷达-惯性里程计（LIO）系统在部署于此类平台时，仍然面临着估计不一致和计算瓶颈的问题。为了解决这些问题，本文提出了一种为无人机量身定制的一致且高效的紧耦合LIO框架。在高效的多状态约束卡尔曼滤波器（MSCKF）框架内，我们构建了从滑动窗口中观测到的平面特征推断出的共面约束。通过将零空间投影应用于滑动窗口共面约束，我们消除了状态向量中对特征参数的直接依赖性，从而减轻了过度自信并提高了整体一致性。更重要的是，为了进一步提高效率，我们引入了一种基于体素的并行数据关联策略和一个新型的紧凑型簇到平面测量模型。这种紧凑型测量模型无损地降低了观测数据的维度，并显著加速了更新过程。大量的评估表明，我们的方法通过提供一致性和效率之间的卓越平衡，优于大多数最先进的方法。它在退化场景中表现出更高的鲁棒性，通过其无需地图的特性实现了最低的内存使用量，并且可以在资源受限的嵌入式平台（例如，NVIDIA Jetson TX2）上实时运行。

TLDR: This paper presents a novel LiDAR-Inertial Odometry (LIO) framework for UAVs, improving consistency and efficiency by using coplanar constraints, parallel voxel-based data association, and a compact cluster-to-plane measurement model, demonstrating SOTA performance on resource-constrained platforms.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种新的用于无人机的激光雷达惯性里程计（LIO）框架，通过使用共面约束、并行基于体素的数据关联和紧凑的簇到平面测量模型，提高了系统的一致性和效率，并在资源受限的平台上展示了最先进的性能。

Authors: Jinwen Zhu, Xudong Zhao, Fangcheng Zhu, Jun Hu, Shi Jin, Yinian Mao, Guoquan Huang

AoI-FusionNet: Age-Aware Tightly Coupled Fusion of UWB-IMU under Sparse Ranging Conditions

Abstract (English): Accurate motion tracking of snow particles in avalanche events requires robust localization in global navigation satellite system (GNSS)-denied outdoor environments. This paper introduces AoI-FusionNet, a tightly coupled deep learning-based fusion framework that directly combines raw ultra-wideband (UWB) time-of-flight (ToF) measurements with inertial measurement unit (IMU) data for 3D trajectory estimation. Unlike loose-coupled pipelines based on intermediate trilateration, the proposed approach operates directly on heterogeneous sensor inputs, enabling localization even under insufficient ranging availability. The framework integrates an Age-of-Information (AoI)-aware decay module to reduce the influence of stale UWB ranging measurements and a learned attention gating mechanism that adaptively balances the contribution of UWB and IMU modalities based on measurement availability and temporal freshness. To evaluate robustness under limited data and measurement variability, we apply a diffusion-based residual augmentation strategy during training, producing an augmented variant termed AoI-FusionNet-DGAN. We assess the performance of the proposed model using offline post-processing of real-world measurement data collected in an alpine environment and benchmark it against UWB multilateration and loose-coupled fusion baselines. The results demonstrate that AoI-FusionNet substantially reduces mean and tail localization errors under intermittent and degraded sensing conditions.

摘要（中文）: 在雪崩事件中，对雪粒进行精确的运动跟踪需要在全球导航卫星系统（GNSS）拒止的户外环境中进行稳健的定位。本文介绍了一种名为AoI-FusionNet的紧耦合深度学习融合框架，该框架直接将原始超宽带（UWB）飞行时间（ToF）测量数据与惯性测量单元（IMU）数据相结合，用于三维轨迹估计。与基于中间三边测量的松耦合管道不同，所提出的方法直接对异构传感器输入进行操作，即使在测距可用性不足的情况下也能实现定位。该框架集成了一个信息时效性（AoI）感知衰减模块，以减少陈旧UWB测距测量的影响，以及一个学习到的注意力门控机制，该机制根据测量可用性和时间新鲜度自适应地平衡UWB和IMU模态的贡献。为了评估在有限数据和测量可变性下的鲁棒性，我们在训练过程中应用了基于扩散的残差增强策略，产生了一个增强型变体，称为AoI-FusionNet-DGAN。我们使用在高山环境中收集的真实世界测量数据的离线后处理来评估所提出模型的性能，并将其与UWB多边测量和松耦合融合基线进行基准测试。结果表明，在间歇性和退化感知条件下，AoI-FusionNet显著降低了平均和尾部定位误差。

TLDR: The paper introduces AoI-FusionNet, a deep learning framework that tightly couples UWB and IMU data for robust 3D trajectory estimation in GNSS-denied environments, particularly addressing the challenges of sparse ranging and stale measurements.

Authors: Tehmina Bibi, Anselm Köhler, Jan-Thomas Fischer, Falko Dressler

Motion-Specific Battery Health Assessment for Quadrotors Using High-Fidelity Battery Models

Abstract (English): Quadrotor endurance is ultimately limited by battery behavior, yet most energy aware planning treats the battery as a simple energy reservoir and overlooks how flight motions induce dynamic current loads that accelerate battery degradation. This work presents an end to end framework for motion aware battery health assessment in quadrotors. We first design a wide range current sensing module to capture motion specific current profiles during real flights, preserving transient features. In parallel, a high fidelity battery model is calibrated using reference performance tests and a metaheuristic based on a degradation coupled electrochemical model.By simulating measured flight loads in the calibrated model, we systematically resolve how different flight motions translate into degradation modes loss of lithium inventory and loss of active material as well as internal side reactions. The results demonstrate that even when two flight profiles consume the same average energy, their transient load structures can drive different degradation pathways, emphasizing the need for motion-aware battery management that balances efficiency with battery degradation.

摘要（中文）: 四旋翼的续航最终受限于电池性能，然而，大多数能量感知规划将电池视为一个简单的能量储存器，忽略了飞行运动如何产生动态电流负载，从而加速电池衰减。本研究提出了一种端到端的框架，用于四旋翼中运动感知的电池健康评估。首先，我们设计了一个宽范围电流传感模块，以捕捉真实飞行中特定于运动的电流曲线，保留瞬态特征。同时，我们使用参考性能测试和一个基于退化耦合电化学模型的元启发式算法，校准了一个高保真电池模型。通过在校准后的模型中模拟测量的飞行负载，我们系统地解析了不同的飞行运动如何转化为退化模式：锂库存损失、活性材料损失以及内部副反应。结果表明，即使两种飞行轨迹消耗相同的平均能量，它们的瞬态负载结构也会驱动不同的退化路径，强调了运动感知的电池管理的需求，需要在效率和电池退化之间取得平衡。

TLDR: This paper presents a framework for motion-aware battery health assessment in quadrotors, showing that different flight motions, even with the same average energy consumption, lead to different degradation pathways. It emphasizes the need for motion-aware battery management.

简要说明: 本文提出了一个无人机运动感知的电池健康评估框架，表明即使平均能量消耗相同，不同的飞行运动也会导致不同的退化途径。强调了运动感知电池管理的必要性。

Authors: Joonhee Kim, Sanghyun Park, Donghyeong Kim, Eunseon Choi, Soohee Han

Push, Press, Slide: Mode-Aware Planar Contact Manipulation via Reduced-Order Models

Abstract (English): Non-prehensile planar manipulation, including pushing and press-and-slide, is critical for diverse robotic tasks, but notoriously challenging due to hybrid contact mechanics, under-actuation, and asymmetric friction limits that traditionally necessitate computationally expensive iterative control. In this paper, we propose a mode-aware framework for planar manipulation with one or two robotic arms based on contact topology selection and reduced-order kinematic modeling. Our core insight is that complex wrench-twist limit surface mechanics can be abstracted into a discrete library of physically intuitive models. We systematically map various single-arm and bimanual contact topologies to simple non-holonomic formulations, e.g. unicycle for simplified press-and-slide motion. By anchoring trajectory generation to these reduced-order models, our framework computes the required object wrench and distributes feasible, friction-bounded contact forces via a direct algebraic allocator. We incorporate manipulator kinematics to ensure long-horizon feasibility and demonstrate our fast, optimization-free approach in simulation across diverse single-arm and bimanual manipulation tasks.

摘要（中文）: 非抓取式平面操控，包括推和压滑，对于各种机器人任务至关重要，但由于混合接触力学、欠驱动以及非对称摩擦极限等原因，极具挑战性，传统上需要计算成本高昂的迭代控制。在本文中，我们提出了一种基于接触拓扑选择和降阶运动学建模的、具有一个或两个机器人手臂的平面操控模式感知框架。我们的核心思想是将复杂的力-扭矩极限面力学抽象为一个物理直观模型的离散库。我们系统地将各种单臂和双臂接触拓扑映射到简单的非完整约束公式，例如用于简化压滑运动的独轮车模型。通过将轨迹生成锚定到这些降阶模型，我们的框架计算所需的目标力矩，并通过直接代数分配器分配可行且摩擦有界的接触力。我们结合了机械臂运动学以确保长时域可行性，并在仿真中通过各种单臂和双臂操控任务展示了我们快速且无需优化的方法。

TLDR: This paper presents a mode-aware framework for planar manipulation using robotic arms, leveraging reduced-order kinematic models to simplify control and enable fast, optimization-free trajectory generation for tasks like pushing and press-and-slide.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于降阶运动学模型的平面操作模式识别框架，利用机器人手臂简化控制，并为诸如推和按压滑动等任务实现快速、无优化的轨迹生成。

Authors: Melih Özcan, Ozgur S. Oguz, Umut Orguner

FC-Track: Overlap-Aware Post-Association Correction for Online Multi-Object Tracking

Abstract (English): Reliable multi-object tracking (MOT) is essential for robotic systems operating in complex and dynamic environments. Despite recent advances in detection and association, online MOT methods remain vulnerable to identity switches caused by frequent occlusions and object overlap, where incorrect associations can propagate over time and degrade tracking reliability. We present a lightweight post-association correction framework (FC-Track) for online MOT that explicitly targets overlap-induced mismatches during inference. The proposed method suppresses unreliable appearance updates under high-overlap conditions using an Intersection over Area (IoA)-based filtering strategy, and locally corrects detection-to-tracklet mismatches through appearance similarity comparison within overlapped tracklet pairs. By preventing short-term mismatches from propagating, our framework effectively mitigates long-term identity switches without resorting to global optimization or re-identification. The framework operates online without global optimization or re-identification, making it suitable for real-time robotic applications. We achieve 81.73 MOTA, 82.81 IDF1, and 66.95 HOTA on the MOT17 test set with a running speed of 5.7 FPS, and 77.52 MOTA, 80.90 IDF1, and 65.67 HOTA on the MOT20 test set with a running speed of 0.6 FPS. Specifically, our framework FC-Track produces only 29.55% long-term identity switches, which is substantially lower than existing online trackers. Meanwhile, our framework maintains state-of-the-art performance on the MOT20 benchmark.

摘要（中文）: 可靠的多目标跟踪（MOT）对于在复杂和动态环境中运行的机器人系统至关重要。尽管检测和关联方面取得了近期的进展，但在线MOT方法仍然容易受到频繁遮挡和目标重叠导致的身份切换的影响，其中不正确的关联会随着时间的推移而传播并降低跟踪的可靠性。我们提出了一种轻量级的后关联校正框架（FC-Track），用于在线MOT，该框架在推理过程中明确针对重叠引起的错误匹配。该方法使用基于面积交并比（IoA）的过滤策略来抑制高重叠条件下的不可靠外观更新，并通过重叠轨迹对内的外观相似性比较来局部地校正检测到轨迹的错误匹配。通过防止短期错误匹配的传播，我们的框架有效地减少了长期身份切换，而无需诉诸全局优化或重识别。该框架在线运行，无需全局优化或重识别，使其适用于实时机器人应用。我们在MOT17测试集上实现了81.73 MOTA、82.81 IDF1和66.95 HOTA，运行速度为5.7 FPS；在MOT20测试集上实现了77.52 MOTA、80.90 IDF1和65.67 HOTA，运行速度为0.6 FPS。具体而言，我们的框架FC-Track仅产生29.55％的长期身份切换，远低于现有的在线跟踪器。同时，我们的框架在MOT20基准测试中保持了最先进的性能。

TLDR: This paper introduces FC-Track, a lightweight post-association correction framework for online multi-object tracking that addresses identity switches caused by occlusions and object overlap, achieving state-of-the-art performance on MOT benchmarks.

简要说明: 本文介绍了一种轻量级的后关联校正框架FC-Track，用于在线多目标跟踪，旨在解决由遮挡和对象重叠导致的身份切换问题，并在MOT基准测试中取得了最先进的性能。

Authors: Cheng Ju, Zejing Zhao, Akio Namiki

CMHANet: A Cross-Modal Hybrid Attention Network for Point Cloud Registration

Abstract (English): Robust point cloud registration is a fundamental task in 3D computer vision and geometric deep learning, essential for applications such as large-scale 3D reconstruction, augmented reality, and scene understanding. However, the performance of established learning-based methods often degrades in complex, real world scenarios characterized by incomplete data, sensor noise, and low overlap regions. To address these limitations, we propose CMHANet, a novel Cross-Modal Hybrid Attention Network. Our method integrates the fusion of rich contextual information from 2D images with the geometric detail of 3D point clouds, yielding a comprehensive and resilient feature representation. Furthermore, we introduce an innovative optimization function based on contrastive learning, which enforces geometric consistency and significantly improves the model's robustness to noise and partial observations. We evaluated CMHANet on the 3DMatch and the challenging 3DLoMatch datasets. \rev{Additionally, zero-shot evaluations on the TUM RGB-D SLAM dataset verify the model's generalization capability to unseen domains.} The experimental results demonstrate that our method achieves substantial improvements in both registration accuracy and overall robustness, outperforming current techniques. We also release our code in \href{https://github.com/DongXu-Zhang/CMHANet}{https://github.com/DongXu-Zhang/CMHANet}.

摘要（中文）: 稳健的点云配准是三维计算机视觉和几何深度学习中的一项基础任务，对于大规模三维重建、增强现实和场景理解等应用至关重要。然而，在复杂、真实世界的场景中，由于数据不完整、传感器噪声和低重叠区域等因素，现有基于学习的方法的性能往往会下降。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了一种新颖的跨模态混合注意力网络CMHANet。我们的方法集成了来自二维图像的丰富上下文信息与三维点云的几何细节，从而产生全面且具有弹性的特征表示。此外，我们引入了一种基于对比学习的创新优化函数，该函数强制执行几何一致性，并显著提高模型对噪声和部分观测的鲁棒性。我们在3DMatch和具有挑战性的3DLoMatch数据集上评估了CMHANet。\rev{此外，在TUM RGB-D SLAM数据集上的零样本评估验证了模型对未见领域的泛化能力。} 实验结果表明，我们的方法在配准精度和整体鲁棒性方面都取得了显著的提升，优于当前的技术。我们也在\href{https://github.com/DongXu-Zhang/CMHANet}{https://github.com/DongXu-Zhang/CMHANet} 上发布了我们的代码。

TLDR: The paper introduces CMHANet, a cross-modal hybrid attention network for robust point cloud registration, which integrates 2D image features with 3D point cloud geometry and uses contrastive learning for improved robustness. It shows strong performance on standard datasets and good generalization ability.
