Authors: Dongxu Zhang, Yingsen Wang, Yiding Sun, Haoran Xu, Peilin Fan, Jihua Zhu

Spectral-Geometric Neural Fields for Pose-Free LiDAR View Synthesis

Abstract (English): Neural Radiance Fields (NeRF) have shown remarkable success in image novel view synthesis (NVS), inspiring extensions to LiDAR NVS. However, most methods heavily rely on accurate camera poses for scene reconstruction. The sparsity and textureless nature of LiDAR data also present distinct challenges, leading to geometric holes and discontinuous surfaces. To address these issues, we propose SG-NLF, a pose-free LiDAR NeRF framework that integrates spectral information with geometric consistency. Specifically, we design a hybrid representation based on spectral priors to reconstruct smooth geometry. For pose optimization, we construct a confidence-aware graph based on feature compatibility to achieve global alignment. In addition, an adversarial learning strategy is introduced to enforce cross-frame consistency, thereby enhancing reconstruction quality. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework, especially in challenging low-frequency scenarios. Compared to previous state-of-the-art methods, SG-NLF improves reconstruction quality and pose accuracy by over 35.8% and 68.8%. Our work can provide a novel perspective for LiDAR view synthesis.

Coherent Human-Scene Reconstruction from Multi-Person Multi-View Video in a Single Pass

Abstract (English): Recent advances in 3D foundation models have led to growing interest in reconstructing humans and their surrounding environments. However, most existing approaches focus on monocular inputs, and extending them to multi-view settings requires additional overhead modules or preprocessed data. To this end, we present CHROMM, a unified framework that jointly estimates cameras, scene point clouds, and human meshes from multi-person multi-view videos without relying on external modules or preprocessing. We integrate strong geometric and human priors from Pi3X and Multi-HMR into a single trainable neural network architecture, and introduce a scale adjustment module to solve the scale discrepancy between humans and the scene. We also introduce a multi-view fusion strategy to aggregate per-view estimates into a single representation at test-time. Finally, we propose a geometry-based multi-person association method, which is more robust than appearance-based approaches. Experiments on EMDB, RICH, EgoHumans, and EgoExo4D show that CHROMM achieves competitive performance in global human motion and multi-view pose estimation while running over 8x faster than prior optimization-based multi-view approaches. Authors: Sangmin Kim, Minhyuk Hwang, Geonho Cha, Dongyoon Wee, Jaesik Park

Prompt-Driven Lightweight Foundation Model for Instance Segmentation-Based Fault Detection in Freight Trains

Abstract (English): Accurate visual fault detection in freight trains remains a critical challenge for intelligent transportation system maintenance, due to complex operational environments, structurally repetitive components, and frequent occlusions or contaminations in safety-critical regions. Conventional instance segmentation methods based on convolutional neural networks and Transformers often suffer from poor generalization and limited boundary accuracy under such conditions. To address these challenges, we propose a lightweight self-prompted instance segmentation framework tailored for freight train fault detection. Our method leverages the Segment Anything Model by introducing a self-prompt generation module that automatically produces task-specific prompts, enabling effective knowledge transfer from foundation models to domain-specific inspection tasks. In addition, we adopt a Tiny Vision Transformer backbone to reduce computational cost, making the framework suitable for real-time deployment on edge devices in railway monitoring systems. We construct a domain-specific dataset collected from real-world freight inspection stations and conduct extensive evaluations. Experimental results show that our method achieves 74.6 $AP^{\text{box}}$ and 74.2 $AP^{\text{mask}}$ on the dataset, outperforming existing state-of-the-art methods in both accuracy and robustness while maintaining low computational overhead. This work offers a deployable and efficient vision solution for automated freight train inspection, demonstrating the potential of foundation model adaptation in industrial-scale fault diagnosis scenarios. Project page: https://github.com/MVME-HBUT/SAM_FTI-FDet.git

Authors: Guodong Sun, Qihang Liang, Xingyu Pan, Moyun Liu, Yang Zhang

MRGeo: Robust Cross-View Geo-Localization of Corrupted Images via Spatial and Channel Feature Enhancement

Abstract (English): Cross-view geo-localization (CVGL) aims to accurately localize street-view images through retrieval of corresponding geo-tagged satellite images. While prior works have achieved nearly perfect performance on certain standard datasets, their robustness in real-world corrupted environments remains under-explored. This oversight causes severe performance degradation or failure when images are affected by corruption such as blur or weather, significantly limiting practical deployment. To address this critical gap, we introduce MRGeo, the first systematic method designed for robust CVGL under corruption. MRGeo employs a hierarchical defense strategy that enhances the intrinsic quality of features and then enforces a robust geometric prior. Its core is the Spatial-Channel Enhancement Block, which contains: (1) a Spatial Adaptive Representation Module that models global and local features in parallel and uses a dynamic gating mechanism to arbitrate their fusion based on feature reliability; and (2) a Channel Calibration Module that performs compensatory adjustments by modeling multi-granularity channel dependencies to counteract information loss. To prevent spatial misalignment under severe corruption, a Region-level Geometric Alignment Module imposes a geometric structure on the final descriptors, ensuring coarse-grained consistency. Comprehensive experiments on both robustness benchmark and standard datasets demonstrate that MRGeo not only achieves an average R@1 improvement of 2.92\% across three comprehensive robustness benchmarks (CVUSA-C-ALL, CVACT\_val-C-ALL, and CVACT\_test-C-ALL) but also establishes superior performance in cross-area evaluation, thereby demonstrating its robustness and generalization capability.

摘要（中文）: 跨视角地理定位（CVGL）旨在通过检索相应的带有地理标签的卫星图像来精确定位街景图像。 尽管先前的工作在某些标准数据集上几乎实现了完美的性能，但它们在真实世界受损环境中的鲁棒性仍未得到充分研究。 这种疏忽会导致当图像受到诸如模糊或天气等损坏影响时，性能严重下降或失效，从而大大限制了其实际部署。 为了解决这个关键缺口，我们引入了MRGeo，这是第一个为应对损坏下的鲁棒性 CVGL 而设计的系统方法。 MRGeo 采用分层防御策略，增强特征的内在质量，然后强制执行鲁棒的几何先验。 它的核心是空间-通道增强块，它包含：（1）空间自适应表示模块，该模块并行建模全局和局部特征，并使用动态门控机制根据特征可靠性来仲裁它们的融合；以及（2）通道校准模块，该模块通过建模多粒度通道依赖性来执行补偿调整，以抵消信息丢失。 为了防止在严重损坏下的空间错位，区域级几何对齐模块将几何结构施加到最终描述符上，从而确保粗粒度的一致性。 在鲁棒性基准和标准数据集上的综合实验表明，MRGeo 不仅在三个综合鲁棒性基准（CVUSA-C-ALL、CVACT_val-C-ALL 和 CVACT_test-C-ALL）上实现了平均 2.92% 的 R@1 提升，而且还在跨区域评估中建立了卓越的性能，从而证明了其鲁棒性和泛化能力。

TLDR: The paper introduces MRGeo, a method for robust cross-view geo-localization (CVGL) that addresses performance degradation in corrupted images by enhancing feature quality and enforcing geometric priors.

简要说明: 本文介绍了MRGeo，一种鲁棒的跨视角地理定位（CVGL）方法，通过增强特征质量和强制执行几何先验来解决在损坏图像中性能下降的问题。

Authors: Le Wu, Lv Bo, Songsong Ouyang, Yingying Zhu

CalliMaster: Mastering Page-level Chinese Calligraphy via Layout-guided Spatial Planning

Abstract (English): Page-level calligraphy synthesis requires balancing glyph precision with layout composition. Existing character models lack spatial context, while page-level methods often compromise brushwork detail. In this paper, we present \textbf{CalliMaster}, a unified framework for controllable generation and editing that resolves this conflict by decoupling spatial planning from content synthesis. Inspired by the human cognitive process of ``planning before writing'', we introduce a coarse-to-fine pipeline \textbf{(Text $\rightarrow$ Layout $\rightarrow$ Image)} to tackle the combinatorial complexity of page-scale synthesis. Operating within a single Multimodal Diffusion Transformer, a spatial planning stage first predicts character bounding boxes to establish the global spatial arrangement. This intermediate layout then serves as a geometric prompt for the content synthesis stage, where the same network utilizes flow-matching to render high-fidelity brushwork. Beyond achieving state-of-the-art generation quality, this disentanglement supports versatile downstream capabilities. By treating the layout as a modifiable constraint, CalliMaster enables controllable semantic re-planning: users can resize or reposition characters while the model automatically harmonizes the surrounding void space and brush momentum. Furthermore, we demonstrate the framework's extensibility to artifact restoration and forensic analysis, providing a comprehensive tool for digital cultural heritage.

摘要（中文）: 页面级书法合成需要在字形精度与布局构图之间取得平衡。现有的字符模型缺乏空间上下文信息，而页面级方法通常会牺牲笔画细节。在本文中，我们提出了一种统一的、可控的书法生成和编辑框架 \textbf{CalliMaster}，通过将空间规划与内容合成解耦来解决这一冲突。受到人类“先规划后书写”认知过程的启发，我们引入了一个由粗到精的流程 \textbf{(文本 $\rightarrow$ 布局 $\rightarrow$ 图像)}，以应对页面尺度合成的组合复杂性。在一个单一的多模态扩散Transformer中运作，空间规划阶段首先预测字符边界框，以建立全局空间布局。这个中间布局随后作为内容合成阶段的几何提示，在该阶段，同一网络利用流匹配（flow-matching）来渲染高保真的笔画。除了实现最先进的生成质量外，这种解耦还支持多种下游功能。通过将布局视为可修改的约束，CalliMaster 实现了可控的语义重规划：用户可以调整字符大小或重新定位字符，而模型会自动协调周围的空白空间和笔势连贯性。此外，我们还展示了该框架在文物修复和取证分析方面的可扩展性，为数字文化遗产提供了一个全面的工具。

TLDR: CalliMaster is a unified framework for generating and editing page-level Chinese calligraphy by decoupling spatial layout planning from content synthesis using a Multimodal Diffusion Transformer in a coarse-to-fine pipeline.

简要说明: CalliMaster是一个统一的框架，用于生成和编辑页面级中国书法，通过使用多模态扩散变换器，将空间布局规划与内容合成解耦，采用由粗到精的流程。

Authors: Tianshuo Xu, Tiantian Hong, Zhifei Chen, Fei Chao, Ying-cong Chen

Human-AI Collaborative Autonomous Experimentation With Proxy Modeling for Comparative Observation

Abstract (English): Optimization for different tasks like material characterization, synthesis, and functional properties for desired applications over multi-dimensional control parameters need a rapid strategic search through active learning such as Bayesian optimization (BO). However, such high-dimensional experimental physical descriptors are complex and noisy, from which realization of a low-dimensional mathematical scalar metrics or objective functions can be erroneous. Moreover, in traditional purely data-driven autonomous exploration, such objective functions often ignore the subtle variation and key features of the physical descriptors, thereby can fail to discover unknown phenomenon of the material systems. To address this, here we present a proxy-modelled Bayesian optimization (px-BO) via on-the-fly teaming between human and AI agents. Over the loop of BO, instead of defining a mathematical objective function directly from the experimental data, we introduce a voting system on the fly where the new experimental outcome will be compared with existing experiments, and the human agents will choose the preferred samples. These human-guided comparisons are then transformed into a proxy-based objective function via fitting Bradley-Terry (BT) model. Then, to minimize human interaction, this iteratively trained proxy model also acts as an AI agent for future surrogate human votes. Finally, these surrogate votes are periodically validated by human agents, and the corrections are then learned by the proxy model on-the-fly. We demonstrated the performance of the proposed px-BO framework into simulated and BEPS data generated from PTO sample. We find that our approach provided better control of the domain experts for an improved search over traditional data-driven exploration, thus, signifies the importance of human-AI teaming in an accelerated and meaningful material space exploration.

摘要（中文）: 在多维控制参数下，针对材料表征、合成和所需应用的功能特性等不同任务进行优化，需要通过主动学习（例如贝叶斯优化（BO））进行快速战略搜索。然而，这种高维实验物理描述符是复杂且嘈杂的，从中实现低维数学标量度量或目标函数可能会出错。此外，在传统的纯数据驱动自主探索中，这种目标函数通常忽略物理描述符的细微变化和关键特征，因此可能无法发现材料系统的未知现象。为了解决这个问题，本文提出了一种通过人在环人工智能代理的即时协作的代理模型贝叶斯优化（px-BO）。在贝叶斯优化的循环中，我们没有直接从实验数据定义数学目标函数，而是引入了一个即时投票系统，新实验结果将与现有实验进行比较，人类代理将选择更优选的样本。然后，这些人工指导的比较通过拟合 Bradley-Terry（BT）模型转化为基于代理的目标函数。然后，为了最大限度地减少人机交互，这种迭代训练的代理模型也充当人工智能代理，用于未来的替代人工投票。最后，这些替代投票会定期由人类代理进行验证，并且修正会被代理模型即时学习。我们通过模拟和从 PTO 样品生成的 BEPS 数据验证了所提出的 px-BO 框架的性能。我们发现，与传统的数据驱动探索相比，我们的方法为领域专家提供了更好的控制，从而改善了搜索效果，因此，突显了人机协作在加速和有意义的材料空间探索中的重要性。

TLDR: This paper introduces a human-AI collaborative Bayesian optimization (px-BO) framework for material discovery, leveraging human input to guide the optimization process by comparing experimental outcomes, which are then learned by a proxy model to minimize human interaction.

简要说明: 该论文介绍了一种人机协作的贝叶斯优化（px-BO）框架，用于材料发现。该框架利用人类输入来指导优化过程，通过比较实验结果，并由代理模型学习，以最大限度地减少人工干预。

Authors: Arpan Biswas, Hiroshi Funakubo, Yongtao Liu

A Learning-Based Approach for Contact Detection, Localization, and Force Estimation of Continuum Manipulators With Integrated OFDR Optical Fiber

Abstract (English): Continuum manipulators (CMs) are widely used in minimally invasive procedures due to their compliant structure and ability to navigate deep and confined anatomical environments. However, their distributed deformation makes force sensing, contact detection, localization, and force estimation challenging, particularly when interactions occur at unknown arc-length locations along the robot. To address this problem, we propose a cascade learning-based framework (CLF) for CMs instrumented with a single distributed Optical Frequency Domain Reflectometry (OFDR) fiber embedded along one side of the robot. The OFDR sensor provides dense strain measurements along the manipulator backbone, capturing strain perturbations caused by external interactions. The proposed CLF first detects contact using a Gradient Boosting classifier and then estimates contact location and interaction force magnitude using a CNN--FiLM model that predicts a spatial force distribution along the manipulator. Experimental validation on a sensorized tendon-driven CM in an obstructed environment demonstrates that a single distributed OFDR fiber provides sufficient information to jointly infer contact occurrence, location, and force in continuum manipulators.

摘要（中文）: 连续体机械臂（CMs）因其柔顺的结构和在狭窄、深入的解剖环境中导航的能力而被广泛应用于微创手术。然而，其分布式变形使得力感测、接触检测、定位和力估计具有挑战性，尤其是在机器人沿弧长未知位置发生交互时。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种基于级联学习的框架（CLF），用于配备单根分布式光频域反射（OFDR）光纤的连续体机械臂，该光纤嵌入在机器人的一侧。OFDR传感器提供沿机械臂主干的密集应变测量，捕捉由外部交互引起的应变扰动。所提出的CLF首先使用梯度提升分类器检测接触，然后使用CNN--FiLM模型估计接触位置和交互力的大小，该模型预测沿机械臂的空间力分布。在一个受阻环境中的传感器化肌腱驱动连续体机械臂上的实验验证表明，单根分布式OFDR光纤提供了足够的信息，用于联合推断连续体机械臂中接触的发生、位置和力。

TLDR: This paper presents a cascade learning framework utilizing OFDR fiber for contact detection, localization, and force estimation in continuum manipulators, demonstrating successful application in an obstructed environment.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种级联学习框架，利用OFDR光纤来实现连续体机械臂的接触检测、定位和力估计，并在障碍环境中成功进行了应用演示。

Authors: Mobina Tavangarifard, Jonathan S. Kacines, Qiyu Li, Farshid Alambeigi

SortScrews: A Dataset and Baseline for Real-time Screw Classification

Abstract (English): Automatic identification of screw types is important for industrial automation, robotics, and inventory management. However, publicly available datasets for screw classification are scarce, particularly for controlled single-object scenarios commonly encountered in automated sorting systems. In this work, we introduce $\textbf{SortScrews}$, a dataset for casewise visual classification of screws. The dataset contains 560 RGB images at $512\times512$ resolution covering six screw types and a background class. Images are captured using a standardized acquisition setup and include mild variations in lighting and camera perspective across four capture settings. To facilitate reproducible research and dataset expansion, we also provide a reusable data collection script that allows users to easily construct similar datasets for custom hardware components using inexpensive camera setups. We establish baseline results using transfer learning with EfficientNet-B0 and ResNet-18 classifiers pretrained on ImageNet. In addition, we conduct a well-explored failure analysis. Despite the limited dataset size, these lightweight models achieve strong classification accuracy, demonstrating that controlled acquisition conditions enable effective learning even with relatively small datasets. The dataset, collection pipeline, and baseline training code are publicly available at https://github.com/ATATC/SortScrews.

摘要（中文）: 螺钉类型的自动识别对于工业自动化、机器人技术和库存管理至关重要。然而，公开可用的螺钉分类数据集稀缺，尤其是在自动化分拣系统中常见的受控单物体场景的数据集。在这项工作中，我们推出了 $\textbf{SortScrews}$，一个用于螺钉的按实例视觉分类的数据集。该数据集包含 560 张分辨率为 $512\times512$ 的 RGB 图像，涵盖六种螺钉类型和一个背景类别。图像采用标准化的采集设置捕获，并在四种采集设置中包含光照和相机透视的轻微变化。 为了方便可重复的研究和数据集扩展，我们还提供了一个可重用的数据收集脚本，允许用户使用廉价的相机设置轻松构建类似的数据集，用于自定义硬件组件。 我们使用在 ImageNet 上预训练的 EfficientNet-B0 和 ResNet-18 分类器，通过迁移学习建立了基线结果。此外，我们进行了一项充分探索的失效分析。尽管数据集规模有限，但这些轻量级模型实现了强大的分类准确率，表明受控的采集条件即使在相对较小的数据集也能实现有效的学习。数据集、收集流程和基线训练代码已在 https://github.com/ATATC/SortScrews 上公开。

TLDR: The paper introduces SortScrews, a new dataset for screw classification with corresponding data collection scripts and baseline results using transfer learning. It aims to facilitate research in industrial automation and robotics via a controlled single-object scenario.

Authors: Tianhao Fu, Bingxuan Yang, Juncheng Guo, Shrena Sribalan, Yucheng Chen

On Using Machine Learning to Early Detect Catastrophic Failures in Marine Diesel Engines

Abstract (English): Catastrophic failures of marine engines imply severe loss of functionality and destroy or damage the systems irreversibly. Being sudden and often unpredictable events, they pose a severe threat to navigation, crew, and passengers. The abrupt nature makes early detection the only effective countermeasure. However, research has concentrated on modeling the gradual degradation of components, with limited attention to sudden and anomalous phenomena. This work proposes a new method for early detection of catastrophic failures. Based on real data from a failed engine, the approach evaluates the derivatives of the deviation between actual sensor readings and expected values of engine variables. Predictions are obtained by a Random Forest, which is the most suitable Machine Learning algorithm among the tested ones. Traditional methods focus on deviations of monitored signals, whereas the proposed approach employs the derivatives of the deviations to provide earlier indications of abnormal dynamics, and to alert that a rapid and dangerous event is breaking out within the system. The method allows the detection of anomalies before measurements reach critical thresholds and alarms are triggered, which is the common method in industry. Consequently, operators can be warned in advance and shut down the engine, then prevent damage and unexpected power loss. Moreover, they have the time to safely change the ship route and avoid potential obstacles. Simulation results conf irm the effectiveness of the proposed approach in anticipating occurrence of catastrophic failures. Validation on real-world data further reinforces the robustness and practical applicability of the method. It is worth noting that data acquisition to train the predictive algorithm is not a problem, since a Deep Learning-based data augmentation procedure is used.

摘要（中文）: 海洋发动机的灾难性故障意味着严重的性能损失，并不可逆地破坏或损坏系统。这些故障通常是突然且难以预测的事件，对航行、船员和乘客构成严重威胁。由于其突发性，早期检测是唯一有效的应对措施。然而，以往的研究主要集中于对组件的逐渐退化进行建模，而对突发和异常现象关注有限。本文提出了一种用于早期检测灾难性故障的新方法。该方法基于来自故障发动机的真实数据，评估实际传感器读数与发动机变量的预期值之间偏差的导数。预测结果由随机森林算法获得，在测试的机器学习算法中，它是最合适的。传统方法侧重于监测信号的偏差，而本文提出的方法利用偏差的导数，以更早地提供异常动态的指示，并警惕系统内正在爆发的快速且危险的事件。该方法能够在测量值达到临界阈值并触发警报之前检测到异常，而这在工业界是一种常见的做法。因此，操作人员可以提前得到警告并关闭发动机，从而防止损坏和意外的功率损失。此外，他们有时间安全地改变船舶航线，避免潜在障碍。仿真结果证实了所提出的方法在预测灾难性故障发生方面的有效性。在真实世界数据上的验证进一步增强了该方法的稳健性和实际应用性。值得注意的是，用于训练预测算法的数据采集不成问题，因为使用了基于深度学习的数据增强程序。

TLDR: This paper proposes a machine learning method using Random Forest to detect catastrophic failures in marine diesel engines by analyzing the derivatives of deviations between actual and expected sensor readings. The method aims to provide earlier warnings compared to traditional threshold-based methods, enabling preventative actions.

简要说明: 本文提出了一种基于随机森林的机器学习方法，通过分析实际传感器读数与预期值的偏差导数来检测船用柴油发动机的灾难性故障。 该方法旨在提供比传统的基于阈值的方法更早的警告，从而能够采取预防措施。

Authors: Francesco Maione, Paolo Lino, Giuseppe Giannino, Guido Maione

Optimizing Task Completion Time Updates Using POMDPs

Abstract (English): Managing announced task completion times is a fundamental control problem in project management. While extensive research exists on estimating task durations and task scheduling, the problem of when and how to update completion times communicated to stakeholders remains understudied. Organizations must balance announcement accuracy against the costs of frequent timeline updates, which can erode stakeholder trust and trigger costly replanning. Despite the prevalence of this problem, current approaches rely on static predictions or ad-hoc policies that fail to account for the sequential nature of announcement management. In this paper, we formulate the task announcement problem as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) where the control policy must decide when to update announced completion times based on noisy observations of true task completion. Since most state variables (current time and previous announcements) are fully observable, we leverage the Mixed Observability MDP (MOMDP) framework to enable more efficient policy optimization. Our reward structure captures the dual costs of announcement errors and update frequency, enabling synthesis of optimal announcement control policies. Using off-the-shelf solvers, we generate policies that act as feedback controllers, adaptively managing announcements based on belief state evolution. Simulation results demonstrate significant improvements in both accuracy and announcement stability compared to baseline strategies, achieving up to 75\% reduction in unnecessary updates while maintaining or improving prediction accuracy.

摘要（中文）: 管理已宣布的任务完成时间是项目管理中一项基本的控制问题。尽管存在大量关于估计任务持续时间和任务调度的研究，但关于何时以及如何更新传达给利益相关者的完成时间的问题仍然缺乏研究。组织必须平衡公告的准确性与频繁更新时间线的成本，频繁更新会削弱利益相关者的信任并触发代价高昂的重新计划。尽管这个问题普遍存在，但目前的方法依赖于静态预测或临时策略，而未能考虑到公告管理的顺序性。在本文中，我们将任务公告问题建模为一个部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），在该过程中，控制策略必须根据对实际任务完成时间的噪声观察来决定何时更新已宣布的完成时间。由于大多数状态变量（当前时间和先前的公告）是完全可观察的，因此我们利用混合可观察性MDP（MOMDP）框架来实现更高效的策略优化。我们的奖励结构捕获了公告错误和更新频率的双重成本，从而能够合成最佳的公告控制策略。使用现成的求解器，我们生成了作为反馈控制器运行的策略，从而能够基于信念状态的演化自适应地管理公告。与基线策略相比，仿真结果表明在准确性和公告稳定性方面都有显著提高，在保持或提高预测准确性的同时，不必要的更新减少了高达75%。

TLDR: This paper formulates the problem of updating task completion times in project management as a POMDP/MOMDP and demonstrates improved accuracy and reduced update frequency compared to baseline strategies through simulations.

简要说明: 本文将项目管理中更新任务完成时间的问题建模为POMDP/MOMDP，并通过模拟结果表明，与基线策略相比，该方法提高了准确性并减少了更新频率。

Authors: Duncan Eddy, Esen Yel, Emma Passmore, Niles Egan, Grayson Armour, Dylan M. Asmar, Mykel J. Kochenderfer

Rooftop Wind Field Reconstruction Using Sparse Sensors: From Deterministic to Generative Learning Methods

Abstract (English): Real-time rooftop wind-speed distribution is important for the safe operation of drones and urban air mobility systems, wind control systems, and rooftop utilization. However, rooftop flows show strong nonlinearity, separation, and cross-direction variability, which make flow field reconstruction from sparse sensors difficult. This study develops a learning-from-observation framework using wind-tunnel experimental data obtained by Particle Image Velocimetry (PIV) and compares Kriging interpolation with three deep learning models: UNet, Vision Transformer Autoencoder (ViTAE), and Conditional Wasserstein GAN (CWGAN). We evaluate two training strategies, single wind-direction training (SDT) and mixed wind-direction training (MDT), across sensor densities from 5 to 30, test robustness under sensor position perturbations of plus or minus 1 grid, and optimize sensor placement via Proper Orthogonal Decomposition with QR decomposition. Results show that deep learning methods can reconstruct rooftop wind fields from sparse sensor data effectively. Compared with Kriging interpolation, the deep learning models improved SSIM by up to 32.7%, FAC2 by 24.2%, and NMSE by 27.8%. Mixed wind-direction training further improved performance, with gains of up to 173.7% in SSIM, 16.7% in FAC2, and 98.3% in MG compared with single-direction training. The results also show that sensor configuration, optimization, and training strategy should be considered jointly for reliable deployment. QR-based optimization improved robustness by up to 27.8% under sensor perturbations, although with metric-dependent trade-offs. Training on experimental rather than simulated data also provides practical guidance for method selection and sensor placement in different scenarios.

摘要（中文）: 实时屋顶风速分布对于无人机和城市空中交通系统的安全运行、风力控制系统以及屋顶利用至关重要。然而，屋顶气流表现出强烈的非线性、分离和交叉方向变异性，这使得从稀疏传感器数据重建流场变得困难。本研究开发了一种基于观测学习的框架，利用粒子图像测速（PIV）获得的风洞实验数据，并将克里金插值与三种深度学习模型进行比较：UNet、视觉Transformer自编码器(ViTAE)和条件Wasserstein生成对抗网络(CWGAN)。我们评估了两种训练策略：单一风向训练（SDT）和混合风向训练（MDT），涵盖5到30的传感器密度，测试了传感器位置正负1个网格扰动下的鲁棒性，并通过基于QR分解的本征正交分解优化了传感器布局。结果表明，深度学习方法能够有效地从稀疏传感器数据中重建屋顶风场。与克里金插值相比，深度学习模型在结构相似性指数（SSIM）上提高了高达32.7%，在二倍因子（FAC2）上提高了24.2%，并在均方误差归一化(NMSE)上提高了27.8%。混合风向训练进一步提升了性能，与单风向训练相比，在SSIM上增益高达173.7%，在FAC2上增益16.7%，在几何平均数(MG)上增益98.3%。结果还表明，传感器配置、优化和训练策略应联合考虑，以实现可靠的部署。基于QR的优化将传感器扰动下的鲁棒性提高了高达27.8%，但存在指标相关的权衡。基于实验数据而非模拟数据进行训练，也为不同场景下的方法选择和传感器放置提供了实践指导。

TLDR: This paper explores using deep learning models (UNet, ViTAE, CWGAN) with sparse sensor data to reconstruct rooftop wind fields, demonstrating improved performance compared to Kriging interpolation and highlighting the importance of sensor placement optimization and training strategies.

简要说明: 本文探讨了使用深度学习模型（UNet, ViTAE, CWGAN）和稀疏传感器数据来重建屋顶风场， 结果表明与Kriging插值相比， 这些模型表现出更好的性能， 并强调了传感器放置优化和训练策略的重要性。

Authors: Yihang Zhou, Chao Lin, Hideki Kikumoto, Ryozo Ooka, Sibo Cheng

Wear Classification of Abrasive Flap Wheels using a Hierarchical Deep Learning Approach

Abstract (English): Abrasive flap wheels are common for finishing complex free-form surfaces due to their flexibility. However, this flexibility results in complex wear patterns such as concave/convex flap profiles or flap tears, which influence the grinding result. This paper proposes a novel, vision-based hierarchical classification framework to automate the wear condition monitoring of flap wheels. Unlike monolithic classification approaches, we decompose the problem into three logical levels: (1) state detection (new vs. worn), (2) wear type identification (rectangular, concave, convex) and flap tear detection, and (3) severity assessment (partial vs. complete deformation). A custom-built dataset of real flap wheel images was generated and a transfer learning approach with EfficientNetV2 architecture was used. The results demonstrate high robustness with classification accuracies ranging from 93.8% (flap tears) to 99.3% (concave severity). Furthermore, Gradient-weighted Class Activation Mapping (Grad-CAM) is utilized to validate that the models learn physically relevant features and examine false classifications. The proposed hierarchical method provides a basis for adaptive process control and wear consideration in automated flap wheel grinding.

摘要（中文）: 磨料性叶轮由于其灵活性，常用于精加工复杂的自由曲面。然而，这种灵活性会导致复杂的磨损模式，例如凹/凸叶片轮廓或叶片撕裂，从而影响研磨结果。本文提出了一种新颖的、基于视觉的分层分类框架，以实现叶轮磨损状况的自动化监测。与整体式分类方法不同，我们将问题分解为三个逻辑层级：（1）状态检测（新的 vs. 已磨损），（2）磨损类型识别（矩形、凹形、凸形）和叶片撕裂检测，以及（3）严重程度评估（部分 vs. 完全变形）。我们构建了一个自定义的真实叶轮图像数据集，并采用了基于 EfficientNetV2 架构的迁移学习方法。结果表明，该方法具有很高的鲁棒性，分类精度范围从 93.8%（叶片撕裂）到 99.3%（凹形严重程度）。此外，利用梯度加权类激活映射 (Grad-CAM) 来验证模型是否学习到物理相关的特征，并检查错误分类的情况。所提出的分层方法为自适应过程控制和自动化叶轮研磨中的磨损考虑因素提供了基础。

TLDR: This paper presents a hierarchical deep learning framework for classifying the wear condition of abrasive flap wheels based on visual inspection, achieving high accuracy in identifying wear state, type, tear detection, and severity.

Authors: Falko Kähler, Maxim Wille, Ole Schmedemann, Thorsten Schüppstuhl

Federated Few-Shot Learning on Neuromorphic Hardware: An Empirical Study Across Physical Edge Nodes

Abstract (English): Federated learning on neuromorphic hardware remains unexplored because on-chip spike-timing-dependent plasticity (STDP) produces binary weight updates rather than the floating-point gradients assumed by standard algorithms. We build a two-node federated system with BrainChip Akida AKD1000 processors and run approximately 1,580 experimental trials across seven analysis phases. Of four weight-exchange strategies tested, neuron-level concatenation (FedUnion) consistently preserves accuracy while element-wise weight averaging (FedAvg) destroys it (p = 0.002). Domain-adaptive fine-tuning of the upstream feature extractor accounts for most of the accuracy gains, confirming feature quality as the dominant factor. Scaling feature dimensionality from 64 to 256 yields 77.0% best-strategy federated accuracy (n=30, p < 0.001). Two independent asymmetries (wider features help federation more than individual learning, while binarization hurts federation more) point to a shared prototype complementarity mechanism: cross-node transfer scales with the distinctiveness of neuron prototypes.

摘要（中文）: 神经形态硬件上的联邦学习仍未被探索，因为片上尖峰时序依赖可塑性 (STDP) 产生的是二值权重更新，而非标准算法假设的浮点梯度。我们构建了一个具有 BrainChip Akida AKD1000 处理器的双节点联邦系统，并在七个分析阶段运行了大约 1,580 次实验试验。在测试的四种权重交换策略中，神经元级别联结 (FedUnion) 能够始终保持准确性，而逐元素权重平均 (FedAvg) 则会破坏准确性 (p = 0.002)。上游特征提取器的领域自适应微调是大部分准确度提升的原因，证实了特征质量是主导因素。将特征维度从 64 扩展到 256 可以产生 77.0% 的最佳策略联邦准确率 (n=30, p < 0.001)。 两个独立的非对称性（更宽的特征比个体学习更有助于联邦，而二值化对联邦的损害更大）指向一种共享的原型互补机制：跨节点传输随神经元原型区分度的增加而扩展。

TLDR: This paper explores federated few-shot learning on neuromorphic hardware using BrainChip Akida processors, finding that neuron-level concatenation weight exchange and domain-adaptive fine-tuning significantly impact accuracy. The study reveals prototype complementarity as a key factor for cross-node transfer scaling.

简要说明: 本文探讨了使用BrainChip Akida处理器在神经形态硬件上的联邦小样本学习，发现神经元级联接权重交换和领域自适应微调对准确性有显著影响。 研究表明原型互补是跨节点传输缩放的关键因素。

Authors: Steven Motta, Gioele Nanni

From AI Weather Prediction to Infrastructure Resilience: A Correction-Downscaling Framework for Tropical Cyclone Impacts

Abstract (English): This paper addresses a missing capability in infrastructure resilience: turning fast, global AI weather forecasts into asset-scale, actionable risk. We introduce the AI-based Correction-Downscaling Framework (ACDF), which transforms coarse AI weather prediction (AIWP) into 500-m, unbiased wind fields and transmission tower/line failure probabilities for tropical cyclones. ACDF separates storm-scale bias correction from terrain-aware downscaling, preventing error propagation while restoring sub-kilometer variability that governs structural loading. Tested on 11 typhoons affecting Zhejiang, China under leave-one-storm-out evaluation, ACDF reduces station-scale wind-speed MAE by 38.8% versus Pangu-Weather, matches observation-assimilated mesoscale analyses, yet runs in 25 s per 12-h cycle on a single GPU. In the Typhoon Hagupit case, ACDF reproduced observed high-wind tails, isolated a coastal high-risk corridor, and flagged the line that failed, demonstrating actionable guidance at tower and line scales. ACDF provides an end-to-end pathway from AI global forecasts to operational, impact-based early warning for critical infrastructure.

摘要（中文）: 本文旨在解决基础设施韧性方面的一个缺失能力：将快速、全局的AI天气预报转化为资产层面的、可执行的风险预警。我们提出了基于AI的校正-降尺度框架（ACDF），能够将粗糙的AI天气预测（AIWP）转化为500米分辨率的、无偏的风场以及热带气旋期间输电塔/线故障概率。ACDF将风暴尺度的偏差校正与考虑地形的降尺度分离，防止误差传播，同时恢复控制结构荷载的亚千米级变异性。经过对影响中国浙江的11个台风进行的留一风暴法评估测试，与盘古气象相比，ACDF将站点尺度的风速平均绝对误差（MAE）降低了38.8%，与经过观测同化的中尺度分析结果相匹配，且在单个GPU上运行每个12小时周期仅需25秒。在海高斯台风案例中，ACDF重现了观测到的高风速尾部，识别出沿海高风险走廊，并标记出发生故障的线路，展示了塔和线路尺度的可执行指导。ACDF提供了一条从AI全局预报到关键基础设施的、基于影响的运营级早期预警的端到端路径。

TLDR: The paper introduces an AI-based correction-downscaling framework (ACDF) that refines global AI weather predictions into asset-scale, actionable risk assessments for infrastructure resilience against tropical cyclones, demonstrating significant improvements in wind field accuracy and failure prediction.
